#### Abstracts
##### **Tokenisation via Convex Relaxations**
2605.22821v1 by Jan Tempus, Philip Whittington, Craig W. Schmidt, Dennis Komm, Tiago Pimentel

Tokenisation is an integral part of the current NLP pipeline. Current tokenisation algorithms such as BPE and Unigram are greedy algorithms -- they make locally optimal decisions without considering the resulting vocabulary as a whole. We instead formulate tokeniser construction as a linear program and solve it using convex optimisation tools, yielding a new algorithm we call ConvexTok. We find ConvexTok consistently improves intrinsic tokenisation metrics and the bits-per-byte (BpB) achieved by language models; it also improves downstream task performance, but less consistently. Furthermore, ConvexTok allows the user to certify how far their tokeniser is from optimal, with respect to a certain objective, via a lower bound, and we empirically find it to be within 1\% of optimal at common vocabulary sizes.

摘要：標記化是當前自然語言處理流程中的一個重要組成部分。當前的標記化算法，如BPE和Unigram，都是貪婪算法——它們在不考慮整體詞彙的情況下做出局部最優決策。我們則將標記器的構建形式化為一個線性規劃，並使用凸優化工具來解決，從而產生了一種我們稱之為ConvexTok的新算法。我們發現，ConvexTok能夠持續改善內在的標記化指標以及語言模型所達到的每字節位數（BpB）；它也改善了下游任務的表現，但不如前者一致。此外，ConvexTok允許用戶通過下界來認證其標記器相對於某一特定目標的最優程度，我們實證發現，在常見的詞彙大小下，這一距離在1\%以內。

##### **Vector Policy Optimization: Training for Diversity Improves Test-Time Search**
2605.22817v1 by Ryan Bahlous-Boldi, Isha Puri, Idan Shenfeld, Akarsh Kumar, Mehul Damani, Sebastian Risi, Omar Khattab, Zhang-Wei Hong, Pulkit Agrawal

Language models must now generalize out of the box to novel environments and work inside inference-scaling search procedures, such as AlphaEvolve, that select rollouts with a variety of task-specific reward functions. Unfortunately, the standard paradigm of LLM post-training optimizes a pre-specified scalar reward, often leading current LLMs to produce low-entropy response distributions and thus to struggle at displaying the diversity that inference-time search will require. We propose Vector Policy Optimization (VPO), an RL algorithm that explicitly trains policies to anticipate diverse downstream reward functions and to produce diverse solutions. VPO exploits that rewards are often vector-valued in practice, like per-test-case correctness in code generation or, say, multiple different user personas or reward models. VPO is essentially a drop-in replacement for the GRPO advantage estimator, but it trains the LLM to output a set of solutions where individual solutions specialize to different trade-offs in the vector reward space. Across four tasks, VPO matches or beats the strongest scalar RL baselines on test-time search (e.g. pass@k and best@k), with the gap widening as the search budget grows. For evolutionary search, VPO models unlock problems that GRPO models cannot solve at all. As test-time search becomes more standardized, optimizing for diversity may need to become the default post-training objective.

摘要：語言模型現在必須在新的環境中進行即時泛化，並在推理擴展搜索程序中運作，例如 AlphaEvolve，該程序根據各種特定任務的獎勵函數選擇展開。不幸的是，標準的 LLM 後訓練範式優化一個預先指定的標量獎勵，這常常導致當前的 LLM 產生低熵的回應分佈，因此在展示推理時間搜索所需的多樣性方面表現不佳。我們提出了向量策略優化（VPO），這是一種強化學習算法，明確訓練策略以預測多樣的下游獎勵函數並產生多樣的解決方案。VPO 利用獎勵在實踐中通常是向量值的事實，例如在代碼生成中的每個測試案例的正確性，或者說多個不同的用戶角色或獎勵模型。VPO 本質上是 GRPO 優勢估計器的替代品，但它訓練 LLM 輸出一組解決方案，其中每個解決方案專注於向量獎勵空間中的不同權衡。在四個任務中，VPO 在測試時間搜索（例如 pass@k 和 best@k）中與最強的標量 RL 基準相匹配或超越，隨著搜索預算的增加，差距不斷擴大。對於進化搜索，VPO 模型解鎖了 GRPO 模型無法解決的問題。隨著測試時間搜索變得越來越標準化，優化多樣性可能需要成為默認的後訓練目標。

##### **The Matching Principle: A Geometric Theory of Loss Functions for Nuisance-Robust Representation Learning**
2605.22800v1 by Vishal Rajput

Robustness, domain adaptation, photometric and occlusion invariance, compositional generalisation, temporal robustness, alignment safety, and classical anisotropic regularisation are usually treated as separate problems with separate method families. This paper argues that much of their shared structure is one statistical problem: estimate the covariance of label-preserving deployment nuisance, then regularise the encoder Jacobian along a matrix whose range covers that covariance (the matching principle). CORAL, adversarial training, IRM, augmentation, metric learning, Jacobian penalties, and alignment-style constraints are different estimators of that object, not independent robustness tricks.
  In the linear-Gaussian model we prove closed-form optimality (Theorem A), including cube-root water-filling within the matched range; necessity of range coverage for quadratic Jacobian penalties (Theorem G); the same range dichotomy at deep global minima; and two falsification controls (Lemma C; Corollaries E), with seven conditional consistency lemmas (D1-D7) for estimation under standard identifiability assumptions.
  We introduce the Trajectory Deviation Index (TDI), a label-free probe of embedding sensitivity when task accuracy or Jacobian Frobenius norm is insufficient.
  Thirteen pre-registered blocks from classical ML through Qwen2.5-7B test the predicted matched, then isotropic, then wrong-W ordering on geometry and deployment drift; twelve pass, and the sole exception (Office-31) is an eigengap failure named before the run. At 7B scale, matched style-PMH improves selective honesty and preserves Style TDI where standard DPO degrades it.
  The contribution is naming the deployment nuisance covariance, stating what the regulariser must do, and supplying a closed-form falsifiable theory once that object is identified, not universality on every leaderboard.

摘要：穩健性、領域適應、光度和遮擋不變性、組合泛化、時間穩健性、對齊安全性以及經典各向異性正則化通常被視為獨立的問題，並擁有各自的方法家族。本文主張，它們之間的許多共同結構實際上是一個統計問題：估計標籤保留部署的干擾協方差，然後沿著一個涵蓋該協方差的矩陣對編碼器雅可比進行正則化（匹配原則）。CORAL、對抗訓練、IRM、增強、度量學習、雅可比懲罰和對齊風格約束是該對象的不同估計器，而不是獨立的穩健性技巧。<lb/>在線性高斯模型中，我們證明了封閉形式的最優性（定理A），包括在匹配範圍內的立方根水填充；二次雅可比懲罰的範圍覆蓋必要性（定理G）；在深層全局最小值處的相同範圍二分法；以及兩個偽證控制（引理C；推論E），並提供七個條件一致性引理（D1-D7），以便在標準可識別性假設下進行估計。<lb/>我們引入了軌跡偏差指數（TDI），這是一種無標籤的嵌入敏感性探測工具，當任務準確性或雅可比弗羅貝尼烏斯範數不足時使用。<lb/>來自經典機器學習到Qwen2.5-7B的十三個預註冊區塊測試了預測的匹配，然後是各向同性，然後是錯誤的W排序在幾何和部署漂移上；十二個通過，唯一的例外（Office-31）是一個在運行之前命名的特徵間隙失敗。在7B規模下，匹配的風格-PMH改善了選擇性誠實性，並在標準DPO退化的地方保留了風格TDI。<lb/>貢獻在於命名部署干擾協方差，說明正則化器必須做什麼，並在識別該對象後提供一個封閉形式的可偽證理論，而不是在每個排行榜上的普遍性。

##### **Finite-Particle Convergence Rates for Conservative and Non-Conservative Drifting Models**
2605.22795v1 by Krishnakumar Balasubramanian

We propose and analyze a conservative drifting method for one-step generative modeling. The method replaces the original displacement-based drifting velocity by a kernel density estimator (KDE)-gradient velocity, namely the difference of the kernel-smoothed data score and the kernel-smoothed model score. This velocity is a gradient field, addressing the non-conservatism issue identified for general displacement-based drifting fields. We prove continuous-time finite-particle convergence bounds for the conservative method on $\R^d$: a joint-entropy identity yields bounds for the empirical Stein drift, the smoothed Fisher discrepancy of the KDE, and the squared center velocity. The main finite-particle correction is a reciprocal-KDE self-interaction term, and we give deterministic and high-probability local-occupancy conditions under which this term is controlled. We keep the quadrature constants explicit and track their possible bandwidth dependence: the root residual-velocity rate $N^{-1/(d+4)}$ holds under an additional $h$-uniform quadrature regularity condition, while a more general growth condition yields the optimized root rate $N^{-(2-β)/(2(d+4-β))}$, where $0\le β<2$. We also analyze the non-conservative drifting method with Laplace kernel, corresponding to the original displacement-based velocity proposed in~\cite{deng2026drifting}. For this method, a sharp companion kernel decomposes the velocity into a positive scalar preconditioning of a sharp-score mismatch plus a Laplace scale-mismatch residual, producing an analogous finite-particle rate with an unavoidable residual term. Finally, we explain how the continuous-time residual-velocity bounds translate into one-step generation guarantees through the explicit drift size $η$.

摘要：我們提出並分析了一種保守漂移方法，用於一步生成建模。該方法用核密度估計器（KDE）梯度速度取代了原始的基於位移的漂移速度，即核平滑數據得分與核平滑模型得分之間的差異。這種速度是一個梯度場，解決了針對一般基於位移的漂移場所識別的非保守性問題。我們證明了保守方法在 $\R^d$ 上的連續時間有限粒子收斂界限：一個聯合熵恆等式產生了對經驗Stein漂移、KDE的平滑Fisher差異和平方中心速度的界限。主要的有限粒子修正是一個互惠-KDE自互動項，我們給出了確定性和高概率的局部佔用條件，在這些條件下，這個項是可控的。我們保持積分常數的明確性，並追蹤它們可能的帶寬依賴性：根殘餘速度率 $N^{-1/(d+4)}$ 在額外的 $h$-均勻積分正則性條件下成立，而一個更一般的增長條件產生了優化的根速率 $N^{-(2-β)/(2(d+4-β))}$，其中 $0\le β<2$。我們還分析了使用拉普拉斯核的非保守漂移方法，對應於~\cite{deng2026drifting} 中提出的原始基於位移的速度。對於這種方法，一個尖銳的伴隨核將速度分解為尖銳得分不匹配的正標量預處理加上拉普拉斯尺度不匹配的殘餘，產生類似的有限粒子速率，並伴隨著不可避免的殘餘項。最後，我們解釋了如何將連續時間的殘餘速度界限轉化為一步生成保證，通過明確的漂移大小 $η$。

##### **MOSS: Self-Evolution through Source-Level Rewriting in Autonomous Agent Systems**
2605.22794v1 by Qianshu Cai, Yonggang Zhang, Xianzhang Jia, Wei Xue, Jun Song, Xinmei Tian, Yike Guo

Autonomous agentic systems are largely static after deployment: they do not learn from user interactions, and recurring failures persist until the next human-driven update ships a fix. Self-evolving agents have emerged in response, but all confine evolution to text-mutable artifacts -- skill files, prompt configurations, memory schemas, workflow graphs -- and leave the agent harness untouched. Since routing, hook ordering, state invariants, and dispatch live in code rather than in any text artifact, an entire class of structural failure is physically unreachable from the text layer. We argue that source-level adaptation is a fundamentally more general medium: it is Turing-complete, a strict superset of every text-mutable scope, takes effect deterministically rather than through base-model compliance, and does not erode under long-context drift. We present MOSS, a system that performs self-rewriting at the source level on production agentic substrates. Each evolution is anchored to an automatically curated batch of production-failure evidence and proceeds through a deterministic multi-stage pipeline; code modification is delegated to a pluggable external coding-agent CLI while MOSS retains stage ordering and verdicts. Candidates are verified by replaying the batch against the candidate image in ephemeral trial workers, then promoted via user-consent-gated, in-place container swap with health-probe-gated rollback. On OpenClaw, MOSS lifts a four-task mean grader score from 0.25 to 0.61 in a single cycle without human intervention.

摘要：自主代理系統在部署後基本上是靜態的：它們不會從用戶互動中學習，且重複的失敗會持續存在，直到下一次人為驅動的更新發佈修復。自我進化的代理隨之出現，但所有的進化都限於文本可變的工件——技能檔案、提示配置、記憶架構、工作流程圖——並且不觸及代理的框架。由於路由、掛鉤順序、狀態不變量和調度都存在於代碼中，而不是任何文本工件中，整個結構性失敗類別在文本層面上是物理上無法到達的。我們主張源級適應是一種根本上更通用的媒介：它是圖靈完備的，是每個文本可變範疇的嚴格超集，具有確定性效果，而不是通過基礎模型的合規性來實現，並且在長期上下文漂移下不會退化。我們提出了MOSS，一個在生產代理基底上進行源級自我重寫的系統。每次進化都依賴於自動策劃的生產失敗證據批次，並通過確定性的多階段管道進行；代碼修改委託給可插拔的外部編碼代理CLI，而MOSS保留階段順序和裁決。候選者通過在短暫的試驗工作者中重放批次以驗證候選映像，然後通過用戶同意的就地容器交換進行提升，並進行健康探測的回滾。在OpenClaw上，MOSS在單個周期內將四任務平均評分從0.25提升到0.61，無需人為干預。

##### **Gated DeltaNet-2: Decoupling Erase and Write in Linear Attention**
2605.22791v1 by Ali Hatamizadeh, Yejin Choi, Jan Kautz

Linear attention replaces the unbounded cache of softmax attention with a fixed-size recurrent state, reducing sequence mixing to linear time and decoding to constant memory. The hard part is not just what to forget, but how to edit this compressed memory without scrambling existing associations. Delta-rule models subtract the current read before writing a new value, and Kimi Delta Attention (KDA) sharpens forgetting with channel-wise decay. But the active edit still uses a single scalar gate to control two different things: how much old content to erase on the key side and how much new content to commit on the value side. We introduce Gated DeltaNet-2, which generalizes both Gated DeltaNet and KDA by inheriting adaptive forgetting and channel-wise decay while addressing their shared limitation, the scalar tie between erasing and writing. Gated Delta Rule-2 separates these roles with a channel-wise erase gate b_t and a channel-wise write gate w_t, reducing to KDA when both gates collapse to the same scalar and to Gated DeltaNet when the decay also collapses. We derive a fast-weight update view, a chunkwise WY algorithm with channel-wise decay absorbed into asymmetric erase factors, and a gate-aware backward pass that preserves efficient parallel training. At 1.3B parameters trained on 100B FineWeb-Edu tokens, Gated DeltaNet-2 achieves the strongest overall results among Mamba-2, Gated DeltaNet, KDA, and Mamba-3 variants across language modeling, commonsense reasoning, and retrieval. Its advantage is most pronounced on long-context RULER needle-in-a-haystack benchmarks, where it improves the evaluated multi-key retrieval setting and remains strong in both recurrent and hybrid settings. Code is available at https://github.com/NVlabs/GatedDeltaNet-2.

摘要：線性注意力用固定大小的遞迴狀態取代了軟最大注意力的無界快取，將序列混合降低至線性時間，解碼則減少至常數記憶體。困難的部分不僅在於忘記什麼，還在於如何編輯這個壓縮的記憶體而不打亂現有的聯繫。德爾塔規則模型在寫入新值之前會減去當前的讀取，而 Kimi Delta Attention (KDA) 則通過通道衰減來加強遺忘。但主動編輯仍然使用單一的標量閘來控制兩個不同的事物：在鍵側要抹去多少舊內容，以及在值側要提交多少新內容。我們引入了 Gated DeltaNet-2，它通過繼承自適應遺忘和通道衰減來概括 Gated DeltaNet 和 KDA，同時解決它們的共同限制，即抹去和寫入之間的標量綁定。Gated Delta Rule-2 用通道級抹除閘 b_t 和通道級寫入閘 w_t 分開這些角色，當兩個閘都收斂為相同的標量時，減少為 KDA，而當衰減也收斂時則減少為 Gated DeltaNet。我們推導出一個快速權重更新視圖，一個將通道衰減吸收到非對稱抹除因子的塊狀 WY 算法，以及一個保留高效並行訓練的閘感知反向傳播。在 1.3B 參數上，訓練於 100B FineWeb-Edu 令牌，Gated DeltaNet-2 在 Mamba-2、Gated DeltaNet、KDA 和 Mamba-3 變體中，在語言建模、常識推理和檢索方面取得了最強的整體結果。它的優勢在長上下文 RULER 大海撈針基準上最為明顯，在這裡它改善了評估的多鍵檢索設置，並在遞迴和混合設置中保持強勁。代碼可在 https://github.com/NVlabs/GatedDeltaNet-2 獲得。

##### **LCGuard: Latent Communication Guard for Safe KV Sharing in Multi-Agent Systems**
2605.22786v1 by Sadia Asif, Mohammad Mohammadi Amiri, Momin Abbas, Prasanna Sattigeri, Karthikeyan Natesan Ramamurthy

Large language model (LLM)-based multi-agent systems increasingly rely on intermediate communication to coordinate complex tasks. While most existing systems communicate through natural language, recent work shows that latent communication, particularly through transformer key-value (KV) caches, can improve efficiency and preserve richer task-relevant information. However, KV caches also encode contextual inputs, intermediate reasoning states, and agent-specific information, creating an opaque channel through which sensitive content may propagate across agents without explicit textual disclosure. To address this, we introduce \textbf{LCGuard} (Latent Communication Guard), a framework for safe KV-based latent communication in multi-agent LLM systems. LCGuard treats shared KV caches as latent working memory and learns representation-level transformations before cache artifacts are transmitted across agents. We formalize representation-level sensitive information leakage operationally through reconstruction: a shared cache artifact is unsafe if an adversarial decoder can recover agent-specific sensitive inputs from it. This leads to an adversarial training formulation in which the adversary learns to reconstruct sensitive inputs, while LCGuard learns transformations that preserve task-relevant semantics and reduce reconstructable information. Empirical evaluations across multiple model families and multi-agent benchmarks show that LCGuard consistently reduces reconstruction-based leakage and attack success rates while maintaining competitive task performance compared to standard KV-sharing baselines.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLM）基礎的多代理系統越來越依賴中介通信來協調複雜任務。<lb/>雖然大多數現有系統通過自然語言進行通信，但最近的研究顯示，潛在通信，特別是通過Transformer鍵值（KV）快取，可以提高效率並保留更豐富的任務相關信息。<lb/>然而，KV快取還編碼了上下文輸入、中介推理狀態和代理特定信息，創造了一個不透明的通道，通過該通道，敏感內容可能在代理之間傳播而無需明確的文本披露。<lb/>為了解決這個問題，我們介紹了\textbf{LCGuard}（潛在通信保護），這是一個在多代理LLM系統中進行安全KV基礎潛在通信的框架。<lb/>LCGuard將共享的KV快取視為潛在工作記憶，並在快取工件被傳輸到代理之間之前學習表示層級的轉換。<lb/>我們通過重建形式化表示層級的敏感信息洩漏：如果對手解碼器能夠從共享的快取工件中恢復代理特定的敏感輸入，則該共享快取工件是不安全的。<lb/>這導致了一種對抗訓練的公式，其中對手學習重建敏感輸入，而LCGuard學習保留任務相關語義並減少可重建信息的轉換。<lb/>在多個模型系列和多代理基準上的實證評估顯示，LCGuard始終減少基於重建的洩漏和攻擊成功率，同時與標準KV共享基準相比，保持競爭性的任務性能。

##### **Evaluating Commercial AI Chatbots as News Intermediaries**
2605.22785v1 by Mirac Suzgun, Emily Shen, Federico Bianchi, Alexander Spangher, Thomas Icard, Daniel E. Ho, Dan Jurafsky, James Zou

AI chatbots are rapidly shaping how people encounter the news, yet no prior study has systematically measured how accurately these systems, with their proprietary search integrations and retrieval-synthesis pipelines, handle emerging facts across languages and regions. We present a 14-day (February 9-22, 2026) evaluation of six AI chatbots (Gemini 3 Flash and Pro, Grok 4, Claude 4.5 Sonnet, GPT-5 and GPT-4o mini) on 2,100 factual questions derived from same-day BBC News reporting across six regional services (US & Canada, Arabic, Afrique, Hindi, Russian, Turkish). The best systems achieve over 90% multiple-choice accuracy on questions about events reported hours earlier. The same systems, however, lose 11-13% under free-response evaluation, and 16-17% across the cohort. We further characterize three failure patterns. First, every model achieves its lowest accuracy on Hindi (79% vs. 89-91% elsewhere) and citations indicate an Anglophone retrieval bias (e.g., models answering Hindi queries cite English Wikipedia more than any Hindi outlet). Second, retrieval, not reasoning, failures drive over 70% of all errors. When models retrieve a correct source, they often extract the correct answer; the problem is to land on the right source in the first place. Third, models achieving 88-96% accuracy on well-formed questions drop to 19-70% when questions contain subtle false premises, with the most vulnerable model accepting fabricated facts 64% of the time. We also identify a detection-accuracy paradox: the best false-premise detector ranks second in adversarial accuracy (abstention rate), while a weaker detector ranks first, showing that premise detection and answer recovery are partially independent capabilities. Overall, these suggest that high accuracy can mask systematic regional inequity, near-total dependence on retrieval infrastructure, and vulnerability to imperfect queries real users pose.

摘要：AI 聊天機器人正在迅速改變人們接觸新聞的方式，但之前沒有研究系統性地測量這些系統（擁有其專有的搜索整合和檢索-合成管道）在不同語言和地區處理新興事實的準確性。我們對六個 AI 聊天機器人（Gemini 3 Flash 和 Pro、Grok 4、Claude 4.5 Sonnet、GPT-5 和 GPT-4o mini）進行了為期 14 天（2026 年 2 月 9 日至 22 日）的評估，這些問題來自於六個地區服務（美國和加拿大、阿拉伯語、非洲語、印地語、俄語、土耳其語）當天的 BBC News 報導，共 2,100 個事實問題。最好的系統在關於幾小時前報導的事件的多選題上達到超過 90% 的準確率。然而，這些系統在自由回答評估中失去 11-13% 的準確率，而在整體評估中則下降 16-17%。我們進一步描述了三種失敗模式。首先，每個模型在印地語上的準確率最低（79% 對比其他語言的 89-91%），引用顯示出英語檢索的偏見（例如，模型回答印地語查詢時引用英語維基百科的次數多於任何印地語媒體）。第二，檢索失敗而非推理失敗驅動了超過 70% 的所有錯誤。當模型檢索到正確來源時，它們通常能提取出正確的答案；問題在於首先能否找到正確的來源。第三，對於結構良好的問題，模型的準確率達到 88-96%，但當問題包含微妙的錯誤前提時，準確率下降至 19-70%，其中最脆弱的模型在 64% 的情況下接受虛構事實。我們還識別出一個檢測準確性悖論：最佳的錯誤前提檢測器在對抗準確性（棄權率）中排名第二，而一個較弱的檢測器排名第一，顯示出前提檢測和答案恢復是部分獨立的能力。總體而言，這些結果表明，高準確性可能掩蓋系統性的地區不平等、對檢索基礎設施的幾乎完全依賴，以及對真實用戶提出的不完美查詢的脆弱性。

##### **DeltaBox: Scaling Stateful AI Agents with Millisecond-Level Sandbox Checkpoint/Rollback**
2605.22781v1 by Yunpeng Dong, Jingkai He, Yuze Hou, Dong Du, Zhonghu Xu, Si Yu, Yubin Xia, Haibo Chen

LLM-powered AI agents require high-frequency state exploration (e.g., test-time tree search and reinforcement learning), relying on rapid checkpoint and rollback (C/R) of the complete sandbox state, including files and process state (e.g., memory, contexts, etc.). Existing mechanisms duplicate the entire state, causing hundreds of milliseconds to seconds of latency per C/R, which severely bottlenecks deep search and large-scale fan-outs.
  This paper observes that subsequent checkpoints in AI agents are highly similar. Therefore, instead of full duplication, a sandbox should only duplicate the changes between consecutive checkpoints (Key Insight). However, it is non-trivial to realize the idea, mainly due to the missing OS supports. This paper proposes a new OS-level abstraction, DeltaState, to enable the change-based transactional C/R for AI agents with two co-designed OS mechanisms. First, DeltaFS enables change-based filesystem C/R by organizing the file states into layers and dynamically freezing the writable layer and inserting a new one during checkpoint, reducing file updates to copy-on-write, and making rollback a simple layer switch. Second, DeltaCR enables change-based process state C/R using incremental dumps, and accelerates rollback by bypassing traditional pipelines to directly fork() from a frozen template process. We then present DeltaBox, a novel agent sandbox achieving millisecond level C/R through the two new mechanisms. Evaluations on SWE-bench and RL micro-benchmarks show DeltaBox completes checkpoint and rollback in millisecond-level latency (14ms and 5ms, respectively), empowering agents to explore substantially more nodes under fixed time budgets.

摘要：LLM 驅動的 AI 代理需要高頻率的狀態探索（例如，測試時的樹搜尋和強化學習），依賴於快速的檢查點和回滾（C/R）整個沙盒狀態，包括文件和進程狀態（例如，記憶體、上下文等）。現有機制會重複整個狀態，導致每次 C/R 的延遲達到數百毫秒到幾秒，這嚴重限制了深度搜尋和大規模的分支展開。<lb/>本文觀察到 AI 代理中的後續檢查點高度相似。因此，沙盒應該僅重複連續檢查點之間的變更，而不是完全重複（關鍵見解）。然而，實現這一想法並不簡單，主要是因為缺乏操作系統的支持。<lb/>本文提出了一種新的操作系統級抽象，DeltaState，以實現基於變更的事務性 C/R，並配合兩個共同設計的操作系統機制。首先，DeltaFS 通過將文件狀態組織成層，並在檢查點期間動態凍結可寫層並插入新層，來實現基於變更的文件系統 C/R，將文件更新減少為寫時複製，並使回滾變為簡單的層切換。<lb/>其次，DeltaCR 使用增量轉儲實現基於變更的進程狀態 C/R，並通過繞過傳統管道直接從凍結的模板進程中 fork() 來加速回滾。接著，我們介紹了 DeltaBox，一個新穎的代理沙盒，通過這兩個新機制實現毫秒級的 C/R。<lb/>在 SWE-bench 和 RL 微基準上的評估顯示，DeltaBox 在毫秒級延遲下完成檢查點和回滾（分別為 14 毫秒和 5 毫秒），使代理能夠在固定的時間預算下探索更多的節點。

##### **SDPM: Survival Diffusion Probabilistic Model for Continuous-Time Survival Analysis**
2605.22776v1 by Stanislav R. Kirpichenko, Andrei V. Konstantinov, Lev V. Utkin

Survival analysis aims to estimate a time-to-event distribution from data with censored observations. Many existing methods either impose structural assumptions on the hazard function or discretize the time axis, which may limit flexibility and introduce approximation errors. We propose the Survival Diffusion Probabilistic Model (SDPM), a generative approach to continuous-time survival analysis. SDPM models the conditional distribution of the survival outcome, represented by the pair of observed time and censoring indicator, $\mathbb{P}(T,δ\mid \mathbf{x})$, using a denoising diffusion model. Under the assumption of conditionally independent censoring, conditional samples generated by the model can be transformed into survival function estimates using the Kaplan-Meier estimator. This formulation avoids parametric assumptions on the event-time distribution and does not require a discretization of the output time space. The model operates in a transformed target space, using standardized log-times and a continuous Gaussian-mixture representation of the censoring indicator. We evaluate SDPM on ten real survival datasets and compare it with five strong baselines, including tree-based, boosting-based, and neural survival models. Results show that SDPM achieves competitive predictive performance across C-index, integrated time-dependent AUC, and integrated Brier score. A study on synthetic Cox-Weibull data demonstrates that SDPM can recover the shape of an underlying continuous survival distribution more accurately than a strong nonparametric baseline when sufficiently many samples are generated. An ablation study confirms the importance of the proposed target-space transformations, which improve event-rate calibration, reduce invalid generated times, and provide consistent gains in predictive discrimination. Codes implementing the proposed model are publicly available.

摘要：生存分析旨在從具有截尾觀測值的數據中估計事件發生的時間分佈。許多現有的方法要麼對危險函數施加結構性假設，要麼對時間軸進行離散化，這可能限制靈活性並引入近似誤差。我們提出了生存擴散概率模型（SDPM），這是一種連續時間生存分析的生成方法。SDPM 模型化生存結果的條件分佈，由觀察到的時間和截尾指標的對組成，$\mathbb{P}(T,δ\mid \mathbf{x})$，使用去噪擴散模型。在條件獨立截尾的假設下，模型生成的條件樣本可以使用 Kaplan-Meier 估計器轉換為生存函數估計。這種公式避免了對事件時間分佈的參數假設，並且不需要對輸出時間空間進行離散化。該模型在轉換的目標空間中運行，使用標準化的對數時間和截尾指標的連續高斯混合表示。我們在十個真實生存數據集上評估了 SDPM，並將其與五個強基準進行比較，包括基於樹的、基於提升的和神經生存模型。結果顯示，SDPM 在 C 指數、綜合時間依賴 AUC 和綜合 Brier 分數方面達到了具有競爭力的預測性能。對合成 Cox-Weibull 數據的研究表明，當生成的樣本數量足夠時，SDPM 能夠比強大的非參數基準更準確地恢復潛在連續生存分佈的形狀。一項消融研究確認了所提出的目標空間轉換的重要性，這些轉換改善了事件率的校準，減少了無效生成的時間，並在預測區分上提供了一致的增益。實現所提出模型的代碼已公開可用。

##### **MambaGaze: Bidirectional Mamba with Explicit Missing Data Modeling for Cognitive Load Assessment from Eye-Gaze Tracking Data**
2605.22775v1 by Amir Mousavi, Mohammad Sadegh Sirjani, Erfan Nourbakhsh, Mimi Xie, Rocky Slavin, Leslie Neely, John Davis, John Quarles

Real-time cognitive load assessment from eye-tracking signals could potentially enable adaptive human-centered-AI such as safety-critical applications such as driver vigilance monitoring or automated flight deck assistance, yet two challenges persist: handling frequent data missingness from blinks and tracking failures, and efficiently modeling long-range temporal dependencies. We propose MambaGaze, a framework that addresses these challenges through 1) XMD encoding, which augments raw features with observation masks and time-deltas to explicitly model data uncertainty, and 2) bidirectional Mamba-2, which captures temporal dependencies with linear computational complexity. Experiments on CLARE and CL-Drive datasets under leave-one-subject-out evaluation show that MambaGaze achieves 76.8% and 73.1% accuracy, respectively, outperforming CNN, Transformer, ResNet, and VGG baselines by 4-12 percentage points. Edge deployment benchmarks on NVIDIA Jetson platforms demonstrate real-time inference at 43-68 FPS with power consumption below 7.5W, confirming feasibility for wearable cognitive load monitoring.

摘要：即時的認知負荷評估來自眼動追踪信號，可能使以人為中心的自適應人工智慧成為可能，例如安全關鍵應用，如駕駛員警覺性監測或自動化飛行甲板輔助，但仍然存在兩個挑戰：處理因眨眼和追踪失敗而頻繁出現的數據缺失，以及有效建模長期時間依賴性。我們提出了MambaGaze，這是一個通過1) XMD編碼來解決這些挑戰的框架，該編碼通過觀察掩碼和時間差來增強原始特徵，以明確建模數據不確定性，以及2) 雙向Mamba-2，該模型以線性計算複雜度捕捉時間依賴性。在CLARE和CL-Drive數據集上進行的留一主體評估實驗顯示，MambaGaze分別達到76.8%和73.1%的準確率，超過CNN、Transformer、ResNet和VGG基準4-12個百分點。在NVIDIA Jetson平台上的邊緣部署基準測試顯示，實時推斷達到43-68 FPS，功耗低於7.5W，確認了可穿戴認知負荷監測的可行性。

##### **CogAdapt: Transferring Clinical ECG Foundation Models to Wearable Cognitive Load Assessment via Lead Adaptation**
2605.22774v1 by Amir Mousavi, Mohammad Sadegh Sirjani, Erfan Nourbakhsh, Mimi Xie, Rocky Slavin, Leslie Neely, John Davis, John Quarles

Real-time cognitive load assessment is essential for adaptive human-computer interaction but remains challenging due to limited labeled data and poor cross-subject generalization. Recent ECG foundation models pre-trained on millions of clinical recordings offer rich representations, but cannot be directly applied to wearable devices due to sensor configuration mismatch and task differences. In this paper, we propose CogAdapt, a framework that adapts clinical ECG foundation models to wearable cognitive load assessment. CogAdapt introduces LeadBridge, a learnable adapter that transforms 3-lead wearable signals into anatomically consistent 12-lead representations, and ProFine, a progressive fine-tuning strategy that gradually unfreezes encoder layers while preventing catastrophic forgetting. Evaluations on two public datasets (CLARE and CL-Drive) under leave-one-subject-out cross-validation show that CogAdapt substantially outperforms baselines trained from scratch, achieving macro-F1 scores of 0.626 and 0.768. These results demonstrate the promise of foundation model adaptation for subject-independent cognitive load assessment from wearable sensors.

摘要：即時認知負荷評估對於自適應人機互動至關重要，但由於標記數據有限和跨主體泛化能力差，這一任務仍然具有挑戰性。最近在數百萬臨床錄音上預訓練的心電圖基礎模型提供了豐富的表示，但由於傳感器配置不匹配和任務差異，無法直接應用於可穿戴設備。在本文中，我們提出了CogAdapt，一個將臨床心電圖基礎模型適應於可穿戴認知負荷評估的框架。CogAdapt引入了LeadBridge，一個可學習的適配器，將3導聯可穿戴信號轉換為解剖學一致的12導聯表示，以及ProFine，一種逐步微調策略，在防止災難性遺忘的同時逐漸解凍編碼器層。在兩個公共數據集（CLARE和CL-Drive）下進行的留一主體交叉驗證評估顯示，CogAdapt在從零開始訓練的基準上顯著優於，達到0.626和0.768的宏F1分數。這些結果顯示了基礎模型適應於可穿戴傳感器進行主體獨立認知負荷評估的潛力。

##### **Reducing Political Manipulation with Consistency Training**
2605.22771v1 by Long Phan, Devin Kim, Alexander Pan, Alice Blair, Adam Khoja, Dan Hendrycks

Large language models (LLMs) exhibit systematic political bias across a variety of sensitive contexts. We find that LLMs handle counterpart topics from opposing political sides asymmetrically. We refer to this phenomenon as covert political bias and identify 7 categories of techniques through which it operates. We propose two metrics for covert bias: Sentiment Consistency measures symmetry in rhetoric and framing across paired political prompts; Helpfulness Consistency measures symmetric depth and engagement. To reduce both types of covert bias, we introduce Political Consistency Training (PCT), an RL training method with two complementary paradigms: Sentiment Consistency Training and Helpfulness Consistency Training. We show that PCT preserves overall helpfulness, substantially reduces covert political bias, and generalizes to held-out benchmarks. We release our work at https://political-manipulation.ai

##### **Understanding Data Temporality Impact on Large Language Models Pre-training**
2605.22769v1 by Pilchen Hippolyte, Fabre Romain, Signe Talla Franck, Perez Patrick, Grave Edouard

Large language models (LLMs) are typically trained on shuffled corpora, yielding models whose knowledge is frozen at train time and whose temporal grounding remains poorly understood. In this work, we study the impact of pre-training dynamics on the acquisition of time-sensitive factual knowledge, focusing specifically on data ordering. Our main contributions are twofold. First, we introduce a comprehensive benchmark of over 7,000 temporally grounded questions and an evaluation protocol that enables analysis of whether models correctly associate facts with their corresponding time periods. Second, we pretrain 6B-parameter models on temporally ordered Common Crawl snapshots and compare them against standard shuffled pre-training. Our results show that sequentially trained models match shuffled baselines on general language understanding and common knowledge while consistently exhibiting more up-to-date and temporally precise knowledge. Temporally ordered pre-training yields improved factual freshness, while shuffled pre-training peaks on older data, possibly due to increased factual repetition. These findings, along with the release of our code at https://github.com/kyutai-labs/kairos , checkpoints, and datasets at https://huggingface.co/collections/kyutai/kairos provide a foundation for future research on continual learning for LLMs.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）通常在隨機排列的語料庫上進行訓練，產生的模型其知識在訓練時被凍結，且其時間基礎仍然不甚了解。<lb/>在本研究中，我們探討了預訓練動態對於獲取時間敏感事實知識的影響，特別關注數據排序。<lb/>我們的主要貢獻有兩個方面。<lb/>首先，我們引入了一個包含超過7,000個時間基礎問題的綜合基準，以及一個評估協議，使得可以分析模型是否正確將事實與其對應的時間段關聯起來。<lb/>其次，我們在時間排序的Common Crawl快照上預訓練了6B參數模型，並將其與標準的隨機預訓練進行比較。<lb/>我們的結果顯示，按順序訓練的模型在一般語言理解和常識上與隨機基準相匹配，同時持續展現出更為最新和時間上精確的知識。<lb/>時間排序的預訓練提高了事實的新鮮度，而隨機預訓練則在舊數據上達到高峰，這可能是由於事實重複的增加。<lb/>這些發現，以及我們的代碼在 https://github.com/kyutai-labs/kairos 、檢查點和數據集在 https://huggingface.co/collections/kyutai/kairos 的發布，為未來對LLMs的持續學習研究提供了基礎。

##### **Advancing Mathematics Research with AI-Driven Formal Proof Search**
2605.22763v1 by George Tsoukalas, Anton Kovsharov, Sergey Shirobokov, Anja Surina, Moritz Firsching, Gergely Bérczi, Francisco J. R. Ruiz, Arun Suggala, Adam Zsolt Wagner, Eric Wieser, Lei Yu, Aja Huang, Miklós Z. Horváth, Andrew Ferrauiolo, Henryk Michalewski, Codrut Grosu, Thomas Hubert, Matej Balog, Pushmeet Kohli, Swarat Chaudhuri

Large language models (LLMs) increasingly excel at mathematical reasoning, but their unreliability limits their utility in mathematics research. A mitigation is using LLMs to generate formal proofs in languages like Lean. We perform the first large-scale evaluation of this method's ability to solve open problems. Our most capable agent autonomously resolved 9 of 353 open Erdős problems at the per-problem cost of a few hundred dollars, proved 44/492 OEIS conjectures, and is being deployed in combinatorics, optimization, graph theory, algebraic geometry, and quantum optics research. A basic agent alternating LLM-based generation with Lean-based verification replicated the Erdős successes but proved costlier on the hardest problems. These findings demonstrate the power of AI-aided formal proof search and shed light on the agent designs that enable it.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）在數學推理方面越來越出色，但它們的不可靠性限制了它們在數學研究中的實用性。一種緩解方法是使用LLMs生成像Lean這樣的語言中的正式證明。我們對這種方法解決未解決問題的能力進行了首次大規模評估。我們最強大的代理自主解決了353個開放的Erdős問題中的9個，每個問題的成本為幾百美元，證明了44/492個OEIS猜想，並正在應用於組合學、優化、圖論、代數幾何和量子光學研究。一個基本的代理交替使用基於LLM的生成和基於Lean的驗證，複製了Erdős的成功，但在最難的問題上成本更高。這些發現展示了AI輔助正式證明搜索的力量，並闡明了使其可行的代理設計。

##### **Towards a General Intelligence and Interface for Wearable Health Data**
2605.22759v1 by Girish Narayanswamy, Maxwell A. Xu, A. Ali Heydari, Samy Abdel-Ghaffar, Marius Guerard, Kara Vaillancourt, Zhihan Zhang, Jake Garrison, Levi Albuquerque, Dimitris Spathis, Hong Yu, Hamid Palangi, Xuhai "Orson" Xu, David G. T. Barrett, Joseph Breda, Jed McGiffin, Yubin Kim, Yuwei Zhang, Naghmeh Rezaei, Samuel Solomon, Karan Ahuja, Tim Althoff, Jake Sunshine, Ming-Zher Poh, Benjamin Yetton, Ari Winbush, Nicholas B. While ubiquitous wearable sensors capture a wealth of behavioral and physiological information, effectively transforming these signals into personalized health insights is challenging. Specifically, converting low-level sensor data into representations capable of characterizing higher-level states is difficult due to high phenotypic diversity and variation in individual baseline health, physiology, and lifestyle factors. Moreover, collecting wearable data paired with health outcome annotations is laborious and expensive, and retrospective annotation remains practically unfeasible, contributing to a scarcity of data with high-quality labels. To overcome these limitations, we propose a foundation model for wearable health that is pretrained on more than one trillion minutes of unlabeled sensor signals drawn from a large cohort of five million participants. We demonstrate that the joint scaling of model capacity and pretraining data volume leads to systematic improvements in performance, as evaluated on a diverse set of 35 health prediction tasks, spanning cardiovascular, metabolic, sleep, and mental health, as well as lifestyle choices and demographic factors. We find that this population scale representation unlocks label-efficient few-shot learning and generative capabilities for robust daily metric estimation. To further leverage this learned representation, we deploy a classroom of LLM agents to autonomously search the space of downstream predictive heads built on the model embeddings, showing broad performance improvements that increase with LLM model capacity. Finally, we show how integrating these downstream predictors into a Personal Health Agent can support model responses that are more relevant, contextually aware, and safe, and we validate this via 1,860 ratings from a cohort of clinicians.

##### **Cyber-Physical Anomaly Detection in IoT-Enabled Smart Grids Using Machine Learning and Metaheuristic Feature Optimization**
2605.22749v1 by Adis Alihodžić, Eva Tuba, Milan Tuba

Modern smart grids rely on dense measurement infrastructures, communication links, and intelligent field devices. Although this improves supervision and control, it also increases vulnerability to cyber-physical disruptions. Operators must distinguish physical incidents, such as faults or line disturbances, from malicious actions, such as false data injection or unauthorized command execution. This chapter investigates this problem using the well-known MSU/ORNL Power System Attack Dataset. The proposed method combines machine learning with genetic-algorithm-based feature selection. The objective is twofold: to classify attack and natural events accurately, and to determine whether a reduced set of physically informative PMU/IED measurements can support reliable detection. Several baseline models are evaluated, including logistic regression, RBF-SVM, XGBoost, Random Forest, and Extra Trees. The results show that tree-based ensemble models are the most effective for the considered dataset, with Extra Trees providing the strongest full-feature baseline. After feature selection, the GA + Extra Trees model reduces the clean PMU feature space from 112 attributes to an average of 27.4 attributes over five runs, while increasing macro-F1 from 0.9118 to 0.9212 and ROC-AUC from 0.9791 to 0.9837. These results indicate that many synchronized electrical measurements are redundant. A compact subset of phasor-based features can still provide accurate and interpretable anomaly detection in smart grids.

##### **Proxy-Based Approximation of Shapley and Banzhaf Interactions**
2605.22738v1 by Santo M. A. R. Thies, Hubert Baniecki, R. Teal Witter, Eyke Hüllermeier, Maximilian Muschalik, Fabian Fumagalli

Shapley and Banzhaf interactions capture the complex dynamics inherent in modern machine learning applications. However, current estimators for these higher-order interactions trade off between speed and accuracy. To overcome this limitation, we introduce ProxySHAP. ProxySHAP reconciles the high sample efficiency of tree-based proxy models with a principled path to consistency via residual correction. On a theoretical level, we derive a polynomial-time generalization of interventional TreeSHAP to compute exact interaction indices for tree ensembles, successfully bypassing exponential tree-depth dependencies in prior methods. Furthermore, we formally analyze the residual adjustment strategy, characterizing the specific conditions under which Maximum Sample Reuse (MSR) corrects proxy bias without its variance scaling exponentially with interaction size. Extensive benchmarking demonstrates that ProxySHAP sets a new state-of-the-art standard for approximation quality, including in large-scale applications with thousands of features. By achieving the lowest error in both small- and large-budget regimes, ProxySHAP significantly outperforms the prior best estimators ProxySPEX and KernelSHAP-IQ, while also delivering superior performance on downstream explainability tasks.

摘要：Shapley 和 Banzhaf 互動捕捉了現代機器學習應用中固有的複雜動態。<lb/>然而，目前這些高階互動的估計器在速度和準確性之間存在權衡。<lb/>為了克服這一限制，我們引入了 ProxySHAP。<lb/>ProxySHAP 將基於樹的代理模型的高樣本效率與通過殘差校正實現一致性的原則性路徑相結合。<lb/>在理論層面上，我們推導出一種多項式時間的干預 TreeSHAP 的廣義形式，以計算樹集成的精確互動指數，成功地避開了先前方法中指數樹深度的依賴性。<lb/>此外，我們正式分析了殘差調整策略，描述了最大樣本重用（MSR）在何種特定條件下能夠校正代理偏差，而不會隨著互動大小的增加而指數增長其方差。<lb/>廣泛的基準測試顯示，ProxySHAP 在近似質量上設立了新的最先進標準，包括在具有數千個特徵的大規模應用中。<lb/>通過在小型和大型預算範疇內實現最低的誤差，ProxySHAP 顯著超越了先前最佳的估計器 ProxySPEX 和 KernelSHAP-IQ，同時在下游可解釋性任務上也表現出色。

##### **The Distillation Game: Adaptive Attacks & Efficient Defenses**
2605.22737v1 by Youssef Allouah, Mahdi Haghifam, Sanmi Koyejo, Reza Shokri

Distillation attacks create a deployment trade-off for model providers: the same outputs that make a model more useful can also make it easier to imitate. We study this trade-off through a minimax game between a utility-constrained teacher and an adaptive student. Our framework yields tractable one-sided response rules: an adaptive evaluation rule in which the student reweights high-value examples, and a teacher-side defense template that suppresses outputs most useful for distillation. From a cheap proxy for example value, we derive Product-of-Experts (PoE), a simple forward-pass-only defense that combines the teacher with a proxy student during generation. Empirically, adaptive evaluation reveals a large passive--adaptive gap: on state-of-the-art defenses, adaptive students recover substantially more capability than passive evaluation suggests on GSM8K and MATH. Under this stronger evaluation, the apparent robustness gap between expensive defenses and PoE narrows considerably, while PoE remains substantially cheaper and preserves higher-quality reasoning traces. Overall, our results suggest that strong distillation remains difficult to stop, and that progress on antidistillation should be judged against adaptive students rather than passive ones. Our code is available at: https://github.com/ysfalh/distillation-game.

摘要：蒸餾攻擊為模型提供者創造了一個部署權衡：使模型更有用的相同輸出也可能使其更容易被模仿。我們通過一個在效用受限的教師和一個自適應學生之間的最小最大博弈來研究這個權衡。我們的框架產生了可處理的單側反應規則：一種自適應評估規則，其中學生重新加權高價值範例，以及一個教師端防禦模板，抑制對蒸餾最有用的輸出。從一個便宜的範例價值代理中，我們推導出專家乘積（Product-of-Experts, PoE），這是一種簡單的僅前向傳遞的防禦，在生成過程中將教師與代理學生結合起來。實證結果顯示，自適應評估揭示了巨大的被動--自適應差距：在最先進的防禦下，自適應學生恢復的能力遠超過被動評估在GSM8K和MATH上所暗示的。在這種更強的評估下，昂貴防禦和PoE之間明顯的穩健性差距顯著縮小，而PoE仍然便宜得多，並保持更高質量的推理痕跡。總體而言，我們的結果表明，強蒸餾仍然難以阻止，對抗蒸餾的進展應該根據自適應學生而不是被動學生來評價。我們的代碼可在以下網址獲得：https://github.com/ysfalh/distillation-game。

##### **ChronoMedKG: A Temporally-Grounded Biomedical Knowledge Graph and Benchmark for Clinical Reasoning**
2605.22734v1 by Md Shamim Ahmed, Farzaneh Firoozbakht, Lukas Galke Poech, Jan Baumbach, Richard Röttger

Biomedical knowledge graphs (KGs) treat disease associations as static facts, but temporal information is crucial for clinical reasoning, e.g., a symptom diagnostic of one disease at age 3 may imply a different disease at age 13. Existing KGs such as PrimeKG, Hetionet, and iKraph do not encode when a finding becomes clinically relevant over the course of a disease. This limits their usefulness for longitudinal clinical reasoning and retrieval augmentation.
  We introduce ChronoMedKG, a temporal biomedical knowledge graph that contains 460,497 evidence-linked triples (filtered from 13M raw extractions) covering 13,431 diseases. Each association is tied to temporal components like onset window or progression stage, which are backed by PMID-traceable evidence and a multi-signal credibility score. The graph is constructed through a disease-autonomous multi-agent pipeline in which multiple frontier LLMs independently extract knowledge from PubMed and PMC literature. Only those relations are kept that are supported by multi-model consensus, survive credibility filtering, as well as ontology alignment.
  ChronoMedKG scored 92.7% agreement against Orphadata and adds temporal grounding for 6,250 diseases absent from HPOA, Orphadata, and Phenopackets, including 1,657 Orphanet-coded rare diseases. We further introduce ChronoTQA, a benchmark of 3,341 questions across eight task types (six temporal plus two static controls), with a 12-question supplementary probe. Frontier LLMs lose roughly 30 points moving from static to temporal questions; ChronoMedKG retrieval rescues 47-65% of their long-tail failures, against 17-29% for HPOA-RAG. As such, ChronoMedKG provides a crucial temporal axis for retrieval-augmented clinical systems that was previously absent.

摘要：生物醫學知識圖譜（KGs）將疾病關聯視為靜態事實，但時間信息對於臨床推理至關重要，例如，3歲時診斷為某種疾病的症狀可能在13歲時暗示另一種疾病。現有的KGs，如PrimeKG、Hetionet和iKraph，並未編碼在疾病過程中何時發現變得臨床相關。這限制了它們在縱向臨床推理和檢索增強方面的實用性。<lb/>

##### **HarnessAPI: A Skill-First Framework for Unified Streaming APIs and MCP Tools**
2605.22733v1 by Edwin Jose

Every Python function deployed as an LLM tool must today exist in two forms: an HTTP endpoint for human-facing clients and CI pipelines, and an MCP tool registration for agent runtimes such as Claude and Cursor. These representations share business logic yet diverge in all the surrounding machinery (routing, validation, serialisation, streaming, and schema maintenance), and they drift apart as the underlying code evolves. We present HarnessAPI, a Python framework that eliminates this duplication by treating a typed skill folder as the single source of truth. From one handler.py plus Pydantic schemas, the framework automatically derives a streaming HTTP endpoint with Server-Sent Events, an interactive OpenAPI/Swagger UI, and a zero-configuration MCP tool, all served from a single process. Dual-mode content negotiation lets the same handler serve SSE-streaming and JSON-returning clients with no handler changes. A dynamic code-generation mechanism ensures Pydantic type annotations propagate correctly to FastMCP's inspection layer, resolving a technical limitation that prevents naive closure-based registration. Measured across six representative skills using cloc, HarnessAPI reduces framework-facing boilerplate by 74% compared with a manually maintained dual-stack implementation (FastAPI server + FastMCP server). HarnessAPI subclasses FastAPI, inheriting its full middleware, dependency-injection, and deployment ecosystem. It is available at https://github.com/edwinjosechittilappilly/harnessapi and on PyPI (pip install harnessapi)

摘要：每個作為 LLM 工具部署的 Python 函數今天必須以兩種形式存在：一個供人類客戶端和 CI 管道使用的 HTTP 端點，以及一個供 Claude 和 Cursor 等代理運行時使用的 MCP 工具註冊。這些表示共享業務邏輯，但在所有周邊機制（路由、驗證、序列化、流式傳輸和架構維護）上有所不同，隨著底層代碼的演變而逐漸分離。我們提出了 HarnessAPI，一個 Python 框架，通過將類型化技能文件夾視為唯一的真相來源來消除這種重複。從一個 handler.py 加上 Pydantic 架構，該框架自動推導出一個帶有伺服器推送事件的流式 HTTP 端點、一個互動式的 OpenAPI/Swagger UI，以及一個零配置的 MCP 工具，所有這些都由單一進程提供服務。雙模式內容協商允許相同的處理器為 SSE 流式和 JSON 返回的客戶端提供服務，而無需更改處理器。動態代碼生成機制確保 Pydantic 類型註解正確地傳播到 FastMCP 的檢查層，解決了一個技術限制，該限制阻止了基於閉包的天真註冊。通過使用 cloc 對六個代表性技能進行測量，HarnessAPI 與手動維護的雙棧實現（FastAPI 伺服器 + FastMCP 伺服器）相比，減少了 74% 的框架面向的樣板代碼。HarnessAPI 是 FastAPI 的子類，繼承了其完整的中介軟體、依賴注入和部署生態系統。它可以在 https://github.com/edwinjosechittilappilly/harnessapi 和 PyPI（pip install harnessapi）上獲得。

##### **Beyond Acoustic Emotion Recognition: Multimodal Pathos Analysis in Political Speech Using LLM-Based and Acoustic Emotion Models**
2605.22732v1 by Juergen Dietrich

We investigate whether acoustic emotion recognition models can serve as proxies for the Pathos dimension in political speech analysis, as operationalised by the TRUST multi-agent large language model (LLM) pipeline. Using a Bundestag plenary speech by Felix Banaszak (51 segments, 245 s) as a case study, we compare three analysis modalities: (1) emotion2vec_plus_large, an acoustic speech emotion recognition (SER) model whose continuous Arousal and Valence values are derived via post-hoc Russell Circumplex projection; (2) Gemini 2.5 Flash, an LLM analysing the full speech audio together with its transcript in an open-ended, context-aware fashion; and (3) TRUST-Pathos scores from a three-advocate LLM supervisor ensemble. Spearman rank correlations reveal that Gemini Valence correlates strongly with TRUST-Pathos (rho = +0.664, p < 0.001), whereas emotion2vec Valence does not (rho = +0.097, p = 0.499). We further demonstrate, via a systematic quality evaluation of the Berlin Database of Emotional Speech (EMO-DB) using Gemini in an open-ended annotation paradigm, that standard SER benchmark corpora suffer from acted speech, cultural bias, and category incompatibility. Our results suggest that LLM-based multimodal analysis captures semantically defined political emotion substantially better than acoustic models alone, while acoustic features remain informative for low-level Arousal estimation. Future work will extend this approach to video-based analysis incorporating facial expression and gaze.

摘要：我們調查聲音情感識別模型是否可以作為政治演講分析中Pathos維度的代理，這一維度由TRUST多代理大型語言模型（LLM）管道操作化。以Felix Banaszak的德國聯邦議院全體會議演講（51個片段，245秒）作為案例研究，我們比較三種分析模式：（1）emotion2vec_plus_large，一種聲音演講情感識別（SER）模型，其連續的喚起和價值值通過事後的Russell Circumplex投影得出；（2）Gemini 2.5 Flash，一種LLM以開放式、上下文感知的方式分析完整的演講音頻及其文字記錄；以及（3）來自三位倡導者LLM監督者集成的TRUST-Pathos分數。Spearman等級相關性顯示，Gemini的價值與TRUST-Pathos強烈相關（rho = +0.664，p < 0.001），而emotion2vec的價值則不然（rho = +0.097，p = 0.499）。我們進一步通過使用Gemini在開放式標註範式中對柏林情感語音數據庫（EMO-DB）進行系統質量評估，證明標準SER基準語料庫存在表演性語音、文化偏見和類別不相容性。我們的結果表明，基於LLM的多模態分析在捕捉語義定義的政治情感方面顯著優於僅使用聲音模型，而聲音特徵對低層次的喚起估計仍然具有信息價值。未來的工作將擴展此方法至結合面部表情和凝視的視頻分析。

##### **Post-Training is About States, Not Tokens: A State Distribution View of SFT, RL, and On-Policy Distillation**
2605.22731v1 by Dong Nie

Large language model post-training methods such as supervised fine-tuning (SFT), reinforcement learning (RL), and distillation are often analyzed through their loss functions: maximum likelihood, policy gradients, forward KL, reverse KL, or related objective-level variants. We study a complementary factor: the state distribution on which supervision is applied. For an autoregressive policy, a state is a prompt plus generated prefix. SFT trains on fixed dataset states, while RL and on-policy distillation (OPD) train on states induced by the current learner. We formalize post-training as state-distribution shaping and run a controlled smallscale study using Qwen3-0.6B-Base on GSM8K, with TruthfulQA and MMLU as retention evaluations. Our results show three phenomena. First, a mild SFT run improves GSM8K with little forgetting, while a stress SFT run causes substantial retention loss. Second, OPD from a degraded SFT teacher surpasses that teacher on GSM8K, TruthfulQA, and MMLU, despite using the teacher as its only supervision source. Third, a lightweight on-policy RL run improves GSM8K while preserving retention. These results support a state-centric view of post-training: the source and locality of training states can be as important as the form of the supervision signal.

摘要：大型語言模型的後訓練方法，如監督微調（SFT）、強化學習（RL）和蒸餾，通常通過其損失函數進行分析：最大似然、策略梯度、前向KL、反向KL或相關的目標級變體。我們研究一個互補因素：施加監督的狀態分佈。對於自回歸策略，狀態是提示加上生成的前綴。SFT 在固定數據集狀態上進行訓練，而 RL 和在線蒸餾（OPD）則在當前學習者誘導的狀態上進行訓練。我們將後訓練形式化為狀態分佈塑形，並使用 Qwen3-0.6B-Base 在 GSM8K 上進行受控的小規模研究，以 TruthfulQA 和 MMLU 作為保留評估。我們的結果顯示三個現象。首先，輕度的 SFT 執行改善了 GSM8K，幾乎沒有遺忘，而壓力 SFT 執行則導致了顯著的保留損失。其次，來自退化 SFT 教師的 OPD 在 GSM8K、TruthfulQA 和 MMLU 上超越了該教師，儘管只使用該教師作為唯一的監督來源。第三，輕量級的在線 RL 執行改善了 GSM8K，同時保持了保留。這些結果支持了一種以狀態為中心的後訓練觀點：訓練狀態的來源和位置可能與監督信號的形式一樣重要。

##### **The Value of Covariance Matching in Gaussian DDPMs and the Lanczos Sampler**
2605.22723v1 by Md Sahil Akhtar, Aymane El Gadarri, Vivek F. Farias, Adam D. Jozefiak

A central error measure in Gaussian DDPMs is the path-space KL divergence between the exact reverse chain and the learned Gaussian reverse process. This quantity is especially relevant for procedures such as classifier guidance, which perturb the entire reverse trajectory rather than only the terminal sample. Prior analyses show that standard isotropic reverse covariances suffer an unavoidable $Ω(1/T)$ path-KL error as the number of denoising steps $T$ grows. We show that matching the full posterior covariance breaks this barrier, yielding an order-wise improvement that reduces the path KL to $O(1/T^2)$. To make full covariance matching practical, we introduce the Lanczos Gaussian sampler (LGS), a training-free, matrix-free method for sampling from the optimal reverse covariance using only covariance-vector products, which are available through Jacobian-vector products of the posterior mean. LGS avoids dense covariance storage and auxiliary covariance models. We prove that LGS approximation error decays exponentially in the number of Lanczos steps, where each Lanczos step requires a single Jacobian-vector product. Empirically, using only just three such steps improves sample quality over strong diagonal-covariance baselines, including OCM-DDPM, across standard image benchmarks. This identifies full covariance matching as both theoretically valuable and practically accessible for fast DDPM sampling.

摘要：一個在高斯DDPM中的核心誤差度量是精確反向鏈與學習到的高斯反向過程之間的路徑空間KL散度。<lb/>這個量對於像分類器引導這樣的程序特別相關，因為這些程序會擾動整個反向軌跡，而不僅僅是終端樣本。<lb/>先前的分析顯示，標準的各向同性反向協方差隨著去噪步驟數$T$的增加，會遭受不可避免的$Ω(1/T)$路徑-KL誤差。<lb/>我們顯示，匹配完整的後驗協方差打破了這一障礙，帶來了逐次改進，將路徑KL降低到$O(1/T^2)$。<lb/>為了使完整協方差匹配變得實用，我們引入了Lanczos高斯取樣器（LGS），這是一種無需訓練、無需矩陣的方法，僅使用協方差-向量乘積從最佳反向協方差中取樣，這些乘積可以通過後驗均值的雅可比-向量乘積獲得。<lb/>LGS避免了密集的協方差存儲和輔助協方差模型。<lb/>我們證明，LGS的近似誤差隨著Lanczos步驟數的增加而指數衰減，每個Lanczos步驟需要一個雅可比-向量乘積。<lb/>在實證上，僅使用三個這樣的步驟就能改善樣本質量，超越強大的對角協方差基準，包括OCM-DDPM，在標準圖像基準測試中。<lb/>這表明完整協方差匹配在理論上是有價值的，並且在快速DDPM取樣中是實際可及的。

##### **Can AI Make Conflicts Worse? An Alignment Failure in LLM Deployment Across Conflict Contexts**
2605.22720v1 by Andrii Kryshtal

AI models are already deployed in societies affected by armed conflict, and journalists, humanitarian workers, governments and ordinary citizens rely on them for information or for their work processes. No established practice exists for checking whether their outputs can make those conflicts worse. We tested nine model configurations from four providers (OpenAI, Anthropic, DeepSeek, xAI) on 90 multi-turn scenarios designed to surface misaligned behaviour in conflict contexts: false equivalence between documented atrocities, denial of genocide, and failure to recognise ethnic slurs, among others. When such outputs feed into journalism, humanitarian reporting, or public debate, they can deepen divisions in fragile societies. Failure rates span 6\% to 47\% between the best and worst performing models, which makes model choice a safety question in its own right and when users pushed for ``balance'' in cases where international courts have already assigned responsibility, five of nine configurations failed 80 to 100 percent of the time. We release the first evaluation framework for this domain and propose adding it to alignment evaluation portfolios.

摘要：AI 模型已在受武裝衝突影響的社會中部署，記者、人道工作者、政府和普通公民依賴它們獲取信息或進行工作流程。尚未建立檢查其輸出是否可能加劇這些衝突的實踐。我們測試了來自四個提供商（OpenAI、Anthropic、DeepSeek、xAI）的九種模型配置，針對90個多輪場景進行設計，以揭示衝突背景中的不當行為：包括對已記錄的暴行的虛假等同、對種族滅絕的否認，以及未能識別種族歧視詞語等情況。當這些輸出進入新聞報導、人道主義報告或公共辯論時，可能會加深脆弱社會中的分歧。最佳和最差表現模型之間的失敗率範圍從6\%到47\%，這使得模型選擇本身成為一個安全問題，而當用戶在國際法院已經分配責任的情況下推動“平衡”時，九種配置中有五種在80%到100%的時間內失敗。我們發布了該領域的第一個評估框架，並建議將其納入對齊評估組合中。

##### **Live Music Diffusion Models: Efficient Fine-Tuning and Post-Training of Interactive Diffusion Music Generators**
2605.22717v1 by Zachary Novack, Stephen Brade, Haven Kim, Hugo Flores García, Nithya Shikarpur, Chinmay Talegaonkar, Suwan Kim, Valerie K. Chen, Julian McAuley, Taylor Berg-Kirkpatrick, Cheng-Zhi Anna Huang

Interactive streaming music generation promises the use of generative models for live performance and co-creation that is impossible with offline models. However, SOTA models exist in the discrete-AR regime, requiring industrial levels of compute for both training and inference. In this work, we investigate whether audio diffusion models, with their wide support in the open-source community but non-streaming bidirectional nature, can be repurposed efficiently into interactive models accessible on consumer hardware. By taking a critical look at the modern pipeline for block-wise outpainting diffusion, we identify critical inefficiencies during inference that result in strictly worse computational efficiency than their discrete-AR counterparts. We propose Live Music Diffusion Models (LMDMs), a simple modification of the generative diffusion process that recovers, and then outperforms, the inference complexity of the discrete Live Music Models (LMMs) through block-wise KV Caching. Unlike LMMs, LMDMs further enable stable post-training alignment through our novel ARC-Forcing paradigm, reducing error accumulation without any explicit RL or reward models. We demonstrate the application of LMDMs in a number of creative domains, including text-conditioned generation, sketch-based music synthesis, and jamming. We finally show how LMDMs can be used as a generative instrument in a real artist-AI collaboration, utilizing LMDMs as a "generative delay" to transform musicians' improvisation live for variable timbral effects while running locally on a consumer gaming laptop.

摘要：互動式串流音樂生成承諾使用生成模型進行現場表演和共同創作，這在離線模型中是無法實現的。然而，最先進的模型存在於離散自回歸（discrete-AR）範疇，對於訓練和推斷都需要工業級別的計算資源。在本研究中，我們探討音頻擴散模型是否可以有效地重新利用，儘管它們在開源社區中得到廣泛支持，但其非串流的雙向特性使其難以轉化為可在消費者硬體上訪問的互動模型。通過對現代塊狀擴散的管道進行批判性分析，我們識別出推斷過程中的關鍵低效，這導致其計算效率明顯低於離散自回歸模型。我們提出了現場音樂擴散模型（LMDMs），這是一種對生成擴散過程的簡單修改，通過塊狀鍵值緩存（KV Caching）恢復並超越離散現場音樂模型（LMMs）的推斷複雜度。與LMMs不同，LMDMs進一步通過我們的新穎ARC-Forcing範式實現穩定的後訓練對齊，減少了錯誤累積，而不需要任何明確的強化學習或獎勵模型。我們展示了LMDMs在多個創意領域的應用，包括文本條件生成、草圖音樂合成和即興演奏。我們最終展示了如何將LMDMs用作真實藝術家與AI合作中的生成工具，利用LMDMs作為“生成延遲”，即時轉換音樂家的即興演奏，以實現可變音色效果，同時在消費者遊戲筆記本上本地運行。

##### **AnyMo: Geometry-Aware Setup-Agnostic Modeling of Human Motion in the Wild**
2605.22715v1 by Baiyu Chen, Zechen Li, Wilson Wongso, Lihuan Li, Xiachong Lin, Hao Xue, Benjamin Tag, Flora Salim

As wearable and mobile devices become increasingly embedded in daily life, they offer a practical way to continuously sense human motion in the wild. But inertial signals are highly dependent on the sensing setup, including body location, mounting position, sensor orientation, device hardware, and sampling protocol. This setup dependence makes it difficult to learn motion representations that transfer across devices and datasets, and limits the broader use of wearable IMUs beyond closed-set recognition. We introduce AnyMo, a geometry-aware framework for setup-agnostic human motion modeling. AnyMo uses physics-grounded IMU simulation over dense body-surface placements to generate diverse and plausible synthetic signals, pre-trains a graph encoder from paired synthetic placement views and masked partial observations, tokenizes multi-position IMU into full-body motion tokens, and aligns these tokens with an LLM for motion-language understanding. We evaluate AnyMo on three complementary tasks: zero-shot activity recognition across 14 unseen downstream datasets, cross-modal retrieval, and wearable IMU motion captioning, where it improves average Accuracy/F1/R@2 by 11.7\%/11.6\%/22.6\% on HAR, increases zero-shot IMU-to-text and text-to-IMU retrieval MRR by 15.9\% and 28.6\%, respectively, and improves zero-shot captioning BERT-F1 by 18.8\%. These results support AnyMo as a generalist model for wearable motion understanding in the wild. Project page: https://baiyuchen.com/project/AnyMo.

摘要：隨著可穿戴和移動設備越來越深入日常生活，它們提供了一種實用的方法來持續感知人類在自然環境中的運動。<lb/>但是，慣性信號高度依賴於感測設置，包括身體位置、安裝位置、感測器方向、設備硬體和取樣協議。<lb/>這種設置依賴性使得學習能夠跨設備和數據集轉移的運動表示變得困難，並限制了可穿戴IMU在封閉集識別之外的更廣泛應用。<lb/>我們介紹了AnyMo，一個對設置無關的人類運動建模的幾何感知框架。<lb/>AnyMo使用基於物理的IMU模擬，通過密集的身體表面放置來生成多樣且合理的合成信號，從配對的合成放置視圖和遮蔽的部分觀察中預訓練圖編碼器，將多位置IMU標記為全身運動標記，並將這些標記與LLM對齊以實現運動-語言理解。<lb/>我們在三個互補任務上評估AnyMo：在14個未見的下游數據集上進行零樣本活動識別，跨模態檢索，以及可穿戴IMU運動標註，在HAR上平均準確率/F1/R@2提高了11.7\%/11.6\%/22.6\%，零樣本IMU到文本和文本到IMU檢索的MRR分別提高了15.9\%和28.6\%，並且零樣本標註的BERT-F1提高了18.8\%。<lb/>這些結果支持AnyMo作為一個通用模型，用於在自然環境中理解可穿戴運動。<lb/>項目頁面：https://baiyuchen.com/project/AnyMo。

##### **AMEL: Accumulated Message Effects on LLM Judgments**
2605.22714v1 by Sid-ali Temkit

Large language models are routinely used as automated evaluators: to review code, moderate content, or score outputs, often with many items passing through one conversation. We ask whether the polarity of prior conversation history biases subsequent judgments, an effect we call the accumulated message effect on LLM judgments (AMEL). Across 75,898 API calls to 11 models from 4 providers (OpenAI, Anthropic, Google, and four open-source models), we present identical test items in isolation or following histories saturated with predominantly positive or negative evaluations.
  Models shift toward the conversation's prevailing polarity (d = -0.17, p < 10^-46). The effect concentrates on items where the model is genuinely uncertain at baseline (d = -0.34 for high-entropy items, vs d = -0.15 when the baseline is deterministic). Bias does not grow with context length: 5 prior turns and 50 produce the same shift (Spearman |r| < 0.01; OLS slope p = 0.80). And there is a negativity asymmetry: paired per item, negative histories induce 1.62x more bias than positive (t = 13.46, p < 10^-39, n = 2,481). Scaling helps but does not solve it (Anthropic: Haiku -0.22 to Opus -0.17; OpenAI: Nano -0.34 to GPT-5.2 -0.17).
  Three follow-ups narrow the mechanism. The token probability distribution shifts continuously, not at a threshold. The negativity asymmetry has both token-level and semantic components, though attributing the balance is exploratory at our sample sizes. Position does not matter: five biased turns anywhere in a 50-turn history produce the same shift. The simplest fix for evaluation pipelines is a fresh context per item; when batching is unavoidable, balancing the history helps.

摘要：大型語言模型常被用作自動評估者：來審查代碼、調節內容或評分輸出，通常在一次對話中會有許多項目通過。我們詢問先前對話歷史的極性是否會影響後續判斷，這種效應我們稱之為對LLM判斷的累積訊息效應（AMEL）。在對來自四個提供者（OpenAI、Anthropic、Google，以及四個開源模型）的11個模型進行75,898次API調用中，我們在孤立情況下或在主要為正面或負面評價的歷史之後呈現相同的測試項目。<lb/>
模型會向對話的主導極性轉變（d = -0.17，p < 10^-46）。這一效應集中在模型在基線上確實不確定的項目上（高熵項目的d = -0.34，而基線是確定性的時候d = -0.15）。偏見不隨上下文長度增加而增長：5個先前回合和50個產生相同的轉變（Spearman |r| < 0.01；OLS斜率p = 0.80）。而且存在負面不對稱性：每個項目配對，負面歷史引起的偏見是正面歷史的1.62倍（t = 13.46，p < 10^-39，n = 2,481）。擴展有幫助但無法解決問題（Anthropic: Haiku -0.22到Opus -0.17；OpenAI: Nano -0.34到GPT-5.2 -0.17）。<lb/>
三個後續研究縮小了機制。標記概率分佈持續變化，而不是在某個閾值。負面不對稱性具有標記級別和語義組件，儘管在我們的樣本大小中，歸因於平衡的探索性仍然存在。位置並不重要：在50回合歷史中的任何地方，五個有偏見的回合產生相同的轉變。對於評估管道，最簡單的解決方案是每個項目使用新的上下文；當批量處理無法避免時，平衡歷史有助於改善。

##### **Tokenization with Split Trees**
2605.22705v1 by Craig W. Schmidt, Michael Krumdick, Adam Wiemerslage, Seth Ebner, Varshini Reddy, Yuval Pinter, Chris Tanner

We introduce Tokenization with Split Trees (ToaST), a subword tokenization method that directly optimizes compression under a new recursive inference procedure. ToaST greedily splits each pretoken into a full binary tree using precomputed byte n-gram counts, independent of any vocabulary. Given a vocabulary, inference recursively descends each split tree and emits the first in-vocabulary node reached on each path. Vocabulary selection is formulated as an Integer Program (IP) that minimizes the total token count over all split trees under this inference procedure. The Linear Programming (LP) relaxation is near-integral in practice, yielding provably near-optimal vocabularies, with training time empirically scaling quadratically in the number of split trees. On English text, ToaST reduces token counts by more than 11% compared to BPE, WordPiece, and UnigramLM at vocabulary sizes of 40,960 and above, reducing the number of inference tokens for models using this tokenizer, thus extending the effective context length. ToaST also uses common single-byte tokens less frequently than these baselines, leading to a substantial improvement in Renyi efficiency. In experiments training 1.5B parameter language models, ToaST achieves the highest CORE score, outperforming baselines by 2.6%--7.6%, with significance for two of three, and scoring best on 13 of 22 individual tasks.

摘要：我們介紹了帶有分割樹的標記化方法（ToaST），這是一種子詞標記化方法，直接在新的遞歸推理程序下優化壓縮。ToaST 貪婪地將每個預標記分割成一個完整的二元樹，使用預計算的字節 n-gram 計數，與任何詞彙表無關。給定一個詞彙表，推理會遞歸地下降每個分割樹，並在每條路徑上發出到達的第一個詞彙表內節點。詞彙選擇被公式化為一個整數規劃（IP），旨在最小化在這個推理程序下所有分割樹的總標記數。線性規劃（LP）放鬆在實踐中接近整數，產生可證明的近似最佳詞彙表，訓練時間在經驗上隨著分割樹的數量以二次方增長。在英語文本中，ToaST 將標記數量相比 BPE、WordPiece 和 UnigramLM 減少了超過 11%，在詞彙表大小為 40,960 及以上時，減少了使用此標記器的模型的推理標記數量，從而延長了有效的上下文長度。ToaST 也使用常見的單字節標記的頻率低於這些基準，從而在 Renyi 效率上實現了顯著改善。在訓練 15 億參數的語言模型的實驗中，ToaST 獲得了最高的 CORE 分數，超越基準 2.6%--7.6%，對三個任務中的兩個具有顯著性，並在 22 個單獨任務中獲得 13 個最佳分數。

##### **Scout-Assisted Planning for Heterogeneous Robot Teams under Partially Known Environments**
2605.22693v1 by Hoang-Dung Bui, Abhish Khanal, Raihan Islam Arnob, Gregory J. Stein

Autonomous robot teams navigating partially known environments face costly backtracking when ground robots encounter blocked roads that are only revealed upon physical traversal. We address this with Scout-Assisted Planning, a heterogeneous planning framework in which scouting Unmanned Aerial Vehicles proactively gather environmental information to improve Unmanned Ground Vehicle navigation. To focus scouting on the most consequential edges, we propose Information Gain-based Action Pruning, which scores candidate scouting actions by their expected impact on ground robot behavior. Since exact Information Gain-based Action Pruning computation is prohibitively expensive, we develop a Graph Neural Network based model that predicts information gain values directly from graph structure and belief state, reducing planning time to real-time levels without sacrificing solution quality. Experiments across three environment types show that SAP with Information Gain Action Pruning reduces ground robot travel cost by 31.9--37.7% over the Canadian Traveler Problem baseline, and outperforms proximity-based scouting guidance by an additional 8--14%, confirming that principled information-gain-guided scouting is both more effective and computationally feasible for real-world deployment

摘要：自主機器人團隊在部分已知環境中導航時，當地面機器人遇到被封鎖的道路時，會面臨昂貴的回溯成本，這些封鎖的道路只有在實際通行後才能揭示。我們通過偵查輔助規劃來解決這一問題，這是一種異質規劃框架，其中偵查無人機主動收集環境信息，以改善無人地面車輛的導航。為了將偵查集中在最重要的邊緣上，我們提出了基於信息增益的行動修剪，通過預期對地面機器人行為的影響來評分候選偵查行動。由於精確的基於信息增益的行動修剪計算成本過高，我們開發了一種基於圖神經網絡的模型，該模型直接從圖結構和信念狀態預測信息增益值，將規劃時間減少到實時水平而不犧牲解決方案質量。三種環境類型的實驗顯示，使用基於信息增益的行動修剪的SAP比加拿大旅行者問題基線降低了31.9%到37.7%的地面機器人旅行成本，並且比基於接近度的偵查指導額外提高了8%到14%的性能，證實了有原則的信息增益指導的偵查在現實世界部署中既更有效又計算上可行。

##### **Forecasting Scientific Progress with Artificial Intelligence**
2605.22681v1 by Sean Wu, Pan Lu, Yupeng Chen, Jonathan Bragg, Yutaro Yamada, Peter Clark, David Clifton, Philip Torr, James Zou, Junchi Yu

Artificial intelligence (AI) is increasingly embedded in scientific discovery, yet whether it can anticipate scientific progress remains unclear. To study this question, we introduce a temporally grounded evaluation framework for forecasting scientific progress under controlled knowledge constraints. We present CUSP (Cutoff-conditioned Unseen Scientific Progress), a multi-disciplinary and event-level benchmark that evaluates scientific forecasting in AI systems through feasibility assessment, mechanistic reasoning, generative solution design, and temporal prediction. Across 4,760 scientific events, we observe systematic and domain-dependent limitations in current frontier models. While models can identify plausible research directions from competing candidates, they fail to reliably predict whether scientific advances will be realized and systematically misestimate when they will occur. Performance is highly heterogeneous across domains, with the timing of AI progress more predictable than advances in biology, chemistry, and physics. Performance is largely insensitive to whether events occur before or after the training cutoff, suggesting these limitations cannot be explained solely by knowledge exposure in training data. Under controlled information access, additional pre-cutoff knowledge improves performance but does not close the gap to full-information settings, which becomes more pronounced for high-citation advances. Models also exhibit systematic overconfidence and strong response biases, indicating unreliable uncertainty estimation. Taken together, current AI systems fall short as predictive tools for scientific progress. Access to prior knowledge does not translate into reliable forecasting, and performance benefits more from post-event information than from forward-looking prediction.

摘要：人工智慧（AI）越來越多地嵌入科學發現中，但它是否能預測科學進展仍不清楚。為了研究這個問題，我們引入了一個基於時間的評估框架，用於在受控知識約束下預測科學進展。我們提出了 CUSP（Cutoff-conditioned Unseen Scientific Progress），這是一個跨學科的事件級基準，通過可行性評估、機制推理、生成解決方案設計和時間預測來評估 AI 系統中的科學預測。在 4,760 個科學事件中，我們觀察到當前前沿模型存在系統性和領域依賴的限制。儘管模型可以從競爭候選者中識別出合理的研究方向，但它們無法可靠地預測科學進展是否會實現，並且系統性地錯誤估計其發生時間。不同領域的表現差異很大，AI 進展的時間預測比生物學、化學和物理學的進展更具可預測性。表現在事件發生在訓練截止之前或之後的情況下大體上不敏感，這表明這些限制不能僅僅通過訓練數據中的知識曝光來解釋。在受控信息訪問下，額外的截止前知識提高了表現，但並未縮小與全信息設置之間的差距，這在高引用的進展中變得更加明顯。模型還表現出系統性的過度自信和強烈的反應偏見，顯示出不可靠的不確定性估計。綜合來看，當前的 AI 系統作為預測科學進展的工具仍然不足。獲取先前的知識並未轉化為可靠的預測，並且表現更受事件後信息的影響，而不是來自前瞻性的預測。

##### **Swift Sampling: Selecting Temporal Surprises via Taylor Series**
2605.22678v1 by Dahye Kim, Bhuvan Sachdeva, Karan Uppal, Naman Gupta, Vineeth N. Balasubramanian, Deepti Ghadiyaram

While most frames in long-form video are redundant, the critical information resides in temporal surprises: moments where the actual visual features deviate from their predicted evolution. Inspired by the human brain's predictive coding, we introduce Swift Sampling, an elegant, training-free frame selection algorithm that automatically identifies high-information moments in a video. Specifically, we model a video as a differentiable trajectory in the visual latent space and compute the velocity and acceleration of its features. Then, we apply Taylor expansion to project the expected path of subsequent frames. Frames that diverge sharply from this predicted manifold are identified as temporally surprising frames and selected for sampling. Unlike prior training-free methods that rely on auxiliary networks or video-specific hyperparameter tuning, Swift Sampling is incredibly lightweight, adding only 0.02x additional computational cost over baseline making it 30x cheaper overhead than leading baselines. Across three long-video question answering benchmarks and 10 different downstream tasks, Swift Sampling outperforms uniform sampling and prior query-agnostic baselines. It is especially powerful for long videos with limited frame budgets improving accuracy by up to +12.5 points.

摘要：雖然長格式視頻中的大多數幀是冗餘的，但關鍵信息存在於時間上的驚喜中：實際視覺特徵偏離其預測演變的時刻。受到人類大腦預測編碼的啟發，我們介紹了Swift Sampling，一種優雅的無需訓練的幀選擇算法，能自動識別視頻中的高信息時刻。具體來說，我們將視頻建模為視覺潛在空間中的可微軌跡，並計算其特徵的速度和加速度。然後，我們應用泰勒展開來預測後續幀的預期路徑。與此預測流形明顯偏離的幀被識別為時間上驚訝的幀並被選擇進行取樣。與依賴輔助網絡或視頻特定超參數調整的先前無需訓練的方法不同，Swift Sampling 極其輕量，僅增加0.02倍的計算成本，相較於基準使其開銷便宜30倍。在三個長視頻問答基準和10個不同的下游任務中，Swift Sampling 超越了均勻取樣和先前的查詢無關基準。對於有限幀預算的長視頻，它特別強大，準確率提高了多達+12.5個點。

##### **Self-Policy Distillation via Capability-Selective Subspace Projection**
2605.22675v1 by Guangya Hao, Yitong Shang, Yunbo Long, Zhuokai Zhao, Hanxue Liang

Self-distillation bootstraps large language models (LLMs) by training on their own generations. However, existing methods either rely on external signals to curate self-generated outputs (e.g., correctness filtering, execution feedback, and reward search), which are costly and unavailable for the best-performing frontier models, or skip curation entirely and train on all raw outputs, an approach that is often domain-specific and hard to generalize. Both also share a deeper weakness that self-generated outputs entangle task-relevant capability with others, such as stylistic patterns, formatting artifacts, and model-specific errors, diluting the signal for the specific capability one aims to improve. In this paper, we propose Self-Policy Distillation (SPD), which achieves generalizable, capability selective without any external signal. Specifically, SPD extracts a low-rank capability subspace from the model's own gradients on correctness-defining tokens, projects key-value (KV) activations into this subspace during self-generation, and fine-tunes on the resulting raw outputs with standard next-token prediction loss. Through extensive experiments across code generation, mathematical reasoning, and multiple-choice QA, we show that SPD achieves up to 13% improvement over state-of-the-art self-distillation methods without external signals and up to 16% improvement over pre-trained baselines. Notably, SPD demonstrates superior generalizability, achieving 15% better performance under out-of-domain generalization settings.

摘要：自我蒸餾通過訓練自身生成的輸出來啟動大型語言模型（LLMs）。然而，現有的方法要麼依賴外部信號來策劃自我生成的輸出（例如，正確性過濾、執行反饋和獎勵搜索），這些方法成本高且對於表現最佳的前沿模型來說不可用；要麼完全跳過策劃，訓練所有原始輸出，這種方法通常是特定於領域的，並且難以泛化。兩者還有一個更深層的弱點，即自我生成的輸出將與其他因素（例如風格模式、格式化工件和模型特定錯誤）糾纏在一起，稀釋了旨在改善的特定能力的信號。在本文中，我們提出了自我策略蒸餾（SPD），它在沒有任何外部信號的情況下實現了可泛化的、能力選擇性的方法。具體而言，SPD 從模型在正確性定義標記上的梯度中提取低秩能力子空間，在自我生成過程中將關鍵值（KV）激活投影到該子空間中，並在得到的原始輸上進行標準的下個標記預測損失的微調。通過在代碼生成、數學推理和多選擇問答等領域的廣泛實驗，我們表明 SPD 在沒有外部信號的情況下相對於最先進的自我蒸餾方法實現了高達 13% 的改進，相對於預訓練基準則實現了高達 16% 的改進。值得注意的是，SPD 展示了卓越的可泛化性，在域外泛化設置下實現了 15% 的性能提升。

##### **Is Capability a Liability? More Capable Language Models Make Worse Forecasts When It Matters Most**
2605.22672v1 by Nick Merrill, Jaeho Lee, Ezra Karger

We document inverse scaling in LLMs on forecasting problems whose underlying time series exhibit superlinear growth and tail risk of regime change, a structure common in finance and epidemiology. On these tasks, more capable models produce worse distributional forecasts. The pattern appears on ForecastBench-Sim (FBSim), a contamination-free, simulated-world benchmark we release, in forecasting synthetic SIR epidemics with a matched linear control, and replicates in real-world datasets on COVID-19, measles, housing markets, and hyperinflation. A per-quantile decomposition shows the failure concentrates at the upper tail, which more capable models shift upward to track aggressive extrapolations of growth, while the lower tail stays put. A within-family study of Llama-3.1 shows that both model scale and post-training independently contribute to this effect. Domain knowledge does not reliably rescue calibration. This inverse scaling does not appear on single-threshold metrics common in LLM forecasting benchmarks, reversing the sign of the capability--accuracy relationship on identical outputs. Single-threshold scoring at conventional cutoffs misses the upper-tail cost; tail-inclusive scoring reverses the sign of the capability--accuracy relationship on the same outputs. We recommend that LLM forecasting evaluations use continuous (and unbounded) measures of accuracy alongside bounded binary threshold metrics.

摘要：我們記錄了在預測問題中大型語言模型（LLMs）的逆縮放，這些問題的基礎時間序列顯示出超線性增長和政權變更的尾部風險，這種結構在金融和流行病學中很常見。在這些任務中，更強大的模型產生了更差的分佈預測。這一模式出現在我們發布的無污染模擬世界基準ForecastBench-Sim (FBSim)上，該基準在預測合成SIR流行病時，與匹配的線性控制進行比較，並在COVID-19、麻疹、房地產市場和惡性通貨膨脹的真實世界數據集中得到了重現。每個分位數的分解顯示，失敗集中在上尾，更強大的模型將其向上移動，以追蹤增長的激進外推，而下尾則保持不變。對Llama-3.1的家族內研究顯示，模型規模和後訓練獨立地對這一效應有所貢獻。領域知識並不能可靠地改善校準。在大型語言模型預測基準中，這種逆縮放並未出現在單一閾值指標上，反轉了相同輸出上的能力與準確性之間的關係符號。在傳統的截止點進行的單一閾值評分忽略了上尾成本；包含尾部的評分則反轉了相同輸出上的能力與準確性之間的關係符號。我們建議大型語言模型的預測評估使用連續（且無界）準確性度量，並與有界的二元閾值指標一起使用。

##### **WorkstreamBench: Evaluating LLM Agents on End-to-End Spreadsheet Tasks in Finance**
2605.22664v1 by Thomson Yen, Julian Poeltl, Harshith Srinivas Gear, Yilin Meng, Joshua Fan, Adam Shen, Yili Liu, Ali Bauyrzhan, Siri Du, Haoyang Liu, Daniel Guetta, Hongseok Namkoong

LLM agents are increasingly expected to carry out end-to-end workflows, producing complete artifacts from high-level user instructions. To meet enterprise needs, frontier AI labs have developed agents that can construct entire spreadsheets from scratch. This is especially relevant in finance, where core workflows such as financial modeling, forecasting, and scenario analysis are commonly conducted through spreadsheets. Yet, existing spreadsheet benchmarks do not measure this advanced capability, focusing instead on question-answering or single-formula edits. To address this gap, we provide one of the first evaluations of agents on end-to-end spreadsheet tasks, focusing on economically critical financial workflows such as modeling and scenario analysis. Since deliverables therein are routinely reviewed and revised by multiple stakeholders, judging their quality necessarily involves high-level criteria such as readability or ease of modification. To reflect the multidimensional nature of solution quality, we develop an evaluation taxonomy comprising three dimensions: Accuracy, Formula, and Format, each comprising fine-grained criteria that reflect professional standards. The Claude family leads the benchmark and produces the most professional-looking outputs in our qualitative review, but even the strongest agents frequently fall short of professional finance standards and degrade sharply as the difficulty increases beyond a few chained calculations. This suggests that current agents are not yet able to reliably produce professional-quality spreadsheets at the level of complexity real-world workflows demand.

摘要：LLM 代理人越來越被期望能執行端到端的工作流程，根據高層次的用戶指示生成完整的成果物。為了滿足企業需求，前沿的人工智慧實驗室已開發出能夠從零開始構建整個電子表格的代理人。這在金融領域尤其相關，因為核心工作流程如財務建模、預測和情境分析通常通過電子表格進行。然而，現有的電子表格基準並未衡量這一先進能力，而是專注於問答或單一公式的編輯。為了填補這一空白，我們提供了對代理人在端到端電子表格任務中的首次評估，重點關注經濟上關鍵的財務工作流程，如建模和情境分析。由於其中的交付成果通常會被多個利益相關者審查和修訂，因此評估其質量必然涉及高層次的標準，如可讀性或修改的便利性。為了反映解決方案質量的多維特性，我們開發了一個評估分類法，包含三個維度：準確性、公式和格式，每個維度都包含反映專業標準的細緻標準。Claude 家族在基準測試中領先，並在我們的質性評估中產生最專業的輸出，但即使是最強的代理人也常常未能達到專業金融標準，並且隨著難度超過幾個鏈式計算而急劇下降。這表明目前的代理人尚未能夠可靠地生產出符合現實工作流程需求的專業質量電子表格。

##### **Moral Semantics Survive Machine Translation: Cross-Lingual Evidence from Moral Foundations Corpora**
2605.22660v1 by Maciej Skorski

Moral language is subtle and culturally variable, making it difficult to translate faithfully across languages. Idiomatic expressions, slang, and cultural references introduce hard-to-avoid translation artifacts. Yet automated moral values classification depends on language-specific annotated corpora that exist almost exclusively in English. We investigate whether LLM-based translation can bridge this gap, taking Polish as a test case. Using $\sim$50k morally-annotated social media posts from a diverse range of topics, we apply a principled four-method validation pipeline: LaBSE cross-lingual embedding similarity, Centered Kernel Alignment (CKA), LLM-as-judge evaluation, and deep learning classifier parity tests. We show that despite shortcomings in handling slang, vulgarity, and culturally-loaded expressions, direct translation preserves subtle moral cues well enough to be harvested by cross-lingual machine learning -- with mean cosine similarity of 0.86 and AUC gaps of 0.01--0.02 across all foundations closing further under fine-tuning of language models. These results demonstrate that machine translation is a practical and cost-effective path to moral values research in languages currently under-resourced in this domain. We demonstrate this for Polish as a representative Slavic language, with expected generalisation to related languages.

摘要：道德語言微妙且文化變異，使其在不同語言之間忠實翻譯變得困難。習語、俚語和文化參考引入了難以避免的翻譯瑕疵。然而，自動化的道德價值分類依賴於幾乎僅存在於英語的語言特定標註語料庫。我們調查基於大型語言模型的翻譯是否可以彌補這一差距，以波蘭語作為測試案例。使用約50,000條來自多樣主題的道德標註社交媒體帖子，我們應用了一個原則性的四種方法驗證流程：LaBSE跨語言嵌入相似性、中心核對齊（CKA）、大型語言模型作為評判的評估，以及深度學習分類器的平行測試。我們顯示，儘管在處理俚語、粗俗語言和文化負載表達方面存在不足，直接翻譯仍然能夠很好地保留微妙的道德線索，足以被跨語言機器學習所利用——所有基礎模型的平均餘弦相似度為0.86，AUC差距為0.01至0.02，在語言模型的微調下進一步縮小。這些結果表明，機器翻譯是一條實用且具成本效益的途徑，適用於目前在這一領域資源不足的語言的道德價值研究。我們以波蘭語作為代表性的斯拉夫語言來展示這一點，並預期可推廣至相關語言。

##### **Seeing the Poem: Image-Semantic Detection of AI-Generated Modern Chinese Poetry with MLLMs**
2605.22654v1 by Shanshan Wang, Fengying Ye, Hanjia Lyu, Caiwen Gou, Junchao Wu, Jingming Yao, Chengzhong Xu, Jiebo Luo, Derek F. Wong

Previous detection studies have shown that LLMs cannot be effectively used as detectors, but these studies have not addressed modern Chinese poetry. Moreover, no relevant research has explored the performance of LLMs in detecting modern Chinese poetry. This paper evaluates and enhances the performance of LLMs as detectors for modern Chinese poetry, and proposes an image-semantic guided poetry detection method. Compared with traditional detection approaches, our method innovatively incorporates images that reflect the content of the poetry. Through example-driven approaches, our method effectively integrates information such as meaning, imagery, and feeling from the image, then forms a complementary judgment with the poem text. ##### **Whose Voice Counts? Mapping Stakeholder Perspectives on AI Through Public Submissions to the U.S. Government**
2605.22650v1 by Alina Karakanta, Alex Christiansen, Tomás Dodds, Bissie Anderson, Matteo Fuoli, Marcus Perlman, Aletta G. Dorst

As artificial intelligence (AI) systems become more common in our daily lives, it is important to understand how different stakeholders comprehend and envisage the role that these technologies play in shaping social, political, and economic realities.
