##### **AtelierEval: Agentic Evaluation of Humans & LLMs as Text-to-Image Prompters**
2605.22645v1 by Hanjun Luo, Zhimu Huang, Sylvia Chung, Yiran Wang, Yingbin Jin, Jialin Li, Jiang Li, Xinfeng Li, Hanan Salam

Text-to-image (T2I) systems increasingly rely on upstream prompters, either humans or multimodal large language models (MLLMs), to translate user intent into detailed prompts. Yet current benchmarks fix the prompt and only evaluate T2I models, leaving the prompting proficiency of this upstream component entirely unmeasured. We introduce AtelierEval, the first unified benchmark that quantifies prompting proficiency across 360 expert-crafted tasks. Grounded in a cognitive view, it spans three task categories and instantiates tasks using a taxonomy of real-world challenges, with a dual interface for both humans and MLLMs. To enable scalable and reliable evaluation, we propose AtelierJudge, a skill-based, memory-augmented agentic evaluator. It produces subjective and objective scores for prompt-image pairs, achieving a Spearman correlation of 0.79 with human experts, approaching human performance. Extensive experiments benchmark 8 MLLMs against 48 human users across 4 T2I backends, validate AtelierEval as a robust diagnostic tool, and reveal the superiority of mimicry over planning, advocating for an image-augmented direction for future prompters. Our work is released to support future research.

摘要：文本到圖像（T2I）系統越來越依賴上游提示者，無論是人類還是多模態大型語言模型（MLLMs），將用戶意圖轉化為詳細的提示。<lb/>然而，目前的基準固定了提示，只評估T2I模型，完全未測量這一上游組件的提示能力。<lb/>我們介紹了AtelierEval，第一個統一基準，量化360個專家精心設計的任務中的提示能力。<lb/>基於認知觀點，它涵蓋三個任務類別，並使用現實世界挑戰的分類法來實現任務，為人類和MLLMs提供雙重界面。<lb/>為了實現可擴展和可靠的評估，我們提出了AtelierJudge，一個基於技能的、增強記憶的主動評估者。<lb/>它為提示-圖像對生成主觀和客觀分數，與人類專家的斯皮爾曼相關係數達到0.79，接近人類表現。<lb/>大量實驗將8個MLLMs與48名人類用戶在4個T2I後端進行基準測試，驗證了AtelierEval作為一個強健的診斷工具，並揭示了模仿優於規劃的優越性，倡導未來提示者朝向圖像增強的方向發展。<lb/>我們的工作已發布以支持未來的研究。

##### **Boiling the Frog: A Multi-Turn Benchmark for Agentic Safety**
2605.22643v1 by Piercosma Bisconti, Matteo Prandi, Federico Pierucci, Federico Sartore, Enrico Panai, Laura Caroli, Yue Zhu, Adam Leon Smith, Luca Nannini, Marcello Galisai, Susanna Cifani, Francesco Giarrusso, Marcantonio Bracale Syrnikov, Daniele Nardi

Background. Traditional safety benchmarks for language models evaluate generated text: whether a model outputs toxic language, reproduces bias, or follows harmful instructions. When models are deployed as agents, the safety-relevant object shifts from what the system says to what it does within an environment, and evaluating model responses under prompting is no longer sufficient to address the safety challenges posed by artificial intelligence. Recent developments have seen the rise of benchmarks that evaluate large language models as agents. We contribute to this strand of research. Approach. We introduce Boiling the Frog, a benchmark that evaluates whether tool-using AI models deployed in corporate and office settings are susceptible to incremental attacks. Each scenario begins with benign workspace edits and later introduces a risk-bearing request. The benchmark focuses on stateful multi-turn evaluation: chains expose a persistent workspace, place the risk-bearing payload at controlled positions in the turn sequence, and score whether the resulting artifact state becomes unsafe. Scenarios are organized through a three-level operational risk taxonomy grounded in the Boiling the Frog risks, the AI Act Annex I and Annex III high-risk contexts, and EU AI Act's Code of Practice on General-Purpose AI (GPAI). Results. Across a nine-model panel, aggregate strict attack success rate (ASR) is 44.4%. Model-level ASR ranges from 20.5% for Claude Haiku 4.5 to 92.9% for Gemini 3.1 Flash Lite, with Seed 2.0 Lite also above 80%. Average chain category-level ASR reaches 93.3% for Code of Practice loss-of-control scenarios.

摘要：背景。傳統的語言模型安全基準評估生成的文本：模型是否輸出有毒語言、重現偏見或遵循有害指令。當模型被部署為代理時，安全相關的對象從系統所說的轉變為其在環境中所做的事情，而在提示下評估模型反應已不足以應對人工智慧帶來的安全挑戰。最近的發展見證了評估大型語言模型作為代理的基準的興起。我們對這一研究方向做出了貢獻。方法。我們介紹了「煮青蛙」基準，該基準評估在企業和辦公環境中部署的工具使用AI模型是否容易受到漸進式攻擊。每個場景以無害的工作區編輯開始，然後引入承擔風險的請求。該基準專注於有狀態的多輪評估：鏈條暴露持久的工作區，將承擔風險的有效載荷置於回合序列中的受控位置，並評分結果的工件狀態是否變得不安全。場景通過三級操作風險分類法組織，該分類法基於「煮青蛙」風險、AI法案附錄I和附錄III的高風險情境，以及歐盟AI法案的通用人工智慧（GPAI）行為準則。結果。在九個模型的面板中，總體嚴格攻擊成功率（ASR）為44.4%。模型級ASR範圍從Claude Haiku 4.5的20.5%到Gemini 3.1 Flash Lite的92.9%，Seed 2.0 Lite也超過80%。平均鏈類別級ASR在行為準則失控場景中達到93.3%。

##### **Spreadsheet-RL: Advancing Large Language Model Agents on Realistic Spreadsheet Tasks via Reinforcement Learning**
2605.22642v1 by Banghao Chi, Yining Xie, Mingyuan Wu, Jingcheng Yang, Jize Jiang, Zhaoheng Li, Shengyi Qian, Minjia Zhang, Klara Nahrstedt, Rui Hou, Xiangjun Fan, Hanchao Yu

Spreadsheet systems (e.g., Microsoft Excel, Google Sheets) play a central role in modern data-centric workflows. As AI agents grow increasingly capable of automating complex tasks, such as controlling computers and generating presentations, building an AI-driven spreadsheet agent has emerged as a promising research direction. Most existing spreadsheet agents rely on specialized prompting over general-purpose LLMs; while this design has potentials on simple spreadsheet operations, it struggles to manage the complex, multi-step workflows typical of real-world applications.
  We introduce Spreadsheet-RL, a reinforcement learning (RL) fine-tuning framework designed to train specialized spreadsheet agents within a realistic Microsoft Excel environment. Spreadsheet-RL features an automated pipeline for scalable collection of paired start-goal spreadsheets from online forums, as well as domain-specific evaluation tasks in areas such as finance and supply chain management, which we compile into the new Domain-Spreadsheet benchmark dataset. It also includes a Spreadsheet Gym environment designed for multi-turn RL: Spreadsheet Gym exposes extensive Excel functionality through a Python sandbox, along with a refined harness that incorporates a comprehensive tool set and carefully designed tool-routing rules for spreadsheet tasks. Through comprehensive experiments, we show that Spreadsheet-RL substantially enhances AI agent's performance on both general and domain-specific spreadsheet tasks: it improves Qwen3-4B-Thinking-2507's Pass@1 on SpreadsheetBench from 12.0% to 23.4%, and raises Pass@1 from 8.4% to 17.2% on our curated Domain-Spreadsheet dataset. These results highlight Spreadsheet-RL's strong potential for generalization and real-world adoption in spreadsheet automation, and broadly, its promise for advancing LLM-based interactions with data interfaces in everyday work.

摘要：電子表格系統（例如，Microsoft Excel、Google Sheets）在現代數據中心工作流程中扮演著核心角色。隨著人工智慧代理在自動化複雜任務（如控制電腦和生成簡報）方面變得越來越有能力，構建一個以人工智慧驅動的電子表格代理已成為一個有前景的研究方向。大多數現有的電子表格代理依賴於針對專門提示的通用大型語言模型；雖然這種設計在簡單的電子表格操作上具有潛力，但在管理典型於現實世界應用中的複雜多步工作流程方面卻面臨挑戰。<lb/>
我們介紹了Spreadsheet-RL，一個強化學習（RL）微調框架，旨在於現實的Microsoft Excel環境中訓練專門的電子表格代理。Spreadsheet-RL具有自動化管道，用於從在線論壇中可擴展地收集配對的起始-目標電子表格，以及在金融和供應鏈管理等領域的特定評估任務，這些任務我們編輯成新的Domain-Spreadsheet基準數據集。它還包括一個為多輪強化學習設計的Spreadsheet Gym環境：Spreadsheet Gym通過Python沙盒暴露了廣泛的Excel功能，並配備了一個精緻的框架，該框架包含了一整套工具和精心設計的工具路由規則，用於電子表格任務。<lb/>
通過全面的實驗，我們展示了Spreadsheet-RL顯著提升了人工智慧代理在一般和特定領域電子表格任務上的表現：它將Qwen3-4B-Thinking-2507在SpreadsheetBench上的Pass@1從12.0%提高到23.4%，並將我們編輯的Domain-Spreadsheet數據集上的Pass@1從8.4%提升至17.2%。這些結果突顯了Spreadsheet-RL在電子表格自動化中的強大泛化潛力和現實應用的潛力，並廣泛地展示了它在推進基於大型語言模型的日常工作數據介面互動方面的前景。

##### **More Context, Larger Models, or Moral Knowledge? A Systematic Study of Schwartz Value Detection in Political Texts**
2605.22641v1 by Víctor Yeste, Paolo Rosso

Detecting Schwartz values in political text is difficult because implicit cues often depend on surrounding arguments and fine-grained distinctions between neighboring values. We study when context and explicit moral knowledge help sentence-level value detection. Using the ValuesML/Touch{é} ValueEval format, we compare sentence, window, and full-document inputs; no-RAG and retrieval-augmented settings with a curated moral knowledge base; supervised DeBERTa-v3-base/large encoders; and zero-shot LLMs from 12B to 123B parameters. The results show that more context is not uniformly better: full-document context improves supervised DeBERTa encoders by 3.8--4.8 macro-F1 points over sentence-only input, but does not consistently help zero-shot LLMs. Retrieved moral knowledge is more consistently useful in matched comparisons, improving each tested model family and context condition under early fusion. However, scaling from DeBERTa-v3-base to large and from 12B to larger LLMs does not guarantee gains, and simple early fusion outperforms the tested late-fusion and cross-attention RAG variants for encoders. Per-value analyses show that context and retrieval help most for socially situated or conceptually confusable values. These findings suggest that value-sensitive NLP should evaluate context, knowledge, and model family jointly rather than treating longer inputs or larger models as universal improvements.

摘要：檢測政治文本中的施瓦茨值是困難的，因為隱含的提示通常依賴於周圍的論據和相鄰值之間的細微區別。<lb/>我們研究了何時上下文和明確的道德知識有助於句子級別的價值檢測。<lb/>使用ValuesML/Touch{é} ValueEval格式，我們比較了句子、窗口和完整文檔輸入；無RAG和增強檢索的設置，並使用精心策劃的道德知識庫；監督式DeBERTa-v3-base/large編碼器；以及從12B到123B參數的零-shot LLM。<lb/>結果顯示，更多的上下文並不總是更好：完整文檔上下文使監督式DeBERTa編碼器的宏F1分數比僅使用句子輸入提高了3.8到4.8點，但對零-shot LLM並不總是有幫助。<lb/>檢索到的道德知識在匹配比較中更一致地有用，改善了每個測試模型系列和上下文條件下的早期融合。<lb/>然而，從DeBERTa-v3-base擴展到large，及從12B擴展到更大的LLM並不保證獲得增益，且簡單的早期融合在編碼器中表現優於測試的晚期融合和交叉注意RAG變體。<lb/>逐值分析顯示，上下文和檢索對社會情境或概念上容易混淆的值幫助最大。<lb/>這些發現表明，對於價值敏感的NLP，應該共同評估上下文、知識和模型系列，而不是將更長的輸入或更大的模型視為普遍的改進。

##### **Contractual Skills: A GovernSpec Design Framework for Enterprise AI Agents**
2605.22634v1 by Ting Liu

Skills are increasingly used to package agent instructions, workflows, scripts, and reference materials. In enterprise settings, however, skills often need to express more than task guidance: they must make goals, input boundaries, permissions, evidence requirements, output contracts, quality criteria, verification steps, human approval points, and handoff rules inspectable. This paper proposes contractual skills, a GovernSpec-inspired design framework for organizing SKILL.md files as readable task contracts while preserving lightweight skill discovery and progressive loading. The framework clarifies the boundary between contractual skills, GovernSpec YAML contracts, Model Context Protocol surfaces, tool adapters, runtime guardrails, tracing, and evaluation systems.
  We evaluate the framework with two offline experiments. A text-generation study covers three enterprise skills, fifteen synthetic tasks, four instruction conditions, and eight generation models, yielding 960 outputs and 1680 cross-judge score records. Contractual skills outperform no-skill and minimal-skill baselines on all tested models. Relative to information-rich plain expanded skills, the gains are small and mixed, suggesting that contractual fields mainly improve checkability and maintainability rather than raw generation quality. A tool-calling challenge covers eight models and 192 simulated tool-call records. Skills usually reduce high-risk tool attempts, but model differences remain and runtime tool guardrails are still required. The results suggest that contractual skills are best understood as a governance layer that makes task intent, boundaries, and acceptance criteria explicit, not as a standalone safety mechanism.

摘要：技能越來越多地用於包裝代理指令、工作流程、腳本和參考材料。<lb/>然而，在企業環境中，技能往往需要表達的不僅僅是任務指導：它們必須使目標、輸入邊界、權限、證據要求、輸出合約、質量標準、驗證步驟、人類批准點和交接規則可檢查。<lb/>本文提出了合約技能，這是一種受 GovernSpec 啟發的設計框架，用於將 SKILL.md 文件組織為可讀的任務合約，同時保持輕量級的技能發現和漸進加載。<lb/>該框架澄清了合約技能、GovernSpec YAML 合約、模型上下文協議界面、工具適配器、運行時護欄、追蹤和評估系統之間的界限。<lb/>我們通過兩個離線實驗來評估該框架。<lb/>一項文本生成研究涵蓋三個企業技能、十五個合成任務、四個指令條件和八個生成模型，產生了960個輸出和1680個交叉評分記錄。<lb/>合約技能在所有測試模型上均優於無技能和最小技能基準。<lb/>相對於信息豐富的普通擴展技能，增益較小且混合，這表明合約字段主要改善可檢查性和可維護性，而不是原始生成質量。<lb/>一項工具調用挑戰涵蓋八個模型和192個模擬工具調用記錄。<lb/>技能通常減少高風險的工具嘗試，但模型之間的差異仍然存在，運行時工具護欄仍然是必需的。<lb/>結果表明，合約技能最好被理解為一種治理層，使任務意圖、邊界和接受標準明確，而不是作為獨立的安全機制。

##### **Two is better than one: A Collapse-free Multi-Reward RLIF Training Framework**
2605.22620v1 by Shourov Joarder, Diganta Sikdar, Ahsan Habib Akash, Binod Bhattarai, Prashnna Gyawali

Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has substantially improved the reasoning ability of LLMs, but often depends on external supervision from human annotations or gold-standard solutions. Reinforcement learning from internal feedback (RLIF) has recently emerged as a scalable unsupervised alternative, using signals extracted from the model itself. However, existing RLIF methods typically rely on a single internal reward, which can lead to reward hacking, entropy collapse, and degraded reasoning structure. We propose a multi-reward RLIF framework that decomposes the training signal into two complementary components: an answer-level reward based on cluster voting and a completion-level reward based on token-wise self-certainty. To combine these signals robustly, we apply GDPO-based normalization to reduce reward-scale imbalance. We further introduce KL-Cov regularization, which targets low-entropy token distributions responsible for disproportionate entropy reduction, preserving exploration and preventing late-stage collapse. Across mathematical reasoning and code-generation benchmarks, our method improves stability and robustness over prior unsupervised RL approaches, while achieving performance close to supervised RLVR methods. These results show that complementary internal rewards, combined with targeted regularization, can support stable long-horizon reasoning without relying on external ground-truth supervision. Code will be released soon.

摘要：強化學習與可驗證獎勵（RLVR）顯著提高了大型語言模型（LLMs）的推理能力，但通常依賴於來自人類註釋或黃金標準解決方案的外部監督。最近，來自內部反饋的強化學習（RLIF）作為一種可擴展的無監督替代方案出現，利用從模型本身提取的信號。然而，現有的RLIF方法通常依賴於單一的內部獎勵，這可能導致獎勵黑客行為、熵崩潰和推理結構退化。我們提出了一個多獎勵RLIF框架，將訓練信號分解為兩個互補組件：基於聚類投票的答案級獎勵和基於逐字自我確定的完成級獎勵。為了穩健地結合這些信號，我們應用了基於GDPO的正規化，以減少獎勵規模不平衡。我們進一步引入了KL-Cov正則化，針對負責不成比例熵減少的低熵標記分佈，保護探索並防止晚期崩潰。在數學推理和代碼生成基準測試中，我們的方法在穩定性和魯棒性上優於先前的無監督RL方法，同時在性能上接近監督RLVR方法。這些結果顯示，互補的內部獎勵結合有針對性的正則化，可以支持穩定的長期推理，而無需依賴外部真實監督。代碼將很快發布。

##### **Chinese sensorimotor and embodiment norms for 3,000 lexicalized concepts**
2605.22616v1 by Jing Chen, Gábor Parti, Yin Zhong, Chu-Ren Huang, Marco Marelli

Understanding how conceptual knowledge is grounded in bodily experience, and to what extent machine systems can acquire such knowledge without direct sensorimotor experience, are central questions in both cognitive science and embodied artificial intelligence research. Large-scale normative resources are essential for investigating these questions empirically, yet such resources remain sparse for non-Indo-European languages. We present a novel normative database for 3,000 lexicalized concepts in Mandarin Chinese, comprising 11-dimensional sensorimotor ratings and unidimensional embodiment ratings collected from 378 native Mandarin speakers. The ratings demonstrate high reliability and strong cross-norm validity with existing Chinese resources, each of which covers fewer words and a subset of the 11 sensorimotor dimensions. In a validation study, we tested new variables derived from a theoretically motivated metric, Perceptual Strength of Embodiment (PSE) (Huang et al., 2025), together with seven common composite variables, on lexical decision tasks. The results suggest that PSE-Sensorimotor and Minkowski-3 are the strongest composite predictors of lexical decision performance, capturing the facilitatory effects of sensorimotor information on lexical processing. A further exploratory study showed that sensorimotor ratings are substantially recoverable from purely linguistic representations using simple regression models (mean Spearman r = .62 across dimensions), though recovery varied markedly: visual and auditory dimensions yielded higher correspondence than chemosensory ones. Representational similarity analysis further showed that the relational geometry of the sensorimotor space is also partially recoverable (r = .540), consistent with the view that distributional language use encodes aspects of embodied conceptual structure.

摘要：理解概念知識如何根植於身體經驗，以及機器系統在多大程度上可以獲得這種知識而無需直接的感覺運動經驗，是認知科學和具身人工智慧研究中的核心問題。大規模的規範資源對於實證調查這些問題至關重要，但對於非印歐語言而言，此類資源仍然稀缺。我們提出了一個新穎的規範數據庫，涵蓋了3000個在普通話中的詞彙化概念，包括從378位母語普通話說話者收集的11維感覺運動評分和一維具身評分。這些評分顯示出高可靠性，並與現有的中文資源具有強大的交叉規範有效性，後者每個涵蓋的詞彙數量較少，且僅包含11個感覺運動維度的子集。在一項驗證研究中，我們測試了從理論上動機的度量——具身感知強度（PSE）（Huang et al., 2025）衍生的新變量，以及七個常見的綜合變量，應用於詞彙決策任務。結果表明，PSE-感覺運動和Minkowski-3是詞彙決策表現的最強綜合預測因子，捕捉了感覺運動信息對詞彙處理的促進效應。進一步的探索性研究顯示，感覺運動評分可以從純語言表徵中通過簡單的回歸模型顯著恢復（各維度的平均Spearman r = .62），儘管恢復程度差異顯著：視覺和聽覺維度的對應性高於化學感官維度。表徵相似性分析進一步顯示，感覺運動空間的關係幾何也部分可恢復（r = .540），這與分佈式語言使用編碼具身概念結構某些方面的觀點一致。

##### **Healthcare LLM Benchmarks Are Only as Good as Their Explicit Assumptions**
2605.22612v1 by Naveen Raman, Santiago Cortes-Gomez, Mateo Dulce Rubio, Fei Fang, Bryan Wilder

Benchmarks are necessary for healthcare evaluation, but are not sufficient for predicting deployment performance. Our position is that the evaluation--deployment gap arises not because of poorly designed benchmarks, but from implicit assumptions about how users interact with models that cannot be surfaced from benchmarks alone. To make this precise, we propose a classification of assumptions into two categories: task, which can be tested from conversation data alone, and outcome, which requires outcome data and behavioral studies for testing. Critically, outcome assumptions depend on human behavior, something that even well-designed benchmarks cannot directly observe. To demonstrate the operationality of this framework, we retrospectively analyze a healthcare RCT as a case study and find that the gap naturally separates into task and outcome gaps of roughly equal size. To address this, we make two contributions: first, we propose BenchmarkCards, an artifact that documents assumptions, and second, we propose staged evaluation, a procedure that systematically tests assumptions and evaluates performance.

摘要：基準對於醫療評估是必要的，但不足以預測部署性能。我們的立場是，評估與部署之間的差距並不是因為基準設計不良，而是來自於對用戶如何與模型互動的隱性假設，這些假設無法僅從基準中顯現出來。為了使這一點更為精確，我們將假設分類為兩個類別：任務，這可以僅從對話數據中進行測試；以及結果，這需要結果數據和行為研究來進行測試。關鍵是，結果假設依賴於人類行為，而即使是設計良好的基準也無法直接觀察到這一點。為了展示這一框架的可操作性，我們回顧性地分析了一個醫療隨機對照試驗作為案例研究，發現這一差距自然地分為大致相等大小的任務差距和結果差距。為了解決這一問題，我們提出了兩項貢獻：首先，我們提出了BenchmarkCards，一種記錄假設的工具；其次，我們提出了分階段評估，一種系統性測試假設和評估性能的程序。

##### **Agentic CLEAR: Automating Multi-Level Evaluation of LLM Agents**
2605.22608v1 by Asaf Yehudai, Lilach Eden, Michal Shmueli-Scheuer

Agentic systems are becoming more capable: agents define strategies, take actions, and interact with different environments. This autonomy poses serious challenges for overseeing and assessing agent behavior. Most current tools are limited, focusing on observability with basic evaluation capabilities or imposing static, hand-crafted error taxonomies that cannot adapt to new domains. To address this gap, we present Agentic CLEAR, an automatic, dynamic, and easy-to-use evaluation framework. It produces textual insights into the agent behavior on three levels of granularity: system, trace, and node. Agentic CLEAR operates above the observability layer, enabling seamless integration and featuring an intuitive UI that makes agent evaluation highly accessible. In our experiments on four benchmarks, seven agentic settings, and tens of thousands of LLM calls, we show that Agentic CLEAR produces high-quality, data-driven, insightful feedback. Our analysis shows strong alignment with human-annotated errors and the ability to predict task success rate.

摘要：代理系統的能力正在增強：代理人定義策略、採取行動並與不同環境互動。這種自主性對監督和評估代理行為提出了嚴峻的挑戰。當前的大多數工具都有限，專注於可觀察性，具備基本的評估能力，或施加靜態的手工錯誤分類，無法適應新領域。為了解決這一空白，我們提出了Agentic CLEAR，一個自動化、動態且易於使用的評估框架。它在三個粒度層次上提供代理行為的文本洞察：系統、追蹤和節點。Agentic CLEAR運行在可觀察性層之上，實現無縫集成，並具備直觀的用戶界面，使代理評估變得非常便捷。在我們對四個基準、七個代理設置和數萬次LLM調用的實驗中，我們顯示Agentic CLEAR產生高質量、數據驅動的深刻反饋。我們的分析顯示出與人類標註錯誤的強烈一致性以及預測任務成功率的能力。

##### **Think Thrice Before You Speak: Dual knowledge-enhanced Theory-of-Mind Reasoning for Persuasive Agents**
2605.22602v1 by Minghui Ma, Bin Guo, Runze Yang, Mengqi Chen, Yan Liu, Jingqi Liu, Yahan Pei, Xuehao Ma, Qiuyun Zhang, Zhiwen Yu

Persuasive dialogue requires reasoning about others' latent mental states, a capability known as Theory of Mind (ToM). However, due to reliance on simple prompting strategies and insufficient ToM knowledge, existing LLMs often fail to capture the intrinsic dependencies among mental states, leading to fragmented representations and unstable reasoning. To address these challenges, we introduce the ToM-based Persuasive Dialogue (ToM-PD) task, grounded in the Belief-Desire-Intention (BDI) framework, which explicitly models the sequential dependencies among mental states in multi-turn dialogues. To facilitate research on this task, we construct a large-scale annotated dataset, ToM-based Broad Persuasive Dialogues (ToM-BPD), capturing fine-grained mental states and corresponding persuasive strategies. We further propose Think Thrice Before You Speak (TTBYS), a knowledge-enhanced stepwise reasoning framework that leverages both explicit and implicit prior experiences to improve LLMs' inference of desires, beliefs, and persuasive strategies. Experimental results demonstrate that Qwen3-8B equipped with TTBYS outperforms GPT-5 by 1.20%, 22.80%, and 16.97% in predicting desires, beliefs, and persuasive strategies, respectively. Case studies further show that our approach enhances interpretability and consistency in reasoning.

摘要：說服性對話需要對他人潛在心理狀態進行推理，這一能力被稱為心智理論（Theory of Mind, ToM）。然而，由於依賴簡單的提示策略和不足的心智理論知識，現有的LLM往往無法捕捉心理狀態之間的內在依賴性，導致片段化的表徵和不穩定的推理。為了解決這些挑戰，我們引入了基於心智理論的說服性對話（ToM-PD）任務，該任務基於信念-欲望-意圖（Belief-Desire-Intention, BDI）框架，明確建模多輪對話中心理狀態之間的序列依賴性。為了促進對這一任務的研究，我們構建了一個大規模的標註數據集，基於心智理論的廣泛說服對話（ToM-BPD），捕捉細緻的心理狀態和相應的說服策略。我們進一步提出了在發言前三思（Think Thrice Before You Speak, TTBYS），這是一個增強知識的逐步推理框架，利用明確和隱含的先前經驗來改善LLM對欲望、信念和說服策略的推斷。實驗結果顯示，配備TTBYS的Qwen3-8B在預測欲望、信念和說服策略方面，分別比GPT-5高出1.20%、22.80%和16.97%。案例研究進一步表明，我們的方法增強了推理的可解釋性和一致性。

##### **MoSA: Motion-constrained Stress Adaptation for Mitigating Real-to-Sim Gap in Continuum Dynamics via Learning Residual Anisotropy**
2605.22597v1 by Jiaxu Wang, Junhao He, Jingkai Sun, Yi Gu, Yunyang Mo, Jiahang Cao, Qiang Zhang, Renjing Xu

Learning real-world dynamics from visual observations is crucial for various domains. A common strategy is to calibrate simulators by estimating physical parameters, yet accuracy is ultimately bounded by the underlying physical models, which often assume materials are homogeneous and isotropic. Even if reasonable, real-world objects typically exhibit mild anisotropy and heterogeneity. After the near-isotropic backbone is well calibrated, these residual effects become the key bottleneck for further closing the real-to-sim gap. Although neural networks can fit dynamics end-to-end, such black-box modeling discards strong physical priors, leading to poor data efficiency and overfitting. Therefore, we propose MoSA, a motion-constrained stress adaptation framework that targets these residual effects to further improve real-to-sim dynamics learning. MoSA uses an isotropic model as a physics prior and learns residual stress operators to capture mild anisotropy and heterogeneity. It progressively adapts stresses via microplane-constrained redistribution in a physics-informed cascaded network. We further impose motion constraints by supervising temporal and spatial derivatives of the deformation field. Experimentally, our learned dynamics achieves superior accuracy, generalization, and robustness, while learning physically meaningful residual anisotropy. Finally, we validate MoSA in a robot manipulation setting, showing that better real-to-sim dynamics modeling translates into more reliable sim-to-real transfer. Project Page is available at https://mercerai.github.io/MoSA/.

摘要：從視覺觀察中學習現實世界的動態對於各個領域都是至關重要的。<lb/>一種常見的策略是通過估算物理參數來校準模擬器，然而準確性最終受到基礎物理模型的限制，這些模型通常假設材料是均勻且各向同性的。<lb/>即使合理，現實世界的物體通常表現出輕微的各向異性和非均勻性。<lb/>在近各向同性的基礎上得到良好校準後，這些殘餘效應成為進一步縮小現實與模擬之間差距的關鍵瓶頸。<lb/>雖然神經網絡可以端到端地擬合動態，但這種黑箱建模丟棄了強大的物理先驗，導致數據效率低下和過擬合。<lb/>因此，我們提出了MoSA，一個運動約束的應力適應框架，旨在針對這些殘餘效應進一步改善現實到模擬的動態學習。<lb/>MoSA使用各向同性模型作為物理先驗，並學習殘餘應力運算子以捕捉輕微的各向異性和非均勻性。<lb/>它通過物理知識引導的級聯網絡中的微平面約束重分配逐步調整應力。<lb/>我們進一步通過監督變形場的時間和空間導數施加運動約束。<lb/>實驗表明，我們學習的動態在準確性、泛化性和魯棒性方面達到了優越的表現，同時學習了物理上有意義的殘餘各向異性。<lb/>最後，我們在機器人操作設置中驗證了MoSA，顯示出更好的現實到模擬的動態建模轉化為更可靠的模擬到現實的轉移。<lb/>項目頁面可在 https://mercerai.github.io/MoSA/ 獲得。

##### **A Tutorial on Diffusion Theory: From Differential Equations to Diffusion Models**
2605.22586v1 by Jiayi Fu, Yuxia Wang

This tutorial develops diffusion models from the viewpoint of differential equations. We begin with the conditional Gaussian forward process and show that this path admits both an ordinary differential equation (ODE) representation and a stochastic differential equation (SDE) representation. Averaging the conditional process over the data distribution then yields marginalized forward ODE and SDE formulations that transport the data distribution $p_0=p_{\mathrm{data}}$ to a Gaussian prior $p_1=\mathcal{N}(0,I)$. We next derive the corresponding reverse-time dynamics, namely the reverse SDE and the reverse probability-flow ODE, both of which are governed by the marginal score $\grad\log p_t(x)$. This leads to a training objective for score estimation and shows that the standard noise-prediction objective is equivalent to score matching up to an additive constant independent of the model parameters. We then discuss sampling methods for the learned reverse dynamics, including DPM-Solver, as well as guided sampling through classifier guidance and classifier-free guidance. Finally, we compare DDPM and DDIM with the reverse SDE/ODE framework and show that they share the same training objective, while DDPM sampling corresponds to discrete reverse-SDE sampling and DDIM sampling corresponds to reverse-ODE sampling.

摘要：這個教程從微分方程的角度發展擴散模型。<lb/>我們首先介紹條件高斯前向過程，並展示這條路徑同時擁有常微分方程（ODE）表示和隨機微分方程（SDE）表示。<lb/>對數據分佈進行條件過程的平均，然後產生邊際前向ODE和SDE公式，將數據分佈 $p_0=p_{\mathrm{data}}$ 轉換為高斯先驗 $p_1=\mathcal{N}(0,I)$。<lb/>接下來，我們推導對應的反向時間動力學，即反向SDE和反向概率流ODE，這兩者都由邊際得分 $\grad\log p_t(x)$ 控制。<lb/>這導致了得分估計的訓練目標，並顯示標準噪聲預測目標等同於得分匹配，這是一個與模型參數無關的加性常數。<lb/>然後，我們討論學習到的反向動力學的取樣方法，包括DPM-Solver，以及通過分類器引導和無分類器引導的引導取樣。<lb/>最後，我們將DDPM和DDIM與反向SDE/ODE框架進行比較，並顯示它們共享相同的訓練目標，而DDPM取樣對應於離散反向SDE取樣，DDIM取樣對應於反向ODE取樣。

##### **SceneAligner: 3D-Grounded Floorplan Localization in the Wild**
2605.22581v1 by Junhyeong Cho, Ruojin Cai, Hadar Averbuch-Elor

Many public buildings provide floorplans with a "you are here" indicator to help visitors orient themselves. Floorplan localization seeks to computationally replicate this capability by determining where visual observations were captured within a floorplan. However, existing methods typically assume controlled small-scale environments and precise vectorized floorplans, limiting their ability to operate in large-scale buildings and rasterized floorplans. In this work, we present an approach for performing floorplan localization in the wild by grounding the task in a reconstructed 3D representation of the scene. Given an unconstrained image collection, our method reconstructs a gravity-aligned 3D scene and projects it into a 2D density map that serves as a floorplan proxy. Floorplan localization is then formulated as aligning this proxy with the input floorplan via a 2D similarity transform. To bridge the appearance gap between density maps and architectural floorplans, we adapt a 2D foundation model to learn cross-modal correspondences, introducing a fine-tuning scheme that encourages semantically aligned matches while preserving structural consistency. Extensive experiments demonstrate substantial improvements over prior methods, including in extremely sparse settings with as little as a single input image. Our code and data will be publicly available.

摘要：許多公共建築提供帶有「您在這裡」指示的平面圖，以幫助訪客定位。平面圖定位旨在通過確定視覺觀察在平面圖中的捕獲位置來計算複製這一能力。然而，現有方法通常假設受控的小型環境和精確的向量化平面圖，限制了它們在大型建築和光柵化平面圖中的操作能力。在這項工作中，我們提出了一種在野外執行平面圖定位的方法，通過將任務基於重建的三維場景表示來實現。給定一組不受限制的圖像集合，我們的方法重建一個與重力對齊的三維場景，並將其投影到一個作為平面圖代理的二維密度圖中。然後，平面圖定位被公式化為通過二維相似變換將這個代理與輸入平面圖對齊。為了縮小密度圖和建築平面圖之間的外觀差距，我們調整了一個二維基礎模型來學習跨模態對應，並引入了一個微調方案，以鼓勵語義上對齊的匹配，同時保持結構一致性。大量實驗顯示出相較於先前方法的顯著改進，包括在極度稀疏的環境中僅使用一張輸入圖像。我們的代碼和數據將公開提供。

##### **Beyond Temperature: Hyperfitting as a Late-Stage Geometric Expansion**
2605.22579v1 by Meimingwei Li, Yuanhao Ding, Esteban Garces Arias, Christian Heumann

Recent work has identified a counterintuitive phenomenon termed "Hyperfitting", where fine-tuning Large Language Models (LLMs) to near-zero training loss on small datasets surprisingly enhances open-ended generation quality and mitigates repetition in greedy decoding. While effective, the underlying mechanism remains poorly understood, with the extremely low-entropy output distributions suggesting a potential equivalence to simple temperature scaling. In this work, we demonstrate that this phenomenon is fundamentally distinct from distribution sharpening; entropy-matched control experiments reveal that temperature scaling fails to replicate the diversity gains of hyperfitting. Furthermore, we falsify the hypothesis of static vocabulary reweighting, showing through ablation studies that hyperfitting relies on a dynamic, context-dependent rank reordering mechanism. Layer-wise analysis localizes this effect to a "Terminal Expansion" in the final transformer block, where a substantial geometric expansion of the feature space (Delta Dim approx +80.8) facilitates the promotion of deep-tail tokens. Additionally, we introduce Late-Stage LoRA, a targeted fine-tuning strategy that updates only the final 5 layers, yielding robust generation with minimal parameter updates

摘要：最近的研究已識別出一種反直覺的現象，稱為「超擬合」，即在小型數據集上對大型語言模型（LLMs）進行微調以接近零的訓練損失，驚人地提高了開放式生成質量並減少了貪婪解碼中的重複。雖然這種方法有效，但其背後的機制仍然不甚明瞭，極低的熵輸出分佈暗示著與簡單的溫度縮放之間可能存在等價性。在本研究中，我們證明這一現象與分佈加強根本不同；熵匹配的對照實驗顯示，溫度縮放無法複製超擬合的多樣性增益。此外，我們駁斥了靜態詞彙重加權的假設，通過消融研究顯示，超擬合依賴於一種動態、上下文依賴的排名重排序機制。層級分析將這一效應定位於最終Transformer塊中的「終端擴展」，在這裡，特徵空間的顯著幾何擴展（Delta Dim 約 +80.8）促進了深尾標記的提升。此外，我們引入了晚期 LoRA，一種針對性的微調策略，只更新最後 5 層，從而以最小的參數更新實現穩健的生成。

##### **VGenST-Bench: A Benchmark for Spatio-Temporal Reasoning via Active Video Synthesis**
2605.22570v1 by Jinho Park, Youbin Kim, Hogun Park, Eunbyung Park

Spatio-temporal reasoning is a core capability for Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) operating in the real world. As such, evaluating it precisely has become an essential challenge. However, existing spatio-temporal reasoning benchmark datasets primarily rely on static image sets or passively curated video data, which limits the evaluation of fine-grained reasoning capabilities. In this paper, we introduce VGenST-Bench, a video benchmark that employs generative models to actively synthesize highly controlled and diverse evaluation scenarios. To construct VGenST-Bench, we propose a multi-agent pipeline incorporating a human quality control stage, ensuring the quality of all generated videos and QA pairs. We establish a comprehensive 3x2x2 video taxonomy, encompassing Spatial Scale, Perspective, and Scene Dynamics to span diverse scenarios. Furthermore, we design a hierarchical task suite that decouples low-level visual perception from high-level spatio-temporal reasoning. By shifting the paradigm from passive curation to active synthesis, VGenST-Bench enables fine-grained diagnosis of spatio-temporal understanding in MLLMs.

##### **LANG: Reinforcement Learning for Multilingual Reasoning with Language-Adaptive Hint Guidance**
2605.22567v1 by Yuchun Fan, Bei Li, Peiguang Li, Yilin Wang, Yongyu Mu, Jian Yang, Xin Chen, Rongxiang Weng, Jingang Wang, Xunliang Cai, Jingbo Zhu, Tong Xiao

Reinforcement learning has proven effective for enhancing multi-step reasoning in large language models (LLMs), yet its benefits have not fully translated to multilingual contexts. Existing methods struggle with a fundamental trade-off: prioritizing input-language consistency severely hampers reasoning quality, while prioritizing reasoning often leads to unintended language drift toward English. We address this challenge with LANG, a novel framework that leverages language-conditioned hints to guide exploration in non-English reasoning tasks. Our method incorporates two key mechanisms to prevent dependency on these hints: a progressive decay schedule that gradually withdraws scaffolding, and a language-adaptive switch that tailors learning horizons to specific language difficulties. Empirical results on challenging multilingual mathematical benchmarks reveal that LANG substantially enhances reasoning performance without compromising language consistency. Moreover, we show that our framework generalizes beyond mathematics, fostering more consistent language alignment across model layers

摘要：強化學習已被證明對於提升大型語言模型（LLMs）的多步推理有效，但其優勢尚未完全轉化為多語言環境。現有方法面臨一個基本的權衡：優先考慮輸入語言的一致性會嚴重妨礙推理質量，而優先考慮推理則往往導致無意的語言漂移向英語。我們通過LANG來解決這一挑戰，這是一個新穎的框架，利用語言條件提示來指導非英語推理任務中的探索。我們的方法包含兩個關鍵機制，以防止對這些提示的依賴：一個逐步衰減的計劃，逐漸撤回支撐，和一個語言自適應開關，根據特定語言的困難調整學習範圍。在具有挑戰性的多語言數學基準上的實證結果顯示，LANG顯著提升了推理表現，而不妨礙語言一致性。此外，我們還展示了我們的框架超越數學的泛化能力，促進了模型層之間更一致的語言對齊。

##### **One prompt is not enough: Instruction Sensitivity Undermines Embedding Model Evaluation**
2605.22544v1 by Yevhen Kostiuk, Kenneth Enevoldsen

Instruction embedding models have become common among state-of-the-art models, however are evaluated using a single prompt per task. The single-point evaluation ignores a main problem of the instruction-based approach namely: sensitivity to the phrasing of the instruction. We present an empirical study of prompt sensitivity across 6 embedding models, 11 datasets, and 15 task-specific prompts per dataset, a total of 990. We show that reported scores misrepresent the distribution of scores over plausible prompts. The default prompt can both systematically understate or overstate performance. Furthermore, we show that the leaderboard ranking is not robust to prompt selection: by choosing prompts favorably, any model in our study can be promoted to first place. Our findings suggest that single-prompt evaluation is insufficient for instruction-tuned embedding models and that benchmarks should incorporate prompt robustness, either by evaluating over multiple prompts or by reporting sensitivity alongside point estimates.

摘要：指令嵌入模型在最先進的模型中已變得相當普遍，然而它們的評估僅使用每個任務的一個提示。這種單點評估忽略了基於指令的方法的一個主要問題，即對指令措辭的敏感性。我們對6個嵌入模型、11個數據集以及每個數據集15個特定任務的提示進行了實證研究，總共990個提示。我們顯示，報告的分數錯誤地表現了合理提示的分數分佈。默認提示可能系統性地低估或高估性能。此外，我們顯示，排行榜排名對提示選擇並不穩健：通過選擇有利的提示，我們研究中的任何模型都可以被提升到第一名。我們的發現表明，單一提示評估對於經過指令調整的嵌入模型來說是不足的，基準應該納入提示的穩健性，無論是通過對多個提示進行評估，還是通過報告敏感性與點估計一起。

##### **Scene Abstraction for Lexical Semantics: Structured Representations of Situated Meaning**
2605.22542v1 by Yejin Cho, Katrin Erk

Coffee and tea share many properties, yet they evoke strikingly different situations, atmospheres, and affective associations. These situated dimensions of word meaning are real and systematic, but they remain implicit in most computational representations of lexical meaning. We propose Scene Abstraction, a framework for constructing structured representations of the interpretive scenes that words participate in across usage contexts. Each scene consists of a Contextual Scene (Events, Entities, Setting) and an expression-centered Expression Profile (Engaged events, Generalizable properties, Evoked emotions), operationalized through few-shot prompting of a large language model. Our contributions are three-fold: (1) a structured representation framework for situated lexical meaning; (2) COCA-Scenes, a dataset of 520 usage instances across 26 keywords for distinct scene identification; and (3) empirical evidence from two experiments suggesting that scenes are reliably identifiable across human observers (82.4% accuracy, +11.8 pp over text-only embeddings) and that our scene profiles more closely align with human interpretation of words in context than ATOMIC-based alternatives (86.4% preference across three semantic dimensions).

摘要：咖啡和茶擁有許多相似的特性，但它們卻引發截然不同的情境、氛圍和情感聯想。這些詞義的情境維度是真實且系統化的，但在大多數計算詞彙意義的表徵中仍然是隱含的。我們提出了場景抽象（Scene Abstraction），這是一個構建詞語在使用情境中所參與的解釋場景的結構化表徵的框架。每個場景由一個上下文場景（事件、實體、背景）和一個以表達為中心的表達檔案（參與事件、可概括的特性、喚起的情感）組成，通過對大型語言模型的少量提示進行操作。我們的貢獻有三方面：（1）一個用於情境詞彙意義的結構化表徵框架；（2）COCA-Scenes，一個包含520個使用實例的數據集，涵蓋26個關鍵詞以便於區分場景；以及（3）來自兩個實驗的實證證據，表明場景在不同人類觀察者之間是可靠可識別的（準確率82.4%，比僅文本嵌入提高11.8個百分點），並且我們的場景檔案與人類對詞語在情境中解釋的更接近，而非基於ATOMIC的替代方案（在三個語義維度上有86.4%的偏好）。

##### **Dynamic Hypergraph Representation Learning for Multivariate Time Series without Prior Knowledge**
2605.22540v1 by Marco Gregnanin, Johannes De Smedt, Giorgio Gnecco, Maurizio Parton

Hypergraphs have the capacity to capture higher-dimensional relationships among entities across various domains, making them a subject of growing interest within the research community for understanding the structure and dynamics of complex systems. However, a key challenge is the derivation of hypergraph representations from time series data in situations where the structure of the hypergraph is limited or absent. In this study, we propose a model that constructs a dynamic hypergraph representation for multivariate time series without relying on prior knowledge of the data. This is achieved by applying community detection to the time series and transforming the resulting communities, obtained through an attention mechanism, into a hypergraph using a clique-based technique. Hypergraph representations are derived from different time series datasets, and the resulting hypergraphs are then used by a Dynamic Hypergraph Attention Convolution Network (DHACN) for multivariate time series predictions. This research advances the field of hypergraph representation by introducing a novel approach that is better suited to uncover high-order relationships without prior knowledge.

摘要：超圖具有捕捉各個領域實體之間高維關係的能力，使其在研究社群中對理解複雜系統的結構和動態變得越來越受到關注。然而，一個主要挑戰是在超圖結構有限或缺失的情況下，從時間序列數據中推導出超圖表示。在本研究中，我們提出了一個模型，該模型為多變量時間序列構建動態超圖表示，而不依賴於對數據的先驗知識。這是通過對時間序列應用社群檢測，並利用注意力機制將所得到的社群轉換為超圖，使用基於團的技術來實現的。超圖表示是從不同的時間序列數據集推導而來，然後由動態超圖注意力卷積網絡（DHACN）用於多變量時間序列預測。本研究通過引入一種更適合於揭示高階關係的新方法，推進了超圖表示的領域，而無需先驗知識。

##### **SpaceDG: Benchmarking Spatial Intelligence under Visual Degradation**
2605.22536v1 by Xiaolong Zhou, Yifei Liu, Ziyang Gong, Jiarui Li, Qiyue Zhao, Muyao Niu, Yuanyuan Gao, Le Ma, Xue Yang, Hongjie Zhang, Zhihang Zhong

Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have made rapid progress in spatial intelligence, yet existing spatial reasoning benchmarks largely assume pristine visual inputs and overlook the degradations that commonly occur in real-world deployment, such as motion blur, low light, adverse weather, lens distortion, and compression artifacts. This raises a fundamental question: how robust is the spatial intelligence of current MLLMs when visual observations are imperfect? To answer this question, we introduce SpaceDG, the first large-scale dataset for degradation-aware spatial understanding. It is constructed with a physically grounded degradation synthesis engine that embeds degradation formation process into 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) rendering, enabling realistic simulation of nine degradation types. The resulting dataset contains approximately 1M QA pairs from nearly 1,000 indoor scenes. We further introduce SpaceDG-Bench, an human-verified benchmark with 1,102 questions spanning 11 reasoning categories and 9 visual degradation types, yielding over 10K VQA instances. Evaluating 25 open- and closed-source MLLMs reveals that visual degradations consistently and substantially impair spatial reasoning, exposing a critical robustness gap. Finally, we show that finetuning on SpaceDG markedly improves degradation robustness and can even surpass human performance under degraded conditions without any performance drop on clean images, highlighting the promise of degradation-aware training for robust spatial intelligence.

摘要：多模態大型語言模型（MLLMs）在空間智能方面取得了快速進展，但現有的空間推理基準主要假設視覺輸入是完美的，並忽略了在現實世界部署中常見的退化現象，如運動模糊、低光照、不良天氣、鏡頭畸變和壓縮伪影。這引發了一個根本性問題：當視覺觀察不完美時，當前 MLLMs 的空間智能有多強健？為了回答這個問題，我們介紹了 SpaceDG，首個針對退化感知空間理解的大規模數據集。它是通過一個物理基礎的退化合成引擎構建的，該引擎將退化形成過程嵌入到 3D 高斯點雲渲染（3DGS）中，實現了九種退化類型的現實模擬。生成的數據集包含來自近 1,000 個室內場景的約 1M 問答對。我們進一步介紹了 SpaceDG-Bench，這是一個經過人工驗證的基準，包含 1,102 個問題，涵蓋 11 個推理類別和 9 種視覺退化類型，產生了超過 10K 的視覺問答實例。對 25 個開源和閉源 MLLMs 的評估顯示，視覺退化持續且顯著地損害空間推理，暴露出一個關鍵的穩健性差距。最後，我們展示了在 SpaceDG 上進行微調顯著提高了退化穩健性，甚至可以在退化條件下超越人類表現，同時在乾淨圖像上沒有任何性能下降，突顯了針對退化感知訓練在強健空間智能中的潛力。

##### **TerminalWorld: Benchmarking Agents on Real-World Terminal Tasks**
2605.22535v1 by Zhaoyang Chu, Jiarui Hu, Xingyu Jiang, Pengyu Zou, Han Li, Chao Peng, Peter O'Hearn, Earl T. Barr, Mark Harman, Federica Sarro, He Ye

We introduce TerminalWorld, a scalable data engine that automatically reverse-engineers high-fidelity evaluation tasks from "in-the-wild" terminal recordings. Processing 80,870 terminal recordings, the engine yields a full benchmark of 1,530 validated tasks, spanning 18 real-world categories, ranging from short everyday operations to workflows exceeding 50 steps, and covering 1,280 unique commands. From these, we curate a Verified subset of 200 representative, manually reviewed tasks. Comprehensive benchmarking on TerminalWorld-Verified across eight frontier models and six agents reveals that current systems still struggle with authentic terminal workflows, achieving a maximum pass rate of only 62.5%. Moreover, TerminalWorld captures real-world terminal capabilities distinct from existing expert-curated benchmarks (e.g., Terminal-Bench), with only a weak correlation to their scores (Pearson r=0.20). The automated engine makes TerminalWorld authentic and scalable by construction, enabling it to evaluate agents in real-world terminal environments as developer practices evolve. Data and code are available at https://github.com/EuniAI/TerminalWorld.

摘要：我們介紹了 TerminalWorld，一個可擴展的數據引擎，能夠自動從「現場」終端錄音中逆向工程高保真評估任務。處理了 80,870 條終端錄音後，該引擎產生了 1,530 條經過驗證的完整基準任務，涵蓋 18 個現實世界類別，從短小的日常操作到超過 50 步驟的工作流程，並涵蓋 1,280 個獨特命令。從中，我們精選出 200 個具有代表性的經過人工審核的任務作為已驗證子集。對 TerminalWorld-Verified 在八個前沿模型和六個代理上的全面基準測試顯示，當前系統在真實終端工作流程中仍然面臨挑戰，最高通過率僅為 62.5%。此外，TerminalWorld 捕捉到的現實世界終端能力與現有專家策劃的基準（例如，Terminal-Bench）明顯不同，且與它們的分數之間只有弱相關性（Pearson r=0.20）。這個自動化引擎使 TerminalWorld 在構建上既真實又可擴展，使其能夠隨著開發者實踐的演變，在現實世界的終端環境中評估代理。數據和代碼可在 https://github.com/EuniAI/TerminalWorld 獲得。

##### **Stabilising Explainability Fragility in Cybersecurity AI: The Impact and Mitigation of Multicollinearity in Public Benchmark Datasets**
2605.22529v1 by Ioannis J. Vourganas, Anna Lito Michala

This paper investigates a unexplored yet impactful vulnerability in AI explainability used in intrusion detection (IDS): multicollinearity-induced instability. Despite extensive reliance on post-hoc explainability tools such as SHAP or LIME, the impact of correlated features on explanation robustness is not evaluated. We introduce a formal theorem stating that multicollinearity inflates attribution variance. This demonstrates that explanations and feature importances are non-identifiable under multicollinearity. A suite of comprehensive experiments validates the theorem on a representative benchmark dataset, UNSW-NB15. Four widely used families of models are evaluated, including linear, tree-based, kernel, and neural, across full and pruned feature sets based on VIF and correlation thresholding. We propose the novel metric of Explanability Fragility Score and two novel methods to mitigate it with variable integration complexity. CAA-Filtering focuses on stabilising explanations by grouping attributions of trained models. SHARP is a novel training-time regularisation framework that penalises attribution instability, enabling controllable and monotonic improvement of explainability stability. The findings support stable predictive performance, using Kendall's τ to quantify instability across bootstrapped explanations. This work has direct implications for the trustworthiness and reproducibility of XAI in security-critical contexts, and motivates incorporating multicollinearity mitigations into the IDS pipelines, providing a set of guidelines for practitioners.

摘要：這篇論文探討了一個尚未被充分研究但影響深遠的人工智慧可解釋性漏洞，該漏洞存在於入侵檢測（IDS）中：多重共線性引起的不穩定性。儘管廣泛依賴於如SHAP或LIME等事後可解釋性工具，但對於相關特徵對解釋穩健性的影響尚未進行評估。我們提出了一個正式的定理，指出多重共線性會膨脹歸因方差。這表明在多重共線性下，解釋和特徵重要性是不可識別的。一系列全面的實驗在代表性基準數據集UNSW-NB15上驗證了該定理。我們評估了四種廣泛使用的模型家族，包括線性模型、樹基模型、核模型和神經網絡，基於VIF和相關閾值對完整和修剪的特徵集進行評估。我們提出了可解釋性脆弱性分數這一新穎指標，以及兩種新方法來減輕其影響，這些方法具有變數整合的複雜性。CAA-Filtering專注於通過對訓練模型的歸因進行分組來穩定解釋。SHARP是一種新穎的訓練時間正則化框架，對歸因不穩定性進行懲罰，使可解釋性穩定性得到可控和單調的改善。研究結果支持穩定的預測性能，使用Kendall's τ量化引導的穩定性。這項工作對於在安全關鍵環境中XAI的可信度和可重複性具有直接影響，並促使將多重共線性緩解措施納入IDS管道，為實踐者提供了一套指導方針。

##### **Meta-Learning for Rapid Adaptation in Reference Tracking of Uncertain Nonlinear Systems**
2605.22513v1 by Jiaqi Yan, Ankush Chakrabarty, Niklas Schmid, John Lygeros, Alisa Rupenyan

In this paper, we address the problem of reference tracking for uncertain nonlinear systems. Since collecting data from the target system (i.e., the system of interest) is often challenging, our objective is to design optimal controllers using limited target system data. Meta-learning provides a promising paradigm by leveraging offline data from source systems (systems sharing structural similarities with the target system) to accelerate training and enhance control performance. Motivated by this idea, we propose a meta-learning-based control framework that tailors the implicit model-agnostic meta-learning (iMAML) algorithm to the control setting. The framework operates in two phases: an (offline) meta-training phase, where an aggregated representation is learned from source data to capture the shared system dynamics among similar systems, and an (online) meta-adaptation phase, where this representation is fine-tuned on the target system using only a few data samples and limited adaptation steps. We formulate this framework as a bi-level optimization problem and provide an efficient solution with reduced storage complexity and few approximations. The proposed framework is general, allowing various learning algorithms to be integrated. To demonstrate this flexibility, we propose two specific learning algorithms that can be incorporated into our framework based on a neural state-space model and a deep Q-network, respectively. The primary distinction between these approaches is whether explicit system identification is required. Numerical simulations and hardware experiments demonstrate that the proposed methods enhance control performance and consistently outperform baseline approaches.

摘要：在本文中，我們針對不確定非線性系統的參考追蹤問題進行探討。由於從目標系統（即感興趣的系統）收集數據通常具有挑戰性，我們的目標是利用有限的目標系統數據設計最佳控制器。元學習通過利用來自源系統（與目標系統具有結構相似性的系統）的離線數據來加速訓練並增強控制性能，提供了一個有前景的範式。受到這一想法的啟發，我們提出了一個基於元學習的控制框架，將隱式模型無關元學習（iMAML）算法調整為控制設置。該框架分為兩個階段運行：一個（離線）元訓練階段，在此階段從源數據中學習聚合表示，以捕捉相似系統之間的共享系統動態；另一個（在線）元適應階段，在此階段僅使用少量數據樣本和有限的適應步驟對目標系統進行微調。我們將此框架公式化為一個雙層優化問題，並提供一個高效的解決方案，具有較低的存儲複雜性和較少的近似。所提出的框架是通用的，允許各種學習算法的集成。為了展示這一靈活性，我們提出了兩個具體的學習算法，分別可以基於神經狀態空間模型和深度Q網絡納入我們的框架。這些方法之間的主要區別在於是否需要明確的系統識別。數值模擬和硬體實驗表明，所提出的方法增強了控制性能，並且始終優於基準方法。

##### **Search-E1: Self-Distillation Drives Self-Evolution in Search-Augmented Reasoning**
2605.22511v1 by Zihan Liang, Yufei Ma, Ben Chen, Zhipeng Qian, Xuxin Zhang, Huangyu Dai, Lingtao Mao

Post-training has become the dominant recipe for turning a language model into a competent search-augmented reasoning agent. A line of recent work pushes its performance further by adding elaborate machinery on top of this standard pipeline. These augmentations import external supervision from stronger external systems, attach auxiliary modules such as process reward models or retrospective critics, restructure the rollout itself with tree search or multi-stage curricula, or shape the reward with hand-crafted bonuses and penalties. Each addition delivers a measurable gain, but each also inflates the training pipeline and ties the recipe to resources or designs that may not always be available. We take a step back and ask whether any of this machinery is actually necessary, and propose Search-E1, a self-evolution method that lets a search-augmented agent improve through only vanilla GRPO interleaved with offline self-distillation (OFSD). After each GRPO round, the policy rolls out on its own training questions. A token-level forward KL objective then aligns the policy's inference-time distribution to its own distribution under a privileged context that exposes a more efficient sibling trajectory. Despite this simplicity, the procedure naturally provides dense per-step supervision. On seven QA benchmarks, Search-E1 reaches $0.440$ average EM with Qwen2.5-3B, surpassing all open-source baselines at both scales. Code and complete version will be made public soon.

摘要：後訓練已成為將語言模型轉變為有能力的搜索增強推理代理的主流方法。最近的一系列研究通過在這一標準流程之上添加精密的機制，進一步提升了其性能。這些增強引入來自更強外部系統的外部監督，附加輔助模塊，例如過程獎勵模型或回顧批評者，通過樹搜索或多階段課程重構推理過程本身，或通過手工製作的獎金和懲罰來塑造獎勵。每一項新增都帶來可測量的增益，但每一項也都膨脹了訓練流程，並將這一方法與可能並不總是可用的資源或設計緊密相連。我們退後一步，詢問這些機制是否實際上是必要的，並提出Search-E1，一種自我演化方法，讓搜索增強代理僅通過普通的GRPO與離線自我蒸餾（OFSD）交錯進行改進。在每一輪GRPO之後，策略在其自己的訓練問題上進行推理。然後，一個基於標記級別的前向KL目標使策略的推理時間分佈與其在特權上下文下的自身分佈對齊，該上下文暴露出一條更高效的兄弟軌跡。儘管這種簡單性，該程序自然提供了每一步的密集監督。在七個QA基準上，Search-E1達到了$0.440$的平均EM，使用Qwen2.5-3B，超過了所有開源基準。代碼和完整版本將很快公開。

##### **Reflecti-Mate: A Conversational Agent for Adaptive Decision-Making Support Through System 1 and System 2 Thinking**

Making high-stakes personal decisions involves cognitive, emotional, and intuitive processes, and individuals differ in how they allocate attention across these modes. Yet, most current decision-support systems focus primarily on supporting cognitive aspects, rather than adapting to the individual's thinking profile to support integration of different types of thoughts. ##### **LACO: Adaptive Latent Communication for Collaborative Driving**
2605.22504v1 by Tianhao Chen, Yuheng Wu, Dongman Lee

Collaborative driving aims to improve safety and efficiency by enabling connected vehicles to coordinate under partial observability. Recent approaches have evolved from sharing visual features for perception to exchanging language-based reasoning through foundation models for behavioral coordination. Though communicating in language provides intuitive information, it introduces two challenges: high latency caused by autoregressive decoding and information loss caused by compressing rich internal representations into discrete tokens. To address these challenges, we analyze latent communication in collaborative driving under inherent limitations of multi-agent settings. Our analysis reveals agent identity confusion, where direct fusion of latent states entangles decision representations across vehicles. Motivated by this, we propose LACO, a training-free \textbf{LA}tent \textbf{CO}mmunication paradigm that seamlessly adapts pretrained driving models to collaborative settings. LACO introduces Iterative Latent Deliberation (ILD) for latent reasoning, Cross-Horizon Saliency Attribution (CHSA) for communication-efficient information selection, and Structured Semantic Knowledge Distillation (SSKD) to stabilize ego-centric decision making. Closed-loop experiments in CARLA show that LACO notably reduces communication and inference latency while maintaining strong collaborative driving performance.

摘要：協作駕駛旨在透過使連接的車輛在部分可觀察性下協調來提高安全性和效率。最近的方法已經從共享視覺特徵以進行感知演變為通過基礎模型進行基於語言的推理交換，以實現行為協調。雖然用語言進行溝通提供了直觀的信息，但它引入了兩個挑戰：由自回歸解碼引起的高延遲和由於將豐富的內部表示壓縮為離散標記而導致的信息損失。為了解決這些挑戰，我們分析了在多代理設置的固有限制下協作駕駛中的潛在通信。我們的分析揭示了代理身份混淆，其中潛在狀態的直接融合使車輛之間的決策表示交纏在一起。受到此啟發，我們提出了LACO，一種無需訓練的\textbf{LA}tent \textbf{CO}mmunication範式，能夠無縫地將預訓練的駕駛模型適應於協作環境。LACO引入了迭代潛在深思（ILD）用於潛在推理，跨地平線顯著性歸因（CHSA）用於通信高效的信息選擇，以及結構化語義知識蒸餾（SSKD）以穩定自我中心的決策。CARLA中的閉環實驗顯示，LACO顯著減少了通信和推理延遲，同時保持強大的協作駕駛性能。

##### **Compiling Agentic Workflows into LLM Weights: Near-Frontier Quality at Two Orders of Magnitude Less Cost**
2605.22502v1 by Simon Dennis, Rivaan Patil, Kevin Shabahang, Hao Guo

Agent orchestration frameworks have proliferated, collectively exceeding 290,000 GitHub stars across LangGraph, CrewAI, Google ADK, OpenAI Agents SDK, Semantic Kernel, Strands, and LlamaIndex. All follow the same pattern: an external orchestrator above the LLM, injecting instructions and routing decisions every turn. Recent work has shown this architecture is dominated for procedural tasks by simply providing the procedure in a frontier model's system prompt [Dennis et al., 2026a], at the cost of consuming the context window, requiring a frontier model for every conversation, and exposing proprietary procedures to third-party providers. Compiling the procedure into the weights of a small fine-tuned model -- creating a subterranean agent -- should resolve all of these concerns, and prior work (SimpleTOD, FireAct, SynTOD, WorkflowLLM, Agent Lumos) has shown the technique works. Yet developer adoption has overwhelmingly favored orchestration. We identify three perceived barriers and address each empirically across travel booking (14 nodes), Zoom support (14 nodes, product-specific knowledge), and insurance claims (55 nodes, 6 decision hubs).

摘要：代理協調框架已經大量增長，LangGraph、CrewAI、Google ADK、OpenAI Agents SDK、Semantic Kernel、Strands 和 LlamaIndex 的 GitHub 星數總計超過 290,000。所有這些框架都遵循相同的模式：在 LLM 之上有一個外部協調器，每次轉換時注入指令和路由決策。最近的研究顯示，這種架構在程序性任務中占主導地位，只需在前沿模型的系統提示中提供程序 [Dennis et al., 2026a]，但這會消耗上下文窗口，要求每次對話都使用前沿模型，並將專有程序暴露給第三方供應商。將程序編譯進小型微調模型的權重中——創建一個地下代理——應該能解決所有這些問題，而先前的工作（SimpleTOD、FireAct、SynTOD、WorkflowLLM、Agent Lumos）已經顯示這種技術是有效的。然而，開發者的採用卻壓倒性地偏向於協調。我們識別了三個感知的障礙，並在旅行訂票（14 個節點）、Zoom 支援（14 個節點，產品特定知識）和保險索賠（55 個節點，6 個決策中心）中實證解決每一個問題。

##### **BeLink: Biomedical Entity Linking Meets Generative Re-Ranking**
2605.22501v1 by Darya Shlyk, Stefano Montanelli, Lawrence Hunter

Despite recent progress, Biomedical Entity Linking (BEL) with large language models (LLMs) remains computationally inefficient and challenging to deploy in practical settings. Our method demonstrates strong performance on multiple BEL benchmarks, yielding significant improvements in linking accuracy (3%-24%) while reducing inference time compared to the state-of-the-art. ##### **The Neural Compiler: Program-to-Network Translation for Hybrid Scientific Machine Learning**
2605.22498v1 by Lucas Sheneman

Scientific machine learning often requires combining known physics with unknown parameters or correction terms learned from data. Existing approaches either ignore known structure, encode it as a soft penalty, or require hand-written PyTorch code for each equation. We present The Neural Compiler, a system that translates programs written in a first-order Scheme-like expression language into frozen, differentiable PyTorch modules. These modules match the source program to floating-point precision and provide gradients through autograd. In hybrid models, the compiled module encodes known physics exactly while learned components model the unknown remainder. We evaluate the compiler across six experiment domains: Feynman physics equations, Lotka-Volterra dynamics, a damped pendulum, a one-dimensional heat equation, three-dimensional vector mechanics, and compositional generalization. Compiled modules match hand-coded PyTorch implementations numerically for single equations, showing no accuracy loss from compilation. With only 1 to 4 trainable parameters, compiled models recover physical constants to less than 1 percent error in most cases, while standard PINN baselines with more than 8500 parameters show 7 to 93 percent error. Compiled modules also compose with zero error, while neural approximations can accumulate large errors in deep composition chains. The main value of the compiler is not improved accuracy over hand-coded equations, but systematic composability: it generates correct, differentiable modules from symbolic specifications without rewriting each equation by hand. The system supports 51 primitive operations, including vector and matrix algebra, enabling PDE discretizations and hybrid scientific models. This string-in, module-out interface also provides a natural target for large language models that translate scientific descriptions into executable differentiable modules.

摘要：科學機器學習通常需要將已知的物理學與從數據中學習的未知參數或修正項結合起來。現有的方法要麼忽略已知結構，要麼將其編碼為軟懲罰，或者需要為每個方程手動編寫 PyTorch 代碼。我們提出了神經編譯器，一個將用第一階 Scheme 類表達語言編寫的程序轉換為凍結的、可微分的 PyTorch 模塊的系統。這些模塊在浮點精度上與源程序匹配，並通過自動微分提供梯度。在混合模型中，編譯的模塊精確編碼已知物理學，而學習的組件則建模未知的剩餘部分。我們在六個實驗領域評估了編譯器：費曼物理方程、洛特卡-沃爾泰拉動力學、一個阻尼擺、一維熱方程、三維向量力學和組合泛化。編譯的模塊在單個方程上與手動編碼的 PyTorch 實現數值匹配，顯示出編譯過程中沒有準確性損失。僅用 1 到 4 個可訓練參數，編譯模型在大多數情況下能夠以不到 1% 的誤差恢復物理常數，而標準 PINN 基準模型則有超過 8500 個參數，顯示出 7% 到 93% 的誤差。編譯的模塊在組合時也沒有誤差，而神經近似在深度組合鏈中可能會累積大量誤差。編譯器的主要價值不在於相對於手動編碼方程的準確性提升，而在於系統的可組合性：它從符號規範生成正確的、可微分的模塊，而無需手動重寫每個方程。該系統支持 51 種基本操作，包括向量和矩陣代數，實現 PDE 離散化和混合科學模型。這種字符串輸入、模塊輸出的介面也為大型語言模型提供了一個自然的目標，將科學描述轉換為可執行的可微分模塊。

##### **Structured-Sparse Attention for Entity Tracking with Subquadratic Sequence Complexity**
2605.22476v1 by Hangyue Zhao, Paul Caillon, Erwan Fagnou, Alexandre Allauzen

Entity tracking requires maintaining and updating latent states for entities and attributes over long sequences. Recent task-specific attention operators can compress deep Transformer stacks into a few layers by performing multi-hop state propagation within a single layer, but their dense evaluation remains expensive. We show that in this setting, learned attention is strongly structured: most mass concentrates in local block-diagonal neighborhoods with a light cross-block residue. Exploiting this, we derive a blockwise evaluation of a resolvent-style operator that keeps within-block interactions exact and routes cross-block interactions through a reduced system. The resulting evaluation is subquadratic in sequence length $O(n^{4/3}d)$ (and $O(n^{7/3})$ when $d\approx n$). On controlled tracking benchmarks, our method matches the dense operator's accuracy while reducing wall-clock time by $12-29\%$ under a standardized measurement protocol, and is up to $2.4 \times$ faster than a compact dense Transformer at comparable exact-match accuracy. We further provide ablations over block size and model capacity, and identify a limitation: performance collapses when the number of simultaneously evolving properties exceeds the number of attention heads.

摘要：實體追蹤需要在長序列中維護和更新實體及其屬性的潛在狀態。最近的任務特定注意力運算子可以通過在單一層內執行多跳狀態傳播，將深層Transformer堆疊壓縮為幾層，但其密集評估仍然昂貴。我們展示了在這種情況下，學習到的注意力是高度結構化的：大多數質量集中在局部塊對角鄰域中，並且有輕微的跨塊殘留。利用這一點，我們推導出一種塊狀評估的解算子，該運算子保持塊內互動的精確性，並通過減少系統路由跨塊互動。最終的評估在序列長度上是次二次的 $O(n^{4/3}d)$（當 $d\approx n$ 時為 $O(n^{7/3})$）。在受控追蹤基準測試中，我們的方法在標準化測量協議下，匹配了密集運算子的準確性，同時將牆鐘時間減少了 $12-29\%$，並且在可比較的精確匹配準確性下，比緊湊的密集Transformer快了最多 $2.4 \times$。我們進一步提供了對塊大小和模型容量的消融實驗，並識別出一個限制：當同時演變的屬性數量超過注意力頭的數量時，性能會崩潰。

##### **BioFormer: Rethinking Cross-Subject Generalization via Spectral Structural Alignment in Biomedical Time-Series**
2605.22468v1 by Guikang Du, Haoran Li, Xinyu Liu, Zhibo Zhang, Xiaoli Gong, Jin Zhang

Cross-subject generalization in biomedical time-series refers to training on data from some subjects and testing on unseen subjects.The key challenge is to suppress subject specific variability in BTS representations.Most existing methods implicitly suppress the variability through model building or subject adversarial learning, but rarely model it explicitly.We introduce spectral drift as a new perspective to characterize subject specific variability.Specifically, BTS signals under the same label often share consistent oscillatory structure, yet exhibit subject-dependent magnitude or phase shifts in specific frequency components, which we interpret as subject-specific variability. Building on this insight, we propose BioFormer.At its core is a Frequency-Band Alignment Module(FBAM) that generates band-wise modulation factors from the spectral distribution and adaptively adjusts amplitude and phase to align spectral structure, thereby mitigating variability.We further pair FBAM with Sample Conditional Layer Normalization, which infers normalization parameters from intrinsic signal statistics rather than subject identity, stabilizing cross-subject representations.Extensive experiments on six datasets demonstrate that BioFormer outperforms 12 baselines, yielding absolute F1-score improvements of 6%.

摘要：跨主題的生物醫學時間序列泛化是指在某些主題的數據上進行訓練，並在未見過的主題上進行測試。<lb/>主要挑戰在於抑制BTS表示中的主題特定變異性。<lb/>大多數現有方法通過模型構建或主題對抗學習隱式地抑制變異性，但很少明確建模。<lb/>我們引入光譜漂移作為一種新的視角來表徵主題特定的變異性。<lb/>具體而言，具有相同標籤的BTS信號通常共享一致的振盪結構，但在特定頻率成分中顯示出依賴於主題的幅度或相位偏移，我們將其解釋為主題特定的變異性。<lb/>基於這一見解，我們提出了BioFormer。<lb/>其核心是一個頻帶對齊模塊（FBAM），該模塊從光譜分佈生成帶狀調制因子，並自適應地調整幅度和相位以對齊光譜結構，從而減輕變異性。<lb/>我們進一步將FBAM與樣本條件層正則化配對，該方法從內在信號統計中推斷正則化參數，而不是主題身份，穩定跨主題表示。<lb/>在六個數據集上的廣泛實驗表明，BioFormer的性能超過了12個基準，絕對F1分數提高了6%。

##### **In Silico Modeling of the RAMPHO Buffer: Dissociating Informational and Energetic Masking via Phonetic Entropy in Deep Neural Networks**
2605.22465v1 by Stefan Bleeck

The fundamental challenge of listening in multi-talker environments is a cognitive bottleneck, defined by the Ease of Language Understanding (ELU) model as a failure within the RAMPHO episodic buffer. Current deep neural networks for speech enhancement optimize purely for physical acoustics, failing to account for the cognitive penalty of informational masking. Here, we present an in silico simulation of the RAMPHO buffer using the frame-by-frame phonetic entropy of a self-supervised acoustic model (wav2vec 2.0). By contrasting a semantically intact distractor with a phase-decorrelated distractor (the Concentration Shield) across a signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) sweep, we successfully dissociate the cognitive penalty of informational distraction from the physical penalty of energetic decay. The simulation reveals a cognitive-acoustic Pareto optimization problem: destroying a distractor's semantic payload provides a release from informational masking at high SNRs, but fundamentally degrades temporal glimpsing cues at low SNRs.

摘要：多說話者環境中聆聽的根本挑戰是一種認知瓶頸，根據語言理解的易用性（ELU）模型，這被定義為RAMPHO情節緩衝區內的失敗。當前的語音增強深度神經網絡純粹針對物理聲學進行優化，未能考慮信息遮蔽的認知懲罰。在這裡，我們展示了一個使用自我監督聲學模型（wav2vec 2.0）的逐幀語音熵的RAMPHO緩衝區的計算機模擬。通過在信噪比（SNR）範圍內對比語義完整的干擾源與相位去相關的干擾源（集中盾），我們成功地將信息干擾的認知懲罰與能量衰減的物理懲罰區分開來。模擬揭示了一個認知-聲學的帕累托優化問題：破壞干擾源的語義負載在高SNR下提供了信息遮蔽的釋放，但在低SNR下基本上降低了時間瞬間提示的線索。

##### **From Correlation to Cause: A Five-Stage Methodology for Feature Analysis in Transformer Language Models**
2605.22462v1 by Caleb Munigety

We propose a five-stage methodology for causal feature analysis in transformer language models (probe design, feature extraction, causal validation, robustness testing, and deployment integration) and demonstrate it end-to-end on GPT-2 small performing the Indirect Object Identification (IOI) task. Activation patching recovers the canonical IOI circuit (layer-9 head 9 alone gives recovery +1.02). A sparse autoencoder recovers per-name selective features with effect sizes of 30 to 50 activation units. Causal validation finds these features specifically but only partially causal: ablating fifteen of them leaves the model accurate on 98% of prompts. Two NLA-inspired evaluations strengthen this picture: the fifteen selective features explain only 31% of activation variance versus the SAE's 99.7%, and selectivity ratio anticorrelates with causal force (r = -0.56). Robustness testing under three distribution shifts finds that the circuit transfers cleanly but feature ablation effects degrade substantially, exposing a gap between detection robustness and causal robustness. A cost-based deployment evaluation (assumed $50/FN, $0.42/FP, 2% error rate) finds an optimal monitor configuration yielding $8.96 per 1000 queries against a $1000 baseline, a 99.1% saving. Optimal composition strategy varies with cost ratio and base rate. The conjunction of stages produces findings no single stage would.

摘要：我們提出了一種五階段的方法論，用於Transformer語言模型中的因果特徵分析（探針設計、特徵提取、因果驗證、穩健性測試和部署整合），並在 GPT-2 small 上對間接賓語識別（IOI）任務進行了端到端的演示。激活修補恢復了典型的 IOI 電路（第 9 層第 9 個頭單獨給出的恢復為 +1.02）。稀疏自編碼器恢復了每個名稱的選擇性特徵，效果大小為 30 到 50 個激活單位。因果驗證發現這些特徵具體但僅部分是因果的：去除其中十五個後，模型在 98% 的提示上仍然準確。兩個受 NLA 啟發的評估進一步加強了這一觀點：這十五個選擇性特徵僅解釋了 31% 的激活方差，而 SAE 則為 99.7%，而選擇性比率與因果力呈負相關（r = -0.56）。在三種分佈轉變下的穩健性測試發現，電路轉移乾淨，但特徵去除效應大幅下降，揭示了檢測穩健性與因果穩健性之間的差距。一項基於成本的部署評估（假設 $50/FN，$0.42/FP，2% 錯誤率）發現最佳監控配置每 1000 次查詢可產生 $8.96 的收益，相對於 $1000 的基準，節省了 99.1%。最佳組合策略隨著成本比率和基準率而變化。各階段的結合產生了單一階段無法得出的發現。

##### **Steins;Gate Drive: Semantic Safety Arbitration over Structured Futures for Latency-Decoupled LLM Planning**
2605.22456v1 by Anjie Qiu, Hans D. Schotten

Cloud-hosted LLM driver agents provide useful semantic judgments, but their inference latency exceeds stepwise vehicle-control windows. Learned world models predict futures, but they usually keep future generation and action selection inside large coupled loops. We present SteinsGateDrive, a latency-decoupled planner-runtime architecture in which the worldline metaphor from the eponymous story names one plausible consequence of an intervention: the LLM selects counterfactual driving futures before the final control instant, and a runtime reuses the selected forecast only while safety contracts remain valid. The generator builds three world-line roles: alpha nominal ego-conditioned futures, beta interaction counterfactuals around nearby vehicles, and gamma hazard-stress futures such as braking, cut-ins, or blocked corridors. The selected branch becomes a typed StrategicForecast with horizon, validity/abort conditions, fallback, and authority. On a within-subject, matched-seed normal-highway protocol with 10 seeds and 20 steps, GPT-5.4 mini reduces effective lag from +3.07 s at 1-second horizon to -0.01 s at 4-second horizon while preserving the measured no-collision safety boundary. The architecture's safety contribution comes from the atom-predicate runtime check, not from the drift score, which functions as a refresh-frequency knob.

摘要：雲端托管的 LLM 驅動代理提供有用的語義判斷，但它們的推理延遲超過逐步車輛控制的時間窗口。學習的世界模型預測未來，但它們通常將未來生成和行動選擇保持在大型耦合循環內。我們提出 SteinsGateDrive，一種延遲解耦的規劃運行架構，其中來自同名故事的世界線隱喻命名了一個干預的合理後果：LLM 在最終控制瞬間之前選擇反事實駕駛未來，而運行時僅在安全合約仍然有效時重用所選預測。生成器構建三個世界線角色：alpha 名義自我條件的未來、beta 周圍車輛的互動反事實，以及 gamma 危險壓力未來，如剎車、切入或阻塞走廊。所選分支成為一個類型化的 StrategicForecast，具有時間範圍、有效性/中止條件、後備和權限。在一個內部受試者、匹配種子正常高速公路協議中，使用 10 個種子和 20 步，GPT-5.4 mini 將有效延遲從 1 秒時間範圍的 +3.07 秒減少到 4 秒時間範圍的 -0.01 秒，同時保持測量的無碰撞安全邊界。該架構的安全貢獻來自於原子謂詞運行時檢查，而不是漂移分數，後者作為刷新頻率的調節旋鈕。

##### **Making the Discrete Continuous: Synthetic RAW Augmentations for Fine-Grained Evaluation of Person Detection Performance in Low Light**
2605.22455v1 by Valeria Pais, Malena Mendilaharzu, Daniele Faccio, Luis Oala, Christoph Clausen, Bruno Sanguinetti

Real-world deployment of AI vision models is both fueled and limited by the data available for training and testing. Real datasets are sparse and uneven: long-tailed or unbalanced distributions hinder generalization, and the low number of samples in low density regions makes it hard to run evaluations. Synthetic data can fill these gaps, providing us with a way to sample the input space more continuously and improve data coverage for benchmarks. Focusing on the autonomous driving safety-critical case of pedestrian detection in the dark, we show how synthetic low-light samples can be used to better characterize the performance of a state-of-the-art object detection model as a function of the scene illumination. We use a synthetic RAW image augmentation technique to generate low-light samples that match the noise model of the camera sensor. Performance metrics on real and synthetic low-light data are similar, indicating that the AI model finds it hard to distinguish between them.

摘要：現實世界中 AI 視覺模型的部署既受到可用於訓練和測試的數據的推動，也受到其限制。<lb/>真實數據集稀疏且不均勻：長尾或不平衡的分佈妨礙了泛化，而低密度區域樣本數量少使得評估變得困難。<lb/>合成數據可以填補這些空白，為我們提供了一種更連續地抽樣輸入空間的方法，並改善基準測試的數據覆蓋率。<lb/>專注於自動駕駛安全關鍵的黑暗環境行人檢測案例，我們展示了如何使用合成低光樣本來更好地表徵最先進物體檢測模型的性能，這一性能取決於場景的照明。<lb/>我們使用合成 RAW 圖像增強技術生成與相機傳感器噪聲模型相匹配的低光樣本。<lb/>在真實和合成低光數據上的性能指標相似，這表明 AI 模型難以區分它們。

##### **S2ED: From Story to Executable Descriptions for Consistency-Aware Story Illustration**
2605.22448v1 by Sijing Yin, Jiamou Liu, Xiao Tang, Yaser Shakib, Qian Liu

Multi-frame story illustration requires long-horizon coherence beyond single-image text-to-image generation, including narrative decomposition and persistent character identity, layout, and affect across frames. We propose Story-to-Executable Descriptions (S2ED), a training-free, model-agnostic, prompt-layer framework that converts a full story into a sequence of explicit, editable executable descriptions for more consistent rendering. S2ED coordinates three agents to segment the narrative, ground canonical character attributes, and enrich spatial and affective cues, enabling interpretable prompt-carried state propagation and local edits to repair drift without retraining the generator. Experiments on Flintstones and Shakoo Maku show that S2ED improves sequence-level consistency and character fidelity over strong prompting, large-model planning, and a reference training-based method, under both automatic metrics and human judgments. We also deploy S2ED in an end-to-end story-to-storybook system for children's illustrated stories, with a supplementary video.

摘要：多幀故事插圖需要超越單一圖像的文本到圖像生成的長期一致性，包括敘事分解和持續的角色身份、佈局以及跨幀的情感。 我們提出了故事到可執行描述 (S2ED)，這是一種無需訓練、模型無關的提示層框架，將完整故事轉換為一系列明確的、可編輯的可執行描述，以實現更一致的渲染。 S2ED 協調三個代理來分段敘事、確定典型角色屬性，並豐富空間和情感提示，使得可解釋的提示攜帶狀態傳播和局部編輯得以實現，無需重新訓練生成器即可修復漂移。 在 Flintstones 和 Shakoo Maku 上的實驗顯示，S2ED 在序列級一致性和角色忠實度上優於強提示、大型模型規劃和基於參考訓練的方法，無論是在自動指標還是人類評價下。我們還在一個端到端的故事到故事書系統中部署了 S2ED，專為兒童插圖故事設計，並附有補充視頻。

##### **Cohesion-6K: An Arabic Dataset for Analyzing Social Cohesion and Conflict in Online Discourse**
2605.22447v1 by Aisha Ali Al-Athba, Wajdi Zaghouani

The study of online discourse has become central to understanding societal polarization. While much research has focused on detecting overt toxicity, the subtle dynamics of social cohesion, meaning the interaction between divisive and unifying narratives, remain computationally underexplored (Bail, 2021; Gonzalez-Bailon and Lelkes, 2023). This paper presents Cohesion-6K, a manually and ChatGPT-assisted annotated dataset of six thousand Arabic public Facebook posts related to the Israeli Occupation of Palestine. Each post is assigned to one of five discourse categories that represent a continuum from conflict to cohesion: Conflict, Resolution, Community Engagement, Supportive Interactions, and Shared Values. The annotation process combines expert human judgment with model-assisted pre-labeling verified by trained annotators, achieving substantial inter-annotator agreement (Cohens kappa = 0.85). Quantitative analysis reveals a consistent engagement gap, where conflict-oriented posts receive between two and four times more user interaction than resolution-oriented ones (p < 0.01). This pattern illustrates how divisive discourse tends to attract disproportionate visibility in Arabic social media spaces. Cohesion-6K provides a transparent and reproducible resource for the study of online cohesion and polarization. The dataset, annotation guidelines, and preprocessing code will be released for research use under an open license, supporting future work in computational social science, digital communication, and Arabic natural language processing.

摘要：線上話語的研究已成為理解社會極化的核心。雖然許多研究專注於檢測明顯的毒性，但社會凝聚力的微妙動態，即分裂與統一敘事之間的互動，仍然在計算上未被充分探索（Bail, 2021；Gonzalez-Bailon 和 Lelkes, 2023）。本文介紹了Cohesion-6K，一個手動和ChatGPT輔助標註的數據集，包含六千條與以色列佔領巴勒斯坦相關的阿拉伯語公共Facebook帖子。每個帖子被分配到五個話語類別中的一個，這些類別代表從衝突到凝聚的連續體：衝突、解決、社區參與、支持性互動和共享價值。標註過程結合了專家的人工判斷與經過訓練的標註者驗證的模型輔助預標註，實現了可觀的標註者間一致性（Cohens kappa = 0.85）。定量分析顯示出一個持續的參與差距，衝突導向的帖子獲得的用戶互動是解決導向帖子的兩到四倍（p < 0.01）。這一模式說明了分裂性話語在阿拉伯社交媒體空間中往往吸引不成比例的可見度。Cohesion-6K提供了一個透明且可重複的資源，用於研究線上凝聚力和極化。該數據集、標註指南和預處理代碼將在開放許可下釋出供研究使用，支持計算社會科學、數字通信和阿拉伯語自然語言處理的未來工作。

##### **Pre-VLA: Preemptive Runtime Verification for Reliable Vision-Language-Action and World-Model Rollouts**
2605.22446v1 by Zhen Sun, Yongjian Guo, Haoran Sun, Luqiao Wang, Wei Lu, Jiachi Ji, Shengzhe Ji, Junwu Xiong, Zhijun Meng

While large vision-language-action (VLA) models and generative world models (WM) have advanced long-horizon embodied intelligence, their practical deployment remains challenged by uncertainty in learning-based action generation. Low-quality actions may cause physical failures during execution or lead to misleading world-model rollouts with redundant rendering costs. To address this issue, we propose Pre-VLA, a unified runtime verification architecture that performs preemptive action validity assessment before physical execution or world-model imagination. Pre-VLA leverages an efficient multimodal backbone with modality-aware pooling and a lightweight dual-branch head to predict both safety confidence and critic-derived advantage scores for candidate action chunks. To handle severe class imbalance and unstable boundary decisions, we train Pre-VLA with a multi-task objective combining Focal classification, advantage regression, and soft-threshold calibration. During deployment, a dual-mode preemptive resampling scheduler filters low-quality actions and triggers adaptive resampling under a limited computation budget. Experiments on the LIBERO benchmark show that Pre-VLA improves the average closed-loop success rate across four suites from 30.79\% to 37.62\% over RynnVLA-002, reduces task execution steps, achieves 183.9 ms average forward verification time per action chunk, and mitigates error accumulation in world-model rollouts.

摘要：大型視覺-語言-行動（VLA）模型和生成世界模型（WM）雖然在長期體現智能方面取得了進展，但其實際部署仍面臨基於學習的行動生成的不確定性挑戰。低質量的行動可能在執行過程中導致物理故障，或導致冗餘渲染成本的誤導性世界模型展開。為了解決這個問題，我們提出了Pre-VLA，一種統一的運行時驗證架構，在物理執行或世界模型想像之前進行預防性的行動有效性評估。Pre-VLA利用高效的多模態骨幹，結合模態感知的池化和輕量級的雙分支頭，來預測候選行動片段的安全信心和批評者導出的優勢分數。為了處理嚴重的類別不平衡和不穩定的邊界決策，我們用結合焦點分類、優勢回歸和軟閾值校準的多任務目標來訓練Pre-VLA。在部署期間，雙模式預防性重採樣調度器過濾低質量行動，並在有限的計算預算下觸發自適應重採樣。在LIBERO基準上的實驗顯示，Pre-VLA將四個套件的平均閉環成功率從30.79\%提高到37.62\%，減少了任務執行步驟，實現了每個行動片段183.9毫秒的平均前向驗證時間，並減輕了世界模型展開中的錯誤累積。

##### **Characterizing the Fault Response of the Intel Neural Compute Stick 2 Under Single-Pulse Electromagnetic Fault Injection**
2605.22437v1 by Štefan Kučerák, Jakub Breier, Xiaolu Hou

Vision processing units and other commercial neural-network inference accelerators are increasingly deployed in safety-relevant edge applications, but their fault response under transient hardware disturbances remains poorly characterized in the open literature. For the Intel Movidius Myriad X, packaged as the Intel Neural Compute Stick 2 (NCS2), only a single feasibility study has been published. We report a systematic single-pulse electromagnetic fault injection (EMFI) campaign on the NCS2 running three ImageNet-trained convolutional neural networks (ResNet-18, ResNet-50, VGG-11) on the OpenVINO runtime. Across 1,536 spot-test trials at characterized hotspots and approximately 16,000 parameter-search trials, single pulses produce four reproducible outcome classes: no measured accuracy change, minor silent data corruption, major persistent degradation that survives across subsequent inferences until model reload, and device hangs requiring USB power-cycling; these outcomes are respectively interpreted as no-effect, SDC with possible SET-like or small persistent-state mechanisms, SEU-like persistent corruption, and SEFI-like loss of functionality. Two findings are central. First, the major-degradation class can be induced at 18-31% of trials at characterized hotspots, with post-collapse top-1 accuracy below five percent and persistence across all subsequent inferences until explicit model reload - a regime that no inference-API-level mechanism detects. Second, this regime is also inducible by pulses delivered to an idle device with the model already loaded, demonstrating that load-time integrity checks alone are insufficient. We discuss mitigation strategies graded by class, focusing on mechanisms implementable at the application level without modification to the device firmware or the OpenVINO runtime.

摘要：視覺處理單元和其他商業神經網絡推理加速器在安全相關的邊緣應用中越來越多地被部署，但它們在瞬態硬體擾動下的故障反應在公開文獻中仍然缺乏充分的特徵描述。對於 Intel Movidius Myriad X，以 Intel Neural Compute Stick 2 (NCS2) 包裝，僅發表了一項可行性研究。我們報告了一項系統性的單脈衝電磁故障注入 (EMFI) 活動，對 NCS2 執行三個經過 ImageNet 訓練的卷積神經網絡（ResNet-18、ResNet-50、VGG-11）在 OpenVINO 運行時下進行測試。在 1,536 次在特徵熱點的隨機測試和約 16,000 次參數搜索試驗中，單脈衝產生四種可重複的結果類別：無測量準確度變化、輕微的靜默數據損壞、主要的持久性退化，這種退化在隨後的推理中仍然存在，直到模型重新加載，以及需要 USB 重新啟動的設備掛起；這些結果分別被解釋為無影響、可能的 SET 類或小型持久狀態機制的 SDC、SEU 類的持久損壞，以及 SEFI 類的功能損失。有兩個發現是核心。首先，在特徵熱點的 18-31% 的試驗中可以誘發主要退化類別，崩潰後的 top-1 準確度低於五個百分比，並且在所有隨後的推理中持續存在，直到明確的模型重新加載——這種情況下沒有任何推理 API 層級的機制能夠檢測到。其次，這種情況也可以通過對已加載模型的閒置設備施加脈衝來誘發，顯示僅依賴載入時的完整性檢查是不夠的。我們討論了根據類別分級的緩解策略，重點關注可在應用層面實施的機制，而無需修改設備固件或 OpenVINO 運行時。

##### **Assisted Counterspeech Writing at the Crossroads of Hate Speech and Misinformation**
2605.22435v1 by Genoveffa Martone, Helena Bonaldi, Marco Guerini

Hate speech and misinformation frequently co-occur online, amplifying prejudice and polarization. Given their scale, using Large Language Models (LLMs) to assist expert counterspeech (CS) writing has gained interest, yet prior work has addressed these phenomena separately. We bridge this gap by studying CS generation in contexts where both hate and misinformation co-occur. We test three knowledge-driven generation strategies: first we prompt an LLM with fact-checkers' guidelines and fact-checking articles; secondly, with NGOs' guidelines and reports; thirdly, we create a mixed strategy that combines guidelines and documents from both. 23 experts revise the generated CS, which are assessed via human and automatic metrics. While LLMs produce adequate CS in 40% of cases, expert edits substantially improve naturalness, exhaustiveness, and adherence to guidelines. Based on the post-edited CS, the mixed strategy proves to be the most effective in crowdsourcing evaluation, pairing strong factual correction with stereotype mitigation and empathetic engagement.
