摘要：仇恨言論和錯誤資訊在線上經常同時出現，擴大了偏見和極化。考慮到它們的規模，使用大型語言模型（LLMs）來協助專家反駁言論（CS）寫作引起了興趣，然而之前的研究將這些現象分開處理。我們通過研究在仇恨和錯誤資訊同時出現的情境下的CS生成來填補這一空白。我們測試了三種知識驅動的生成策略：首先，我們用事實查核者的指導方針和事實查核文章來提示LLM；其次，使用非政府組織的指導方針和報告；第三，我們創建了一種混合策略，結合了來自兩者的指導方針和文件。23位專家對生成的CS進行修訂，並通過人類和自動化指標進行評估。雖然LLMs在40%的案例中生成了足夠的CS，但專家的編輯顯著提高了自然性、全面性和對指導方針的遵循。根據後編輯的CS，混合策略在眾包評估中被證明是最有效的，將強有力的事實修正與刻板印象緩解和同理心參與相結合。我們發布了一個包含仇恨和錯誤資訊主張的數據集，並附有專家驗證的CS和支持知識。

##### **FastTab: A Fast Table Recognizer with a Tiny Recursive Module and 1D Transformers**
2605.22422v1 by Laziz Hamdi, Amine Tamasna, Pascal Boisson, Thierry Paquet

Table structure recognition (TSR) requires both table-level coherence (row/column counts, headers, spanning cells) and precise separator localization. We introduce FastTab, a grid-centric TSR model that avoids autoregressive HTML decoding by combining (i) a lightweight Tiny Recursive Module (TRM) for global reasoning and (ii) axial 1D Transformer encoders that capture long-range dependencies along rows and columns. The model predicts row/column counts, header rows, and separators to construct a grid, then infers rowspan/colspan using ROI-aligned cell features. Across four benchmarks (PubTabNet, FinTabNet, PubTables-1M, and SciTSR), FastTab achieves competitive structure recovery performance while operating at low-latency inference. We further study robustness under pixel-level anonymisation and show an extension to curved separators for camera-captured documents. The source code will be made publicly available at https://github.com/hamdilaziz/FastTab .

摘要：表格結構識別（TSR）需要表格層級的一致性（行/列計數、標題、跨單元格）以及精確的分隔符定位。<lb/>我們介紹了 FastTab，一種以網格為中心的 TSR 模型，通過結合（i）輕量級的 Tiny Recursive Module（TRM）進行全局推理和（ii）捕捉行和列之間長距離依賴的軸向 1D Transformer 編碼器，避免了自回歸的 HTML 解碼。<lb/>該模型預測行/列計數、標題行和分隔符以構建網格，然後使用 ROI 對齊的單元格特徵推斷 rowspan/colspan。<lb/>在四個基準測試（PubTabNet、FinTabNet、PubTables-1M 和 SciTSR）中，FastTab 在低延遲推理下實現了具有競爭力的結構恢復性能。<lb/>我們進一步研究了在像素級匿名化下的穩健性，並展示了對於相機捕捉文檔的曲線分隔符的擴展。<lb/>源代碼將在 https://github.com/hamdilaziz/FastTab 公開提供。

##### **Diffusion-guided Generalizable Enhancer for Urban Scene Reconstruction**
2605.22420v1 by Henry Che, Jingkang Wang, Yun Chen, Ze Yang, Sivabalan Manivasagam, Raquel Urtasun

Urban scene reconstruction from real-world observations has emerged as a powerful tool for self-driving development and testing. While current neural rendering approaches achieve high-fidelity rendering along the recorded trajectories, their quality degrades significantly under large viewpoint shifts, limiting the applicability for closed-loop simulation. Recent works have shown promising results in using diffusion models to enhance quality at these challenging viewpoints and distill improvements back into 3D representations. However, they often require costly per-scene optimization, and the distilled representations remain fragile and fail to generalize beyond limited synthesized views. To address these limitations, we propose GenRe, a novel diffusion-guided generalizable enhancer for urban scene reconstruction. GenRe takes as input any pretrained 3D Gaussian representation and fixes the deficiencies within a few minutes. By learning to distill generative priors across diverse scenes, GenRe produces robust and high-fidelity representation efficiently that generalizes reliably to challenging unseen viewpoints (e.g., lane change). Experiments show that GenRe outperforms existing methods in both quality and efficiency and benefits various downstream tasks, enabling robust and scalable sensor simulation for autonomous driving.

摘要：城市場景重建從現實世界觀察中已成為自駕車開發和測試的一個強大工具。<lb/>雖然目前的神經渲染方法在錄製的軌跡上實現了高保真渲染，但在大視角變化下其質量顯著下降，限制了其在閉環模擬中的應用。<lb/>最近的研究顯示，使用擴散模型在這些具有挑戰性的視角下增強質量並將改進提煉回3D表示中取得了可喜的結果。<lb/>然而，它們通常需要昂貴的每場景優化，且提煉的表示仍然脆弱，無法在有限的合成視圖之外進行泛化。<lb/>為了解決這些限制，我們提出了GenRe，一種新穎的擴散引導可泛化增強器，用於城市場景重建。<lb/>GenRe接受任何預訓練的3D高斯表示作為輸入，並在幾分鐘內修正不足之處。<lb/>通過學習在多樣場景中提煉生成先驗，GenRe有效地生成穩健且高保真的表示，並可靠地泛化到具有挑戰性的未見視角（例如，變換車道）。<lb/>實驗表明，GenRe在質量和效率上均優於現有方法，並且對各種下游任務有益，使自動駕駛的傳感器模擬變得穩健且可擴展。

##### **Towards Clinically Interpretable Ophthalmic VQA via Spatially-Grounded Lesion Evidence**
2605.22414v1 by Xingyue Wang, Bo Liu, Meng Wang, Zhixuan Zhang, Chengcheng Zhu, Huazhu Fu, Jiang Liu

Visual Question Answering (VQA) holds great promise for clinical support, particularly in ophthalmology, where retinal fundus photography is essential for diagnosis. However, ophthalmic VQA benchmarks primarily emphasize answer accuracy, neglecting the explicit visual evidence necessary for clinical interpretability. In this work, we introduce FundusGround, a new benchmark for clinically interpretable ophthalmic VQA with spatially-grounded lesion evidence. Specifically, we propose a three-stage pipeline that collects 10,719 fundus images with 15,595 image-level meticulously annotated lesions. To ensure anatomical consistency and clinical validity, all lesions are spatially localized using the Early Treatment Diabetic Retinopathy Study (ETDRS) grid, enabling standardized mapping to nine clinically meaningful retinal regions. Built upon this structured lesion evidence, 72,706 questions are then generated spanning four formats: open-ended, closed-ended, single-choice, and multiple-choice. We further benchmark multiple general- and medical- large vision-language models using dual metrics for answer accuracy and lesion-level reasoning. The experiments demonstrate that incorporating lesion-level visual evidence consistently improves model performance and transparency, highlighting the necessity of explicit spatial grounding for reliable and explainable ophthalmic VQA.

摘要：視覺問題回答（VQA）在臨床支持方面具有很大的潛力，特別是在眼科領域，視網膜眼底攝影對於診斷至關重要。<lb/>然而，眼科 VQA 基準主要強調答案的準確性，忽略了臨床可解釋性所需的明確視覺證據。<lb/>在這項工作中，我們介紹了 FundusGround，這是一個新的基準，用於具有空間基礎病變證據的臨床可解釋眼科 VQA。<lb/>具體而言，我們提出了一個三階段的流程，收集了 10,719 張眼底圖像，並附有 15,595 個圖像級別的精心標註病變。<lb/>為了確保解剖一致性和臨床有效性，所有病變都使用早期糖尿病視網膜病變研究（ETDRS）網格進行空間定位，從而實現對九個臨床意義明確的視網膜區域的標準化映射。<lb/>基於這些結構化的病變證據，然後生成了 72,706 個問題，涵蓋四種格式：開放式、封閉式、單選和多選。<lb/>我們進一步基準測試了多個通用和醫學大型視覺-語言模型，使用雙重指標來評估答案的準確性和病變級別的推理。<lb/>實驗表明，納入病變級別的視覺證據始終能改善模型的性能和透明度，突顯了對於可靠和可解釋的眼科 VQA 明確空間基礎的必要性。

##### **DeferMem: Query-Time Evidence Distillation via Reinforcement Learning for Long-Term Memory QA**
2605.22411v1 by Jianing Yin, Tan Tang

Large language model (LLM) agents still struggle with long-term memory question answering, where answer-supporting evidence is often scattered across long conversational histories and buried in substantial irrelevant content. Existing memory systems typically process memory before future queries are known, then retrieve the resulting units based on similarity rather than their utility for answering the query. This workflow leaves downstream answerers to denoise retrieved candidates and reconstruct query-specific evidence. We present DeferMem, a long-term memory framework that decouples this problem into high-recall candidate retrieval and query-conditioned evidence distillation. DeferMem uses a lightweight segment-link structure to organize raw history and retrieve broad candidates at query time. It then applies a memory distiller trained with DistillPO, our reinforcement learning algorithm for distilling the high-recall but highly noisy candidates into a set of faithful, self-contained, and query-conditioned evidence. DistillPO formulates post-retrieval evidence distillation as a structured action comprising message selection and evidence rewriting. It optimizes this action with a decomposed-and-gated reward pipeline and structure-aligned advantage assignment, gating reward components from validity to quality checks while exposing task-level correctness feedback early and assigning each reward to its responsible output span. On LoCoMo and LongMemEval-S, DeferMem surpasses strong baselines in QA accuracy and memory-system efficiency, achieving the highest QA accuracy with the fastest runtime and zero commercial-API token cost for memory operations.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLM）代理在長期記憶問答方面仍然面臨挑戰，因為支持答案的證據經常分散在冗長的對話歷史中，並被大量無關內容掩蓋。現有的記憶系統通常在未來查詢已知之前處理記憶，然後根據相似性而不是其對回答查詢的實用性來檢索結果單元。這種工作流程使得下游回答者需要對檢索到的候選者進行去噪，並重建特定查詢的證據。我們提出了DeferMem，一個長期記憶框架，將這個問題解耦為高召回候選者檢索和查詢條件證據蒸餾。DeferMem使用輕量級的段鏈結構來組織原始歷史並在查詢時檢索廣泛的候選者。然後，它應用一個使用DistillPO訓練的記憶蒸餾器，我們的強化學習算法，用於將高召回但高度噪聲的候選者蒸餾為一組真實、自足且查詢條件的證據。DistillPO將檢索後的證據蒸餾公式化為一個結構化行動，包括消息選擇和證據重寫。它通過一個分解和門控的獎勵管道以及結構對齊的優勢分配來優化這一行動，門控獎勵組件從有效性到質量檢查，同時早期暴露任務級的正確性反饋並將每個獎勵分配給其負責的輸出範圍。在LoCoMo和LongMemEval-S上，DeferMem在問答準確性和記憶系統效率方面超越了強基準，實現了最高的問答準確性，並以最快的運行時間和零商業API令牌成本進行記憶操作。

##### **Epicure: Navigating the Emergent Geometry of Food Ingredient Embeddings**
2605.22391v1 by Jakub Radzikowski, Josef Chen

We present Epicure, a family of three sibling skip-gram ingredient embeddings retrained from scratch on a multilingual recipe corpus. We aggregate 4.14M recipes from 11 sources spanning seven languages, English, Chinese, Russian, Vietnamese, Spanish, Turkish, Indonesian, German, and Indian-English, and normalise the raw ingredient strings to 1,790 canonical entries via an LLM-augmented pipeline. A 203,508-edge ingredient-ingredient NPMI graph and an 80,019-edge typed FlavorDB ingredient-compound graph, 2,247 typed compound nodes across 15 categories, seed three Metapath2Vec variants that share architecture and hyperparameters and differ only in the random-walk schema: Cooc walks the co-occurrence graph only, Chem walks the typed compound metapaths only, and Core blends both via injected ingredient-ingredient walks at controlled mixing, placing each model at a distinct point on the chemistry-vs-recipe-context spectrum.

摘要：我們介紹 Epicure，一個由三個兄弟姐妹組成的 skip-gram 食材嵌入模型，從頭開始在多語言食譜語料庫上重新訓練。<lb/>我們從 11 個來源聚合了 4.14M 食譜，涵蓋七種語言：英語、中文、俄語、越南語、西班牙語、土耳其語、印尼語、德語和印度英語，並通過 LLM 增強的管道將原始食材字符串標準化為 1,790 個典範條目。<lb/>一個 203,508 邊的食材-食材 NPMI 圖和一個 80,019 邊的類型化 FlavorDB 食材-化合物圖，涵蓋 15 類的 2,247 個類型化化合物節點，為三個 Metapath2Vec 變體提供種子，這些變體共享架構和超參數，僅在隨機漫遊方案上有所不同：Cooc 僅在共現圖上漫遊，Chem 僅在類型化化合物的元路徑上漫遊，而 Core 通過在控制混合下注入的食材-食材漫遊來融合兩者，將每個模型放置在化學與食譜上下文光譜的不同點上。

##### **Unified Data Selection for LLM Reasoning**
2605.22389v1 by Xiaoyuan Li, Yubo Ma, Chengpeng Li, Fengbin Zhu, Yiyao Yu, Keqin Bao, Wenjie Wang, Fuli Feng, Dayiheng Liu

Effectively training Large Language Models (LLMs) for complex, long-CoT reasoning is often bottlenecked by the need for massive high-quality reasoning data. Existing methods are either computationally expensive or fail to reliably distinguish high- from low-quality reasoning samples. To address this, we propose High-Entropy Sum (HES), a training-free metric that quantifies reasoning quality by summing only the entropy of the top (e.g., 0.5\%) highest-entropy tokens in each reasoning sample. We validate HES across three mainstream training paradigms: Supervised Fine-tuning (SFT), Rejection Fine-tuning (RFT), and Reinforcement Learning (RL), with extensive results demonstrating its consistent effectiveness and significantly reduced computational overhead. In SFT, training on the top 20\% HES-ranked data matches full-dataset performance, while using the lowest-HES data degrades it. In RFT, our HES-based training approach significantly outperforms baseline methods. In RL, HES-selected successful trajectories enable the model to learn strong reasoning patterns, significantly surpassing other compared methods. Our findings establish HES as a robust, training-free metric that enables a unified, effective, and efficient method for developing advanced reasoning in LLMs.

摘要：有效地訓練大型語言模型（LLMs）以進行複雜的長鏈推理，通常受到需要大量高質量推理數據的瓶頸限制。現有的方法要麼計算成本高昂，要麼無法可靠地區分高質量和低質量的推理樣本。為了解決這個問題，我們提出了高熵總和（HES），這是一種無需訓練的指標，通過僅對每個推理樣本中前（例如，0.5\%）最高熵的標記進行熵的總和來量化推理質量。我們在三種主流訓練範式中驗證了HES：監督微調（SFT）、拒絕微調（RFT）和強化學習（RL），並提供了大量結果，顯示其一致的有效性和顯著降低的計算開銷。在SFT中，對前20\% HES排名數據的訓練達到了全數據集的性能，而使用最低HES數據則會降低性能。在RFT中，我們基於HES的訓練方法顯著優於基線方法。在RL中，HES選擇的成功軌跡使模型能夠學習強大的推理模式，顯著超越其他比較方法。我們的研究結果確立了HES作為一種穩健的、無需訓練的指標，能夠為開發LLMs中的高級推理提供統一的、有效的和高效的方法。

##### **Cross-Subject EEG Emotion Recognition Based on Temporal Asynchronous Alignment Contrastive Learning**
2605.22379v1 by Ying Xie, Yi Zheng, Zehui Xiao, Wenkai Lu, Mengting Liu

With the advancement of science and technology, the importance of emotion research has become increasingly evident. Electroencephalography (EEG)-based emotion recognition has emerged as an active research area in recent years, owing to its objectivity and high temporal resolution. However, most existing methods focus on optimizing encoder structures to enhance feature extraction capabilities, while paying relatively little attention to similarity calculation strategies, particularly overlooking the potential temporal misalignment of responses among different subjects. To address these shortcomings, this paper draws inspiration from the late interaction mechanism of ColBERT in natural language processing (NLP) and proposes a Temporal Asynchronous Alignment-based Contrastive Learning (TA2CL) framework. This method transforms the traditional global "hard alignment" similarity calculation approach into a fine-grained local matching mechanism, enabling the model to adaptively search for and align "locally highly correlated" segments between two EEG signals, thereby effectively mitigating the effects of inter-subject differences and temporal delays. Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed method achieves strong performance across multiple public datasets. Specifically, on the FACED dataset, it achieves an accuracy of 64.5% for the nine-class classification task and 79.5% for the binary classification task, while on the SEED and SEED-V datasets, it achieves accuracies of 86.4% and 70.1%, respectively, validating the method's effectiveness and generalization capability.

摘要：隨著科學和技術的進步，情感研究的重要性變得越來越明顯。基於腦電圖（EEG）的情感識別在近年來成為一個活躍的研究領域，這得益於其客觀性和高時間解析度。然而，大多數現有方法專注於優化編碼器結構以增強特徵提取能力，而相對較少關注相似性計算策略，特別是忽視了不同受試者之間反應的潛在時間錯位。為了解決這些不足，本文受到了自然語言處理（NLP）中ColBERT的晚期互動機制的啟發，提出了一種基於時間異步對齊的對比學習（TA2CL）框架。這種方法將傳統的全局“硬對齊”相似性計算方法轉變為一種細粒度的局部匹配機制，使模型能夠自適應地搜尋並對齊兩個EEG信號之間“局部高度相關”的片段，從而有效減輕受試者之間差異和時間延遲的影響。實驗結果表明，所提出的方法在多個公共數據集上達到了良好的表現。具體而言，在FACED數據集上，該方法在九類分類任務中達到了64.5%的準確率，在二元分類任務中達到了79.5%的準確率，而在SEED和SEED-V數據集上，分別達到了86.4%和70.1%的準確率，驗證了該方法的有效性和泛化能力。

##### **Boundary-targeted Membership Inference Attacks on Safety Classifiers**
2605.22373v1 by Anthony Hughes, Alexander Goldberg, Prince Jha, Adam Perer, Nikolaos Aletras, Niloofar Mireshghallah

Safety classifiers are essential safeguards within generative AI systems, filtering harmful content or identifying at-risk users when interacting with large language models. Despite their necessity, these models are trained on sensitive datasets including discussions of self-harm and mental health, raising important, yet poorly understood, privacy concerns. Membership inference attacks (MIAs) allow adversaries to infer membership of examples used to train models. In this work, we hypothesize that identifying the examples on which the classifier is least confident are informative for an adversary to infer membership. This reflects a localized failure of generalization, where the model relies on memorization to resolve ambiguity in the training set. To investigate this, we introduce a new boundary-targeted selection strategy that identifies low confidence examples that amplify the signal of an examples membership within a training set. Our experimental results show that an adversary can recover 19\% of the conversations a safety classifier flagged as indicating user distress, at a 5\% false-positive rate, on a classifier fine-tuned for detecting a user who may require emotional support. This is $3.5$ times more than attacking using state-of-the-art MIA methods alone. Finally, we characterize the boundary laying examples and show that content-based filtering is ineffective for protection, and existing noise strategies can effectively mitigate susceptibility of these examples.

摘要：安全分類器是生成式 AI 系統中的重要保護措施，在與大型語言模型互動時過濾有害內容或識別高風險用戶。儘管它們是必要的，但這些模型是在敏感數據集上訓練的，包括自我傷害和心理健康的討論，這引發了重要但尚未充分理解的隱私問題。成員推斷攻擊（MIAs）使對手能夠推斷用於訓練模型的示例的成員資格。在這項工作中，我們假設識別分類器最不自信的示例對於對手推斷成員資格是有信息量的。這反映了泛化的局部失敗，模型依賴於記憶來解決訓練集中的模糊性。為了調查這一點，我們引入了一種新的邊界目標選擇策略，該策略識別低信心示例，從而放大訓練集中示例成員資格的信號。我們的實驗結果顯示，對手可以在 5\% 的假陽性率下，恢復安全分類器標記為顯示用戶困擾的 19\% 的對話，這是針對可能需要情感支持的用戶進行微調的分類器。這比僅使用最先進的 MIA 方法進行攻擊多出 $3.5$ 倍。最後，我們對邊界示例進行了特徵描述，並顯示基於內容的過濾對於保護是無效的，而現有的噪聲策略可以有效減輕這些示例的易受攻擊性。

##### **VeriScale: Adversarial Test-Suite Scaling for Verifiable Code Generation**
2605.22368v1 by Yifan Bai, Xiaoyang Liu, Zihao Mou, Guihong Wang, Jian Yu, Shuhan Xie, Yantao Li, Yangyu Zhang, Jingwei Liang, Tao Luo

As large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed for software engineering, constructing high-quality benchmarks is crucial for evaluating not just the functional correctness, but also the formal verifiability of generated code. However, existing benchmarks are limited by the quantity and quality of positive and negative test cases, leading to an overestimation of model capabilities in generating specifications and implementations. To address this, we propose VeriScale, a novel framework driven by the adversarial implementations. It consists of two stages: test-suite expansion to construct diverse and challenging test cases, and test-suite reduction to distill them into compact yet discriminative suites. While VeriScale is general, we instantiate it on Verina to construct VerinaPlus, which expands the original test suites by over 83$\times$, and VerinaLite, a lightweight 14$\times$ variant. Our experiments across eight state-of-the-art LLMs demonstrate that VerinaPlus exposes substantial model weaknesses hidden by the original benchmark, evidenced by sharp score drops on both SpecGen and CodeGen tasks, whereas VerinaLite maintains this discriminative power at a fraction of the evaluation cost. The enhanced benchmarks and source code are publicly available at https://github.com/XiaoyangLiu-sjtu/VeriScale.

摘要：隨著大型語言模型（LLMs）在軟體工程中的應用日益增多，構建高品質的基準測試對於評估生成代碼的功能正確性以及形式可驗證性至關重要。<lb/>然而，現有的基準測試受到正負測試案例的數量和質量的限制，導致對模型在生成規範和實現方面能力的高估。<lb/>為了解決這個問題，我們提出了VeriScale，一個由對抗性實現驅動的新框架。<lb/>它由兩個階段組成：測試套件擴展以構建多樣化且具有挑戰性的測試案例，以及測試套件縮減以將其提煉為緊湊但具區分性的套件。<lb/>雖然VeriScale是通用的，我們在Verina上實現了它，以構建VerinaPlus，該版本將原始測試套件擴展了超過83$\times$，以及VerinaLite，一個輕量級的14$\times$變體。<lb/>我們在八個最先進的LLMs上的實驗表明，VerinaPlus揭示了原始基準測試隱藏的模型弱點，這在SpecGen和CodeGen任務中表現為分數的急劇下降，而VerinaLite在評估成本的一小部分下保持了這種區分能力。<lb/>增強的基準測試和源代碼已公開提供於 https://github.com/XiaoyangLiu-sjtu/VeriScale。

##### **Scaling Observation-aware Planning in Uncertain Domains**
2605.22364v1 by Adrian Zvizdenco, Arthur Conrado Veiga Bosquetti, Alberto Lluch Lafuente, Christoph Matheja

Deciding which sensing capabilities to deploy on an agent in uncertain domains is a fundamental engineering challenge, in which one balances task achievability against the high costs of hardware and processing. This problem has previously been formalized as the Optimal Observability Problem (OOP), based on the well-known Partially Observable Markov Decision Process (POMDP) model for decision-making. This work studies (sub-)symbolic techniques to scale solving of decidable fragments of the OOP, namely the Sensor Selection Problem (SSP) and the Positional Observability Problem (POP). Besides improving the original approach based on parameter synthesis, we develop a new solving method that identifies sensible observation functions via decomposition of POMDPs, improving performance by 3 and 5 orders of magnitude for instance size and runtime, respectively.

摘要：在不確定領域中決定在代理上部署哪些感測能力是一項基本的工程挑戰，這需要在任務可達性與硬體和處理的高成本之間取得平衡。這個問題之前已經被形式化為最佳可觀察性問題（OOP），基於著名的部分可觀察馬可夫決策過程（POMDP）模型進行決策。本研究探討（子）符號技術，以擴展可解片段的解決方案，即感測器選擇問題（SSP）和位置可觀察性問題（POP）。除了改進基於參數合成的原始方法外，我們還開發了一種新的解決方法，通過對POMDP的分解來識別合理的觀察函數，從而在實例大小和運行時間上分別提高了3和5個數量級的性能。

##### **Modeling Pathology-Like Behavioral Patterns in Language Models Through Behavioral Fine-Tuning**
2605.22356v1 by Nicola Milano, Davide Marocco

Large language models are increasingly used as computational tools for modeling human-like behavior. We introduce a behavioral induction framework that modifies model policies through fine-tuning on structured decision-making tasks: using synthetic datasets inspired by maladaptive behavioral patterns, including depression and paranoia, we train transformer-based language models to consistently select specific classes of actions across diverse contexts. We then test whether this behavioral optimization produces systematic changes in generative distributions.
  Across two architectures, fine-tuned models show stable, context-general shifts in next-token probability distributions, including increased probability assigned to negative and threat-related interpretations in open-ended language tasks. These effects generalize beyond training contexts and are detectable in qualitative completions, psychometric-style evaluations, and quantitative distributional metrics such as Jensen-Shannon divergence.
  Induced behavioral profiles also show partial specificity. Models optimized for different behavioral patterns exhibit dissociable response tendencies across evaluation probes, suggesting that structured behavioral training produces differentiated policy-level biases rather than generic distributional skew.
  We interpret these findings as evidence that consistent behavioral optimization in LLMs can generate stable behavioral and distributional patterns consistent with altered latent priors, linking action selection and language generation. More broadly, the results support a view of LLMs as policy-based systems in which behavioral constraints shape emergent representational structure, highlighting their potential as controlled testbeds for studying the relationship between behavior, interpretation, and generative language in computational models of cognition.

摘要：大型語言模型越來越多地被用作模擬人類行為的計算工具。<lb/>我們介紹了一個行為誘導框架，通過在結構化決策任務上進行微調來修改模型策略：使用受不適應性行為模式啟發的合成數據集，包括抑鬱和偏執，我們訓練基於Transformer的語言模型，以在多樣的上下文中一致地選擇特定類別的行動。<lb/>然後，我們測試這種行為優化是否產生生成分佈的系統性變化。<lb/>在兩種架構中，微調後的模型顯示出下一個標記概率分佈的穩定、上下文通用的變化，包括在開放式語言任務中對負面和威脅相關解釋的概率增加。<lb/>這些效果超越了訓練上下文，並且在定性完成、心理測量風格的評估和定量分佈指標（如詹森-香農散度）中可檢測到。<lb/>誘導的行為特徵也顯示出部分特異性。<lb/>針對不同行為模式優化的模型在評估探針中表現出可分離的反應傾向，這表明結構化的行為訓練產生了區分的政策級偏見，而不是通用的分佈偏斜。<lb/>我們將這些發現解釋為證據，表明在大型語言模型中的一致行為優化可以生成穩定的行為和分佈模式，這與改變的潛在先驗一致，將行動選擇和語言生成聯繫起來。<lb/>更廣泛地說，這些結果支持將大型語言模型視為基於政策的系統的觀點，其中行為約束塑造了新興的表徵結構，突顯了它們作為受控測試平台的潛力，以研究行為、解釋和生成語言之間的關係，這在認知的計算模型中具有重要意義。

##### **TransitLM: A Large-Scale Dataset and Benchmark for Map-Free Transit Route Generation**
2605.22355v1 by Hanyu Guo, Jiedong Yang, Chao Chen, Longfei Xu, Kaikui Liu, Xiangxiang Chu

Public transit route planning traditionally depends on structured map infrastructure and complex routing engines, and no existing dataset supports training models to bypass this dependency. We present TransitLM, a large-scale dataset of over 13 million transit route planning records from four Chinese cities covering 120,845 stations and 13,666 lines, released as a continual pre-training corpus and benchmark data for three evaluation tasks with complementary metrics. Experiments show that an LLM trained on TransitLM produces structurally valid routes at high accuracy and implicitly grounds arbitrary GPS coordinates to appropriate stations without any explicit mapping. These results demonstrate that transit route planning can be learned entirely from data, enabling end-to-end, map-free route generation directly from origin-destination information. The dataset and benchmark are available at https://huggingface.co/datasets/GD-ML/TransitLM, with evaluation code at https://github.com/HotTricker/TransitLM.

摘要：公共交通路線規劃傳統上依賴於結構化的地圖基礎設施和複雜的路由引擎，而現有的數據集並不支持訓練模型以繞過這一依賴。我們提出了TransitLM，一個來自四個中國城市的超過1300萬條公共交通路線規劃記錄的大型數據集，涵蓋了120,845個車站和13,666條路線，作為持續預訓練語料庫和三個評估任務的基準數據，並提供互補的指標。實驗表明，基於TransitLM訓練的LLM以高準確度產生結構上有效的路線，並且在沒有任何明確映射的情況下，將任意GPS坐標隱式地對應到適當的車站。這些結果表明，公共交通路線規劃可以完全從數據中學習，使得從起點到終點的信息直接生成端到端、無需地圖的路線。數據集和基準可在https://huggingface.co/datasets/GD-ML/TransitLM獲得，評估代碼則在https://github.com/HotTricker/TransitLM。

##### **Bernini: Latent Semantic Planning for Video Diffusion**
2605.22344v1 by  Bernini Team, Chenchen Liu, Junyi Chen, Lei Li, Lu Chi, Mingzhen Sun, Zhuoying Li, Yi Fu, Ruoyu Guo, Yiheng Wu, Ge Bai, Zehuan Yuan

Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) and diffusion models have each reached remarkable maturity: MLLMs excel at reasoning over heterogeneous multimodal inputs with strong semantic grounding, while diffusion models synthesize images and videos with photorealistic fidelity. We argue that these two families can be unified through a simple division of labor: MLLMs perform semantic planning, while diffusion models render pixels from high-level semantic guidance and low-level visual features. Building on this idea, we propose Bernini, a unified framework for video generation and editing. An MLLM-based planner predicts the target semantic representation directly in the ViT embedding space, and a DiT-based renderer synthesizes pixels conditioned on this plan, augmented by text features and, for editing, source VAE features for detail preservation. Because semantics serve as the interface, the planner and renderer can be trained separately and only lightly co-trained, preserving the pretrained strengths of both components while keeping training efficient. To better handle multiple visual inputs, we introduce Segment-Aware 3D Rotary Positional Embedding (SA-3D RoPE), and further incorporate chain-of-thought reasoning in the planner to better transfer understanding into generation. Bernini achieves state-of-the-art performance across a wide range of video generation and editing benchmarks, with the MLLM's pretrained understanding translating into strong generalization on challenging editing tasks.

摘要：多模態大型語言模型（MLLMs）和擴散模型各自達到了顯著的成熟度：MLLMs 在對異質多模態輸入進行推理時表現出色，具有強大的語義基礎，而擴散模型則以照片真實的保真度合成圖像和視頻。我們認為這兩個家族可以通過簡單的分工來統一：MLLMs 執行語義規劃，而擴散模型則根據高層語義指導和低層視覺特徵渲染像素。在這一想法的基礎上，我們提出了 Bernini，一個統一的視頻生成和編輯框架。基於 MLLM 的規劃器直接在 ViT 嵌入空間中預測目標語義表示，而基於 DiT 的渲染器則根據這一計劃合成像素，並通過文本特徵以及在編輯時通過源 VAE 特徵來增強細節保留。由於語義作為接口，規劃器和渲染器可以分開訓練，並且僅輕度共同訓練，保留兩個組件的預訓練優勢，同時保持訓練的高效性。為了更好地處理多個視覺輸入，我們引入了段落感知 3D 旋轉位置嵌入（SA-3D RoPE），並進一步在規劃器中納入鏈式思維推理，以更好地將理解轉化為生成。Bernini 在廣泛的視頻生成和編輯基準上達到了最先進的性能，MLLM 的預訓練理解轉化為在挑戰性編輯任務上的強泛化能力。

##### **4D-GSW: Kinematic-Aware Spatio-Temporal Consistent Watermarking for 4D Gaussian Splatting**
2605.22342v1 by Sifan Zhou, Hang Zhang, Yuhang Wang, Ming Li

While 4D Gaussian Splatting (4DGS) has revolutionized high-fidelity dynamic reconstruction, safeguarding the intellectual property of these assets remains an open challenge. Conventional steganographic techniques often neglect the underlying kinematic manifolds, triggering non-physical artifacts such as severe temporal flickering and "FVD collapse". To address this, we propose \textbf{4D-GSW}, a kinematic-aware watermarking framework designed to embed robust copyright information while preserving high spatio-temporal consistency. Unlike prior 4D steganography that primarily focuses on opacity-guided invisibility, our approach explicitly addresses the physical coherence of motion trajectories. We introduce a \textbf{Spatio-Temporal Curvature (STC)} metric to identify "Dynamic Instants," adaptively gating watermark gradient injection to shield critical motion manifolds from non-physical perturbations. To ensure global coherence across complex deformations, we formulate a joint \textbf{HMM-MRF energy minimization} model that synchronizes watermark phases within both temporal trajectories and spatial neighborhoods. Furthermore, an \textbf{anisotropic gradient routing} mechanism ensures that watermark embedding remains strictly decoupled from photometric reconstruction fidelity. Extensive experiments have demonstrated the superior performance of our method in robustly hiding watermarks while resisting various attacks and maintaining high rendering quality and spatiotemporal consistency.

摘要：雖然4D高斯噴濺（4DGS）已經徹底改變了高保真動態重建，但保護這些資產的知識產權仍然是一個未解的挑戰。傳統的隱寫術技術往往忽視了潛在的運動流形，導致非物理性伪影，如嚴重的時間閃爍和「FVD崩潰」。為了解決這個問題，我們提出了\textbf{4D-GSW}，一個運動感知水印框架，旨在嵌入穩健的版權信息，同時保持高的時空一致性。與以往主要關注不透明度引導隱形的4D隱寫術不同，我們的方法明確解決了運動軌跡的物理一致性。我們引入了一個\textbf{時空曲率（STC）}度量來識別「動態瞬間」，自適應地調節水印梯度注入，以保護關鍵的運動流形免受非物理擾動。為了確保在複雜變形中的全局一致性，我們制定了一個聯合\textbf{HMM-MRF能量最小化}模型，該模型在時間軌跡和空間鄰域內同步水印階段。此外，一個\textbf{各向異性梯度路由}機制確保水印嵌入與光度重建的保真度嚴格解耦。大量實驗已經證明我們的方法在穩健地隱藏水印的同時，抵抗各種攻擊並保持高渲染質量和時空一致性方面的優越性能。

##### **Meta-Soft: Leveraging Composable Meta-Tokens for Context-Preserving KV Cache Compression**
2605.22337v1 by Wei Luo, Yi Huang, Songchen Ma, Huanyu Qu, Jiang Cai, Mingkun Xu

The KV cache used in large language models has linearly growing time complexity, so LLMs face memory blow-up and reduced decoding efficiency when they process long contexts.Current KV Cache eviction has become an important research direction; however, existing methods based on fixed Soft Tokens (e.g., Judge Q) rely on a static parameter set as the query to evaluate the importance of KV pairs, so they cannot adapt dynamically to different input prompts, and they cannot precisely capture complex and changing task relevance.Also, evicted KV pairs are discarded permanently, so this causes irreversible information loss and context breaks. To address this problem, we propose Meta-Soft, a dynamic compression framework based on probe-driven context integration. Specifically, we build a meta-library with a learnable orthogonal basis matrix $\mathcal{L}$, and we use a selector network with Gumbel-Softmax to produce differentiable sparse combination weights, so we dynamically synthesize the most targeted $k$ Soft Tokens from the input prompt features.We append these Soft Tokens to the end of the input sequence to probe key information. We also introduce an attention-flow based integration mechanism, which redistributes the semantic information of removed tokens into retained tokens, and this keeps the dropped context information effectively.Experiments on multiple datasets show that our method outperforms existing state-of-the-art eviction methods and provides a new solution for KV Cache compression.

摘要：大型語言模型中使用的KV快取具有線性增長的時間複雜度，因此LLMs在處理長上下文時面臨記憶體膨脹和解碼效率降低的問題。目前的KV快取驅逐已成為一個重要的研究方向；然而，基於固定軟性標記（例如Judge Q）的現有方法依賴於一組靜態參數作為查詢來評估KV對的重要性，因此它們無法根據不同的輸入提示動態適應，也無法準確捕捉複雜和變化的任務相關性。此外，被驅逐的KV對會永久丟棄，這會導致不可逆的信息損失和上下文中斷。為了解決這個問題，我們提出了Meta-Soft，一種基於探針驅動的上下文整合的動態壓縮框架。具體而言，我們建立了一個具有可學習正交基矩陣$\mathcal{L}$的元庫，並使用帶有Gumbel-Softmax的選擇器網絡生成可微分的稀疏組合權重，因此我們從輸入提示特徵中動態合成最具針對性的$k$個軟性標記。我們將這些軟性標記附加到輸入序列的末尾，以探測關鍵信息。我們還引入了一種基於注意力流的整合機制，將移除標記的語義信息重新分配到保留標記中，這樣可以有效保持丟棄的上下文信息。在多個數據集上的實驗顯示，我們的方法優於現有的最先進驅逐方法，並為KV快取壓縮提供了一個新解決方案。

##### **SepsisAI Orchestrator: A Containerized and Scalable Platform for Deploying AI Models and Real-Time Monitoring in Early Sepsis Detection**
2605.22331v1 by Santiago Ospitia, John Sanabria, John Garcia-Henao

Despite strong predictive results in the clinical machine learning literature, the translation of these models into bedside use remains limited by systems-level barriers: heterogeneous data representations, the absence of standardized deployment workflows, and a mismatch between research prototypes and the concurrency and latency requirements of hospital environments. We present the SepsisAI-Orchestrator, an open-source modular platform that addresses this deployment gap for early sepsis detection. The platform integrates HL7 FHIR-inspired Clinical Document Architecture (CDA) preprocessing, NoSQL storage, a containerized LightGBM classifier served via REST APIs, and a Streamlit clinical dashboard, orchestrated with Docker and Kubernetes. A previously validated LightGBM model (F1 0.87-0.94 on PhysioNet 2019) is reused without modification; the contribution lies in the surrounding infrastructure and its empirical characterization under load. Using k6 with 50-1000 concurrent virtual users, we find that replica count must be matched to the physical CPU thread count of the host: scaling from 3 to 12 replicas on a 12-thread CPU reduces p95 latency from 3.3s to 1.41s (57.3% reduction) and eliminates all request failures, while over-provisioning to 24 or 48 replicas degrades performance due to scheduler contention. To our knowledge this U-shaped scaling behavior has not been quantified previously for clinical AI inference workloads. We do not claim prospective clinical validation. Source code and deployment manifests are available at https://github.com/nucleusai/sepsisai-orchestrator.

摘要：儘管臨床機器學習文獻中有強大的預測結果，但這些模型轉化為臨床應用仍然受到系統層級障礙的限制：異質數據表示、缺乏標準化的部署工作流程，以及研究原型與醫院環境的並發性和延遲要求之間的不匹配。我們提出了SepsisAI-Orchestrator，一個開源的模組化平台，旨在解決早期敗血症檢測的部署差距。該平台整合了受HL7 FHIR啟發的臨床文檔架構（CDA）預處理、NoSQL存儲、通過REST API提供的容器化LightGBM分類器，以及Streamlit臨床儀表板，並使用Docker和Kubernetes進行協調。先前經過驗證的LightGBM模型（在PhysioNet 2019上的F1為0.87-0.94）未經修改地重用；貢獻在於周邊基礎設施及其在負載下的實證特徵。使用k6進行50-1000個並發虛擬用戶的測試，我們發現副本數量必須與主機的物理CPU線程數量相匹配：在12線程CPU上將副本數量從3擴展到12，將p95延遲從3.3秒降低到1.41秒（減少57.3%），並消除了所有請求失敗，而過度配置到24或48個副本則因調度器競爭而降低性能。據我們所知，這種U型擴展行為之前尚未對臨床AI推理工作負載進行量化。我們不聲稱有前瞻性的臨床驗證。源代碼和部署清單可在https://github.com/nucleusai/sepsisai-orchestrator獲得。

##### **Benchmarking Autonomous Agents against Temporal, Spatial, and Semantic Evasions**
2605.22321v1 by Jianan Ma, Xiaohu Du, Ruixiao Lin, Yaoxiang Bian, Jialuo Chen, Jingyi Wang, Xiaofang Yang, Shiwen Cui, Changhua Meng, Xinhao Deng, Zhen Wang

As autonomous agents (e.g., OpenClaw) increasingly operate with deep system-level privileges to execute complex tasks, they introduce severe, unmitigated security risks. Current vulnerability analyses overwhelmingly focus on single-turn, stateless behaviors, overlooking the expanded attack surface inherent in stateful, multi-turn interactions and dynamic tool invocations. In this paper, we propose a novel, multi-dimensional evasion framework targeting LLM-based agent systems. We introduce three stealthy attack vectors: (1) Temporal evasion, which fragments malicious payloads across sequential interaction turns; (2) Spatial evasion, which conceals payloads within complex external artifacts that evade standard LLM parsing mechanisms; and (3) Semantic evasion, which obscures malicious intents beneath benign contextual noise. To systematically quantify these threats, we construct A3S-Bench, a comprehensive benchmark comprising 2,254 real-world agent execution trajectories. Evaluating a standard agent framework separately integrated with 10 mainstream LLM backbones against 20 practical threat scenarios, we demonstrate that our evasion framework elevates the average risk trigger rate from a 28.3\% baseline to 52.6\%. These findings reveal systemic, architecture-level vulnerabilities in current autonomous agent systems that existing defenses fail to address, highlighting an urgent need for defense mechanisms tailored to the unique threats.

摘要：隨著自主代理（例如 OpenClaw）越來越多地以深層系統級特權運行以執行複雜任務，它們引入了嚴重且未減輕的安全風險。當前的漏洞分析主要集中在單輪的無狀態行為上，忽略了狀態性、多輪互動和動態工具調用中固有的擴展攻擊面。在本文中，我們提出了一種針對基於 LLM 的代理系統的新穎多維逃避框架。我們引入了三個隱蔽的攻擊向量：（1）時間逃避，將惡意有效載荷分散在連續的互動回合中；（2）空間逃避，將有效載荷隱藏在複雜的外部工件中，以避開標準 LLM 解析機制；（3）語義逃避，將惡意意圖掩蓋在良性上下文噪聲之下。為了系統性地量化這些威脅，我們構建了 A3S-Bench，一個包含 2,254 條真實世界代理執行軌跡的綜合基準。對標準代理框架進行評估，該框架分別與 10 個主流 LLM 主幹集成，針對 20 個實際威脅場景，我們證明我們的逃避框架將平均風險觸發率從 28.3\% 的基線提升至 52.6\%。這些發現揭示了當前自主代理系統中的系統性、架構級漏洞，而現有的防禦措施未能解決這些問題，突顯出針對獨特威脅的防禦機制的迫切需求。

##### **Pattern-and-root inflectional morphology: the Arabic broken plural**
2605.22310v1 by Alexis Amid Neme, Eric Laporte

We present a substantially implemented model of description of the inflectional morphology of Arabic nouns, with special attention to the management of dictionaries and other language resources by Arabic-speaking linguists. The breakthrough lies in the reversal of the traditional root-and-pattern Semitic model into pattern-and-root, giving precedence to patterns over roots. Our model includes broken plurals (BPs), i.e. plurals formed by modifying the stem. It is based on the traditional notions of root and pattern of Semitic morphology. However, as compared to traditional Arabic morphology, it keeps the formal description of inflection separate from that of derivation and semantics. As traditional Arabic dictionaries, the updatable dictionary is structured in lexical entries for lemmas, and the reference spelling is fully diacritized. In our model, morphological analysis of Arabic text is performed directly with a dictionary of words and without morphophonological rules. Our taxonomy for noun inflection is simple, orderly and detailed. We simplify the taxonomy of singular patterns by specifying vowel quantity as v or vv, and ignoring vowel quality. Root alternations and orthographical variations are encoded independently from patterns and in a factual way, without deep roots or morphophonological or orthographical rules. Nouns with a triliteral BP are classified according to 22 patterns subdivided into 90 classes, and nouns with a quadriliteral BP according to 3 patterns subdivided into 70 classes. These 160 classes become 300 inflectional classes when we take into account inflectional variations that affect only the singular. We provide a straightforward encoding scheme that we applied to 3 200 entries of BP nouns.

摘要：我們提出了一個實質實現的阿拉伯名詞屈折形態描述模型，特別關注阿拉伯語言學家對字典和其他語言資源的管理。這一突破在於將傳統的根與模式的閃米特模型反轉為模式與根，優先考慮模式而非根。我們的模型包括破碎複數（BPs），即通過修改詞幹形成的複數。它基於閃米特形態學的傳統根與模式概念。然而，與傳統阿拉伯形態學相比，它將屈折的形式描述與派生和語義的描述分開。與傳統阿拉伯字典相似，可更新的字典以詞條的詞彙條目結構化，參考拼寫完全加上變音符號。在我們的模型中，阿拉伯文本的形態分析是直接使用單詞字典進行的，而不使用形態音位規則。我們的名詞屈折分類法簡單、有序且詳細。我們通過將元音數量指定為v或vv，並忽略元音質量，簡化了單數模式的分類法。根的變化和正字法變異獨立於模式進行編碼，並以事實的方式呈現，無需深入的根或形態音位或正字法規則。具有三音節破碎複數的名詞根據22種模式劃分為90個類別，而具有四音節破碎複數的名詞根據3種模式劃分為70個類別。當我們考慮僅影響單數的屈折變化時，這160個類別變成300個屈折類別。我們提供了一個簡單的編碼方案，應用於3,200個破碎複數名詞條目。

##### **One LR Doesn't Fit All: Heavy-Tail Guided Layerwise Learning Rates for LLMs**
2605.22297v1 by Di He, Songjun Tu, Keyu Wang, Lu Yin, Shiwei Liu

Learning rate configuration is a fundamental aspect of modern deep learning. The prevailing practice of applying a uniform learning rate across all layers overlooks the structural heterogeneity of Transformers, potentially limiting their effectiveness as the backbone of Large Language Models (LLMs). In this paper, we introduce Layerwise Learning Rate (LLR), an adaptive scheme that assigns distinct learning rates to individual Transformer layers. Our method is grounded in Heavy-Tailed Self-Regularization (HT-SR) theory, which characterizes the empirical spectral density (ESD) of weight correlation matrices to quantify heavy-tailedness. Layers with weaker heavy-tailedness are assigned larger learning rates to accelerate their training, while layers with stronger heavy-tailedness receive smaller learning rates. By tailoring learning rates in this manner, LLR promotes balanced training across layers, leading to faster convergence and improved generalization. Extensive experiments across architectures (from LLaMA to GPT-nano), optimizers (AdamW and Muon), and parameter scales (60M-1B) demonstrate that LLR achieves up to 1.5x training speedup and outperforms baselines, notably raising average zero-shot accuracy from 47.09% to 49.02%. A key advantage of LLR is its low tuning overhead: it transfers nearly optimal LR settings directly from the uniform baseline. Code is available at https://github.com/hed-ucas/Layer-wise-Learning-Rate.

摘要：學習率配置是現代深度學習的一個基本方面。對所有層應用統一學習率的普遍做法忽視了Transformer的結構異質性，可能限制了它們作為大型語言模型（LLMs）骨幹的有效性。在本文中，我們介紹了逐層學習率（LLR），這是一種自適應方案，為個別Transformer層分配不同的學習率。我們的方法基於重尾自正則化（HT-SR）理論，該理論通過量化重尾性來表徵權重相關矩陣的經驗譜密度（ESD）。重尾性較弱的層被分配較大的學習率以加速其訓練，而重尾性較強的層則接收較小的學習率。通過這種方式量身定制學習率，LLR促進了層之間的平衡訓練，導致更快的收斂和改進的泛化。對各種架構（從LLaMA到GPT-nano）、優化器（AdamW和Muon）以及參數規模（60M-1B）的廣泛實驗表明，LLR實現了高達1.5倍的訓練加速，並且超越了基準，顯著將平均零-shot準確率從47.09%提高到49.02%。LLR的一個主要優勢是其低調整開銷：它幾乎直接從統一基準轉移了最佳學習率設置。代碼可在https://github.com/hed-ucas/Layer-wise-Learning-Rate獲得。

##### **SciCore-Mol: Augmenting Large Language Models with Pluggable Molecular Cognition Modules**
2605.22287v1 by Yuxuan Chen, Changwei Lv, Yunduo Xiao, Zhongjing Du, Daquan Zhou, Yukun Yan, Zheni Zeng, Zhiyuan Liu

Large Language Models (LLMs) are central to the one-for-all intelligent paradigm, but they face a fundamental challenge when dealing with heterogeneous scientific data such as molecules: the inherent gap between discrete linguistic symbols and topological molecular or continuous reaction data leads to significant information loss and semantic noise in text-based reasoning. We propose SciCore-Mol, a modular framework that bridges this gap through three deeply integrated pluggable cognitive modules: a topology-aware perception module, a latent diffusion-based molecular generation module, and a reaction-aware reasoning module. Each module is coupled to the LLM backbone through learned representation interfaces, enabling richer information exchange than is possible with text-only tool feedback. Our experiments on diverse chemical tasks demonstrate that SciCore-Mol achieves strong comprehensive performance across molecular understanding, generation, reaction prediction, and general chemistry knowledge, with an 8B-parameter open-source system that is competitive with and in several dimensions surpasses proprietary large models. This work provides a systematic blueprint for equipping LLMs with scientific expertise through decoupled, pluggable, and flexibly orchestrated modules, with direct implications for drug design, chemical synthesis, and broader scientific discovery.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）在一體化智能範式中占據核心地位，但在處理異質科學數據（如分子）時面臨根本挑戰：離散語言符號與拓撲分子或連續反應數據之間的固有差距導致文本推理中的顯著信息損失和語義噪聲。我們提出了SciCore-Mol，一個模組化框架，通過三個深度集成的可插拔認知模組來彌合這一差距：一個拓撲感知感知模組、一個基於潛在擴散的分子生成模組，以及一個反應感知推理模組。每個模組都通過學習的表示接口與LLM主幹相連，實現比僅依賴文本工具反饋更豐富的信息交換。我們在多樣的化學任務上的實驗表明，SciCore-Mol在分子理解、生成、反應預測和一般化學知識方面實現了強大的綜合性能，並且這個擁有8B參數的開源系統在多個維度上與專有大型模型競爭並超越它們。這項工作為通過解耦、可插拔和靈活協調的模組為LLMs提供科學專業知識提供了一個系統性的藍圖，對藥物設計、化學合成和更廣泛的科學發現具有直接影響。

#### Abstracts
##### **MOSS: Self-Evolution through Source-Level Rewriting in Autonomous Agent Systems**
2605.22794v1 by Qianshu Cai, Yonggang Zhang, Xianzhang Jia, Wei Xue, Jun Song, Xinmei Tian, Yike Guo

Autonomous agentic systems are largely static after deployment: they do not learn from user interactions, and recurring failures persist until the next human-driven update ships a fix. Self-evolving agents have emerged in response, but all confine evolution to text-mutable artifacts -- skill files, prompt configurations, memory schemas, workflow graphs -- and leave the agent harness untouched. Since routing, hook ordering, state invariants, and dispatch live in code rather than in any text artifact, an entire class of structural failure is physically unreachable from the text layer. We argue that source-level adaptation is a fundamentally more general medium: it is Turing-complete, a strict superset of every text-mutable scope, takes effect deterministically rather than through base-model compliance, and does not erode under long-context drift. We present MOSS, a system that performs self-rewriting at the source level on production agentic substrates. Each evolution is anchored to an automatically curated batch of production-failure evidence and proceeds through a deterministic multi-stage pipeline; code modification is delegated to a pluggable external coding-agent CLI while MOSS retains stage ordering and verdicts. Candidates are verified by replaying the batch against the candidate image in ephemeral trial workers, then promoted via user-consent-gated, in-place container swap with health-probe-gated rollback. On OpenClaw, MOSS lifts a four-task mean grader score from 0.25 to 0.61 in a single cycle without human intervention.

摘要：自主代理系統在部署後基本上是靜態的：它們不會從用戶互動中學習，且重複的失敗會持續存在，直到下一次人為驅動的更新發佈修復。自我進化的代理隨之出現，但所有的進化都限於文本可變的工件——技能檔案、提示配置、記憶架構、工作流程圖——並且不觸及代理的框架。由於路由、掛鉤順序、狀態不變量和調度都存在於代碼中，而不是任何文本工件中，整個結構性失敗類別在文本層面上是物理上無法到達的。我們主張源級適應是一種根本上更通用的媒介：它是圖靈完備的，是每個文本可變範疇的嚴格超集，具有確定性效果，而不是通過基礎模型的合規性來實現，並且在長期上下文漂移下不會退化。我們提出了MOSS，一個在生產代理基底上進行源級自我重寫的系統。每次進化都依賴於自動策劃的生產失敗證據批次，並通過確定性的多階段管道進行；代碼修改委託給可插拔的外部編碼代理CLI，而MOSS保留階段順序和裁決。候選者通過在短暫的試驗工作者中重放批次以驗證候選映像，然後通過用戶同意的就地容器交換進行提升，並進行健康探測的回滾。在OpenClaw上，MOSS在單個周期內將四任務平均評分從0.25提升到0.61，無需人為干預。

##### **Understanding Data Temporality Impact on Large Language Models Pre-training**
2605.22769v1 by Pilchen Hippolyte, Fabre Romain, Signe Talla Franck, Perez Patrick, Grave Edouard

Large language models (LLMs) are typically trained on shuffled corpora, yielding models whose knowledge is frozen at train time and whose temporal grounding remains poorly understood. In this work, we study the impact of pre-training dynamics on the acquisition of time-sensitive factual knowledge, focusing specifically on data ordering. Our main contributions are twofold. First, we introduce a comprehensive benchmark of over 7,000 temporally grounded questions and an evaluation protocol that enables analysis of whether models correctly associate facts with their corresponding time periods. Second, we pretrain 6B-parameter models on temporally ordered Common Crawl snapshots and compare them against standard shuffled pre-training. Our results show that sequentially trained models match shuffled baselines on general language understanding and common knowledge while consistently exhibiting more up-to-date and temporally precise knowledge. Temporally ordered pre-training yields improved factual freshness, while shuffled pre-training peaks on older data, possibly due to increased factual repetition. These findings, along with the release of our code at https://github.com/kyutai-labs/kairos , checkpoints, and datasets at https://huggingface.co/collections/kyutai/kairos provide a foundation for future research on continual learning for LLMs.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）通常在隨機排列的語料庫上進行訓練，產生的模型其知識在訓練時被凍結，且其時間基礎仍然不甚了解。<lb/>在本研究中，我們探討了預訓練動態對於獲取時間敏感事實知識的影響，特別關注數據排序。<lb/>我們的主要貢獻有兩個方面。<lb/>首先，我們引入了一個包含超過7,000個時間基礎問題的綜合基準，以及一個評估協議，使得可以分析模型是否正確將事實與其對應的時間段關聯起來。<lb/>其次，我們在時間排序的Common Crawl快照上預訓練了6B參數模型，並將其與標準的隨機預訓練進行比較。<lb/>我們的結果顯示，按順序訓練的模型在一般語言理解和常識上與隨機基準相匹配，同時持續展現出更為最新和時間上精確的知識。<lb/>時間排序的預訓練提高了事實的新鮮度，而隨機預訓練則在舊數據上達到高峰，這可能是由於事實重複的增加。<lb/>這些發現，以及我們的代碼在 https://github.com/kyutai-labs/kairos 、檢查點和數據集在 https://huggingface.co/collections/kyutai/kairos 的發布，為未來對LLMs的持續學習研究提供了基礎。

##### **Advancing Mathematics Research with AI-Driven Formal Proof Search**
2605.22763v1 by George Tsoukalas, Anton Kovsharov, Sergey Shirobokov, Anja Surina, Moritz Firsching, Gergely Bérczi, Francisco J. R. Ruiz, Arun Suggala, Adam Zsolt Wagner, Eric Wieser, Lei Yu, Aja Huang, Miklós Z. Large language models (LLMs) increasingly excel at mathematical reasoning, but their unreliability limits their utility in mathematics research. ##### **ChronoMedKG: A Temporally-Grounded Biomedical Knowledge Graph and Benchmark for Clinical Reasoning**
2605.22734v1 by Md Shamim Ahmed, Farzaneh Firoozbakht, Lukas Galke Poech, Jan Baumbach, Richard Röttger

Biomedical knowledge graphs (KGs) treat disease associations as static facts, but temporal information is crucial for clinical reasoning, e.g., a symptom diagnostic of one disease at age 3 may imply a different disease at age 13. Existing KGs such as PrimeKG, Hetionet, and iKraph do not encode when a finding becomes clinically relevant over the course of a disease. This limits their usefulness for longitudinal clinical reasoning and retrieval augmentation.
  We introduce ChronoMedKG, a temporal biomedical knowledge graph that contains 460,497 evidence-linked triples (filtered from 13M raw extractions) covering 13,431 diseases. Each association is tied to temporal components like onset window or progression stage, which are backed by PMID-traceable evidence and a multi-signal credibility score. The graph is constructed through a disease-autonomous multi-agent pipeline in which multiple frontier LLMs independently extract knowledge from PubMed and PMC literature. Only those relations are kept that are supported by multi-model consensus, survive credibility filtering, as well as ontology alignment.
  ChronoMedKG scored 92.7% agreement against Orphadata and adds temporal grounding for 6,250 diseases absent from HPOA, Orphadata, and Phenopackets, including 1,657 Orphanet-coded rare diseases. We further introduce ChronoTQA, a benchmark of 3,341 questions across eight task types (six temporal plus two static controls), with a 12-question supplementary probe. Frontier LLMs lose roughly 30 points moving from static to temporal questions; ChronoMedKG retrieval rescues 47-65% of their long-tail failures, against 17-29% for HPOA-RAG. As such, ChronoMedKG provides a crucial temporal axis for retrieval-augmented clinical systems that was previously absent.

摘要：生物醫學知識圖譜（KGs）將疾病關聯視為靜態事實，但時間信息對於臨床推理至關重要，例如，3歲時診斷為某種疾病的症狀可能在13歲時暗示另一種疾病。現有的KGs，如PrimeKG、Hetionet和iKraph，並未編碼在疾病過程中何時發現變得臨床相關。這限制了它們在縱向臨床推理和檢索增強方面的實用性。<lb/>
我們介紹ChronoMedKG，一個包含460,497個證據鏈接三元組的時間生物醫學知識圖譜（從1300萬個原始提取中過濾而來），涵蓋13,431種疾病。每個關聯都與時間組件相關，如發病窗口或進展階段，這些都由PMID可追溯的證據和多信號可信度分數支持。該圖譜是通過一個疾病自主的多代理管道構建的，其中多個前沿LLMs獨立從PubMed和PMC文獻中提取知識。僅保留那些得到多模型共識支持、經過可信度過濾以及本體對齊的關係。<lb/>
ChronoMedKG在Orphadata上得分92.7%的一致性，並為6,250種在HPOA、Orphadata和Phenopackets中缺失的疾病提供了時間基礎，包括1,657種Orphanet編碼的罕見疾病。我們進一步介紹ChronoTQA，一個涵蓋八種任務類型（六種時間性加兩種靜態控制）的3,341個問題基準，並附有12個問題的補充探測。前沿LLMs在靜態問題轉向時間性問題時大約損失30分；ChronoMedKG檢索挽救了47-65%的長尾失敗，而HPOA-RAG則為17-29%。因此，ChronoMedKG為增強檢索的臨床系統提供了一個至關重要的時間軸，這在之前是缺失的。

##### **AnyMo: Geometry-Aware Setup-Agnostic Modeling of Human Motion in the Wild**
2605.22715v1 by Baiyu Chen, Zechen Li, Wilson Wongso, Lihuan Li, Xiachong Lin, Hao Xue, Benjamin Tag, Flora Salim

As wearable and mobile devices become increasingly embedded in daily life, they offer a practical way to continuously sense human motion in the wild. But inertial signals are highly dependent on the sensing setup, including body location, mounting position, sensor orientation, device hardware, and sampling protocol. This setup dependence makes it difficult to learn motion representations that transfer across devices and datasets, and limits the broader use of wearable IMUs beyond closed-set recognition. We introduce AnyMo, a geometry-aware framework for setup-agnostic human motion modeling. AnyMo uses physics-grounded IMU simulation over dense body-surface placements to generate diverse and plausible synthetic signals, pre-trains a graph encoder from paired synthetic placement views and masked partial observations, tokenizes multi-position IMU into full-body motion tokens, and aligns these tokens with an LLM for motion-language understanding. We evaluate AnyMo on three complementary tasks: zero-shot activity recognition across 14 unseen downstream datasets, cross-modal retrieval, and wearable IMU motion captioning, where it improves average Accuracy/F1/R@2 by 11.7\%/11.6\%/22.6\% on HAR, increases zero-shot IMU-to-text and text-to-IMU retrieval MRR by 15.9\% and 28.6\%, respectively, and improves zero-shot captioning BERT-F1 by 18.8\%. These results support AnyMo as a generalist model for wearable motion understanding in the wild. Project page: https://baiyuchen.com/project/AnyMo.

摘要：隨著可穿戴和移動設備越來越深入日常生活，它們提供了一種實用的方法來持續感知人類在自然環境中的運動。<lb/>但是，慣性信號高度依賴於感測設置，包括身體位置、安裝位置、感測器方向、設備硬體和取樣協議。<lb/>這種設置依賴性使得學習能夠跨設備和數據集轉移的運動表示變得困難，並限制了可穿戴IMU在封閉集識別之外的更廣泛應用。<lb/>我們介紹了AnyMo，一個對設置無關的人類運動建模的幾何感知框架。<lb/>AnyMo使用基於物理的IMU模擬，通過密集的身體表面放置來生成多樣且合理的合成信號，從配對的合成放置視圖和遮蔽的部分觀察中預訓練圖編碼器，將多位置IMU標記為全身運動標記，並將這些標記與LLM對齊以實現運動-語言理解。<lb/>我們在三個互補任務上評估AnyMo：在14個未見的下游數據集上進行零樣本活動識別，跨模態檢索，以及可穿戴IMU運動標註，在HAR上平均準確率/F1/R@2提高了11.7\%/11.6\%/22.6\%，零樣本IMU到文本和文本到IMU檢索的MRR分別提高了15.9\%和28.6\%，並且零樣本標註的BERT-F1提高了18.8\%。<lb/>這些結果支持AnyMo作為一個通用模型，用於在自然環境中理解可穿戴運動。<lb/>項目頁面：https://baiyuchen.com/project/AnyMo。

##### **Scout-Assisted Planning for Heterogeneous Robot Teams under Partially Known Environments**
2605.22693v1 by Hoang-Dung Bui, Abhish Khanal, Raihan Islam Arnob, Gregory J. Stein

Autonomous robot teams navigating partially known environments face costly backtracking when ground robots encounter blocked roads that are only revealed upon physical traversal. We address this with Scout-Assisted Planning, a heterogeneous planning framework in which scouting Unmanned Aerial Vehicles proactively gather environmental information to improve Unmanned Ground Vehicle navigation. To focus scouting on the most consequential edges, we propose Information Gain-based Action Pruning, which scores candidate scouting actions by their expected impact on ground robot behavior. Since exact Information Gain-based Action Pruning computation is prohibitively expensive, we develop a Graph Neural Network based model that predicts information gain values directly from graph structure and belief state, reducing planning time to real-time levels without sacrificing solution quality. Experiments across three environment types show that SAP with Information Gain Action Pruning reduces ground robot travel cost by 31.9--37.7% over the Canadian Traveler Problem baseline, and outperforms proximity-based scouting guidance by an additional 8--14%, confirming that principled information-gain-guided scouting is both more effective and computationally feasible for real-world deployment

摘要：自主機器人團隊在部分已知環境中導航時，當地面機器人遇到被封鎖的道路時，會面臨昂貴的回溯成本，這些封鎖的道路只有在實際通行後才能揭示。我們通過偵查輔助規劃來解決這一問題，這是一種異質規劃框架，其中偵查無人機主動收集環境信息，以改善無人地面車輛的導航。為了將偵查集中在最重要的邊緣上，我們提出了基於信息增益的行動修剪，通過預期對地面機器人行為的影響來評分候選偵查行動。由於精確的基於信息增益的行動修剪計算成本過高，我們開發了一種基於圖神經網絡的模型，該模型直接從圖結構和信念狀態預測信息增益值，將規劃時間減少到實時水平而不犧牲解決方案質量。三種環境類型的實驗顯示，使用基於信息增益的行動修剪的SAP比加拿大旅行者問題基線降低了31.9%到37.7%的地面機器人旅行成本，並且比基於接近度的偵查指導額外提高了8%到14%的性能，證實了有原則的信息增益指導的偵查在現實世界部署中既更有效又計算上可行。

##### **Forecasting Scientific Progress with Artificial Intelligence**
2605.22681v1 by Sean Wu, Pan Lu, Yupeng Chen, Jonathan Bragg, Yutaro Yamada, Peter Clark, David Clifton, Philip Torr, James Zou, Junchi Yu

Artificial intelligence (AI) is increasingly embedded in scientific discovery, yet whether it can anticipate scientific progress remains unclear. To study this question, we introduce a temporally grounded evaluation framework for forecasting scientific progress under controlled knowledge constraints. We present CUSP (Cutoff-conditioned Unseen Scientific Progress), a multi-disciplinary and event-level benchmark that evaluates scientific forecasting in AI systems through feasibility assessment, mechanistic reasoning, generative solution design, and temporal prediction. Across 4,760 scientific events, we observe systematic and domain-dependent limitations in current frontier models. While models can identify plausible research directions from competing candidates, they fail to reliably predict whether scientific advances will be realized and systematically misestimate when they will occur. Performance is highly heterogeneous across domains, with the timing of AI progress more predictable than advances in biology, chemistry, and physics. Performance is largely insensitive to whether events occur before or after the training cutoff, suggesting these limitations cannot be explained solely by knowledge exposure in training data. Under controlled information access, additional pre-cutoff knowledge improves performance but does not close the gap to full-information settings, which becomes more pronounced for high-citation advances. Models also exhibit systematic overconfidence and strong response biases, indicating unreliable uncertainty estimation. Taken together, current AI systems fall short as predictive tools for scientific progress. Access to prior knowledge does not translate into reliable forecasting, and performance benefits more from post-event information than from forward-looking prediction.

摘要：人工智慧（AI）越來越多地嵌入科學發現中，但它是否能預測科學進展仍不清楚。為了研究這個問題，我們引入了一個基於時間的評估框架，用於在受控知識約束下預測科學進展。我們提出了 CUSP（Cutoff-conditioned Unseen Scientific Progress），這是一個跨學科的事件級基準，通過可行性評估、機制推理、生成解決方案設計和時間預測來評估 AI 系統中的科學預測。在 4,760 個科學事件中，我們觀察到當前前沿模型存在系統性和領域依賴的限制。儘管模型可以從競爭候選者中識別出合理的研究方向，但它們無法可靠地預測科學進展是否會實現，並且系統性地錯誤估計其發生時間。不同領域的表現差異很大，AI 進展的時間預測比生物學、化學和物理學的進展更具可預測性。表現在事件發生在訓練截止之前或之後的情況下大體上不敏感，這表明這些限制不能僅僅通過訓練數據中的知識曝光來解釋。在受控信息訪問下，額外的截止前知識提高了表現，但並未縮小與全信息設置之間的差距，這在高引用的進展中變得更加明顯。模型還表現出系統性的過度自信和強烈的反應偏見，顯示出不可靠的不確定性估計。綜合來看，當前的 AI 系統作為預測科學進展的工具仍然不足。獲取先前的知識並未轉化為可靠的預測，並且表現更受事件後信息的影響，而不是來自前瞻性的預測。

##### **Is Capability a Liability? More Capable Language Models Make Worse Forecasts When It Matters Most**
2605.22672v1 by Nick Merrill, Jaeho Lee, Ezra Karger

We document inverse scaling in LLMs on forecasting problems whose underlying time series exhibit superlinear growth and tail risk of regime change, a structure common in finance and epidemiology. On these tasks, more capable models produce worse distributional forecasts. The pattern appears on ForecastBench-Sim (FBSim), a contamination-free, simulated-world benchmark we release, in forecasting synthetic SIR epidemics with a matched linear control, and replicates in real-world datasets on COVID-19, measles, housing markets, and hyperinflation. A per-quantile decomposition shows the failure concentrates at the upper tail, which more capable models shift upward to track aggressive extrapolations of growth, while the lower tail stays put. A within-family study of Llama-3.1 shows that both model scale and post-training independently contribute to this effect. Domain knowledge does not reliably rescue calibration. This inverse scaling does not appear on single-threshold metrics common in LLM forecasting benchmarks, reversing the sign of the capability--accuracy relationship on identical outputs. Single-threshold scoring at conventional cutoffs misses the upper-tail cost; tail-inclusive scoring reverses the sign of the capability--accuracy relationship on the same outputs. We recommend that LLM forecasting evaluations use continuous (and unbounded) measures of accuracy alongside bounded binary threshold metrics.

摘要：我們記錄了在預測問題中大型語言模型（LLMs）的逆縮放，這些問題的基礎時間序列顯示出超線性增長和政權變更的尾部風險，這種結構在金融和流行病學中很常見。在這些任務中，更強大的模型產生了更差的分佈預測。這一模式出現在我們發布的無污染模擬世界基準ForecastBench-Sim (FBSim)上，該基準在預測合成SIR流行病時，與匹配的線性控制進行比較，並在COVID-19、麻疹、房地產市場和惡性通貨膨脹的真實世界數據集中得到了重現。每個分位數的分解顯示，失敗集中在上尾，更強大的模型將其向上移動，以追蹤增長的激進外推，而下尾則保持不變。對Llama-3.1的家族內研究顯示，模型規模和後訓練獨立地對這一效應有所貢獻。領域知識並不能可靠地改善校準。在大型語言模型預測基準中，這種逆縮放並未出現在單一閾值指標上，反轉了相同輸出上的能力與準確性之間的關係符號。在傳統的截止點進行的單一閾值評分忽略了上尾成本；包含尾部的評分則反轉了相同輸出上的能力與準確性之間的關係符號。我們建議大型語言模型的預測評估使用連續（且無界）準確性度量，並與有界的二元閾值指標一起使用。

##### **More Context, Larger Models, or Moral Knowledge? A Systematic Study of Schwartz Value Detection in Political Texts**
2605.22641v1 by Víctor Yeste, Paolo Rosso

Detecting Schwartz values in political text is difficult because implicit cues often depend on surrounding arguments and fine-grained distinctions between neighboring values. We study when context and explicit moral knowledge help sentence-level value detection. Using the ValuesML/Touch{é} ValueEval format, we compare sentence, window, and full-document inputs; no-RAG and retrieval-augmented settings with a curated moral knowledge base; supervised DeBERTa-v3-base/large encoders; and zero-shot LLMs from 12B to 123B parameters. The results show that more context is not uniformly better: full-document context improves supervised DeBERTa encoders by 3.8--4.8 macro-F1 points over sentence-only input, but does not consistently help zero-shot LLMs. Retrieved moral knowledge is more consistently useful in matched comparisons, improving each tested model family and context condition under early fusion. However, scaling from DeBERTa-v3-base to large and from 12B to larger LLMs does not guarantee gains, and simple early fusion outperforms the tested late-fusion and cross-attention RAG variants for encoders. Per-value analyses show that context and retrieval help most for socially situated or conceptually confusable values. These findings suggest that value-sensitive NLP should evaluate context, knowledge, and model family jointly rather than treating longer inputs or larger models as universal improvements.

摘要：檢測政治文本中的施瓦茨值是困難的，因為隱含的提示通常依賴於周圍的論據和相鄰值之間的細微區別。<lb/>我們研究了何時上下文和明確的道德知識有助於句子級別的價值檢測。<lb/>使用ValuesML/Touch{é} ValueEval格式，我們比較了句子、窗口和完整文檔輸入；無RAG和增強檢索的設置，並使用精心策劃的道德知識庫；監督式DeBERTa-v3-base/large編碼器；以及從12B到123B參數的零-shot LLM。<lb/>結果顯示，更多的上下文並不總是更好：完整文檔上下文使監督式DeBERTa編碼器的宏F1分數比僅使用句子輸入提高了3.8到4.8點，但對零-shot LLM並不總是有幫助。<lb/>檢索到的道德知識在匹配比較中更一致地有用，改善了每個測試模型系列和上下文條件下的早期融合。<lb/>然而，從DeBERTa-v3-base擴展到large，及從12B擴展到更大的LLM並不保證獲得增益，且簡單的早期融合在編碼器中表現優於測試的晚期融合和交叉注意RAG變體。<lb/>逐值分析顯示，上下文和檢索對社會情境或概念上容易混淆的值幫助最大。<lb/>這些發現表明，對於價值敏感的NLP，應該共同評估上下文、知識和模型系列，而不是將更長的輸入或更大的模型視為普遍的改進。

##### **Chinese sensorimotor and embodiment norms for 3,000 lexicalized concepts**
2605.22616v1 by Jing Chen, Gábor Parti, Yin Zhong, Chu-Ren Huang, Marco Marelli

Understanding how conceptual knowledge is grounded in bodily experience, and to what extent machine systems can acquire such knowledge without direct sensorimotor experience, are central questions in both cognitive science and embodied artificial intelligence research. Large-scale normative resources are essential for investigating these questions empirically, yet such resources remain sparse for non-Indo-European languages. We present a novel normative database for 3,000 lexicalized concepts in Mandarin Chinese, comprising 11-dimensional sensorimotor ratings and unidimensional embodiment ratings collected from 378 native Mandarin speakers. The ratings demonstrate high reliability and strong cross-norm validity with existing Chinese resources, each of which covers fewer words and a subset of the 11 sensorimotor dimensions. In a validation study, we tested new variables derived from a theoretically motivated metric, Perceptual Strength of Embodiment (PSE) (Huang et al., 2025), together with seven common composite variables, on lexical decision tasks. The results suggest that PSE-Sensorimotor and Minkowski-3 are the strongest composite predictors of lexical decision performance, capturing the facilitatory effects of sensorimotor information on lexical processing. A further exploratory study showed that sensorimotor ratings are substantially recoverable from purely linguistic representations using simple regression models (mean Spearman r = .62 across dimensions), though recovery varied markedly: visual and auditory dimensions yielded higher correspondence than chemosensory ones. Representational similarity analysis further showed that the relational geometry of the sensorimotor space is also partially recoverable (r = .540), consistent with the view that distributional language use encodes aspects of embodied conceptual structure.

摘要：理解概念知識如何根植於身體經驗，以及機器系統在多大程度上可以獲得這種知識而無需直接的感覺運動經驗，是認知科學和具身人工智慧研究中的核心問題。大規模的規範資源對於實證調查這些問題至關重要，但對於非印歐語言而言，此類資源仍然稀缺。我們提出了一個新穎的規範數據庫，涵蓋了3000個在普通話中的詞彙化概念，包括從378位母語普通話說話者收集的11維感覺運動評分和一維具身評分。這些評分顯示出高可靠性，並與現有的中文資源具有強大的交叉規範有效性，後者每個涵蓋的詞彙數量較少，且僅包含11個感覺運動維度的子集。在一項驗證研究中，我們測試了從理論上動機的度量——具身感知強度（PSE）（Huang et al., 2025）衍生的新變量，以及七個常見的綜合變量，應用於詞彙決策任務。結果表明，PSE-感覺運動和Minkowski-3是詞彙決策表現的最強綜合預測因子，捕捉了感覺運動信息對詞彙處理的促進效應。進一步的探索性研究顯示，感覺運動評分可以從純語言表徵中通過簡單的回歸模型顯著恢復（各維度的平均Spearman r = .62），儘管恢復程度差異顯著：視覺和聽覺維度的對應性高於化學感官維度。表徵相似性分析進一步顯示，感覺運動空間的關係幾何也部分可恢復（r = .540），這與分佈式語言使用編碼具身概念結構某些方面的觀點一致。

##### **Think Thrice Before You Speak: Dual knowledge-enhanced Theory-of-Mind Reasoning for Persuasive Agents**
2605.22602v1 by Minghui Ma, Bin Guo, Runze Yang, Mengqi Chen, Yan Liu, Jingqi Liu, Yahan Pei, Xuehao Ma, Qiuyun Zhang, Zhiwen Yu

Persuasive dialogue requires reasoning about others' latent mental states, a capability known as Theory of Mind (ToM). However, due to reliance on simple prompting strategies and insufficient ToM knowledge, existing LLMs often fail to capture the intrinsic dependencies among mental states, leading to fragmented representations and unstable reasoning. To address these challenges, we introduce the ToM-based Persuasive Dialogue (ToM-PD) task, grounded in the Belief-Desire-Intention (BDI) framework, which explicitly models the sequential dependencies among mental states in multi-turn dialogues. To facilitate research on this task, we construct a large-scale annotated dataset, ToM-based Broad Persuasive Dialogues (ToM-BPD), capturing fine-grained mental states and corresponding persuasive strategies. We further propose Think Thrice Before You Speak (TTBYS), a knowledge-enhanced stepwise reasoning framework that leverages both explicit and implicit prior experiences to improve LLMs' inference of desires, beliefs, and persuasive strategies. Experimental results demonstrate that Qwen3-8B equipped with TTBYS outperforms GPT-5 by 1.20%, 22.80%, and 16.97% in predicting desires, beliefs, and persuasive strategies, respectively. Case studies further show that our approach enhances interpretability and consistency in reasoning.

摘要：說服性對話需要對他人潛在心理狀態進行推理，這一能力被稱為心智理論（Theory of Mind, ToM）。然而，由於依賴簡單的提示策略和不足的心智理論知識，現有的LLM往往無法捕捉心理狀態之間的內在依賴性，導致片段化的表徵和不穩定的推理。為了解決這些挑戰，我們引入了基於心智理論的說服性對話（ToM-PD）任務，該任務基於信念-欲望-意圖（Belief-Desire-Intention, BDI）框架，明確建模多輪對話中心理狀態之間的序列依賴性。為了促進對這一任務的研究，我們構建了一個大規模的標註數據集，基於心智理論的廣泛說服對話（ToM-BPD），捕捉細緻的心理狀態和相應的說服策略。我們進一步提出了在發言前三思（Think Thrice Before You Speak, TTBYS），這是一個增強知識的逐步推理框架，利用明確和隱含的先前經驗來改善LLM對欲望、信念和說服策略的推斷。實驗結果顯示，配備TTBYS的Qwen3-8B在預測欲望、信念和說服策略方面，分別比GPT-5高出1.20%、22.80%和16.97%。案例研究進一步表明，我們的方法增強了推理的可解釋性和一致性。

##### **Case-Aware Medical Image Classification with Multimodal Knowledge Graphs and Reliability-Guided Refinement**
2605.22547v1 by Yiming Xu, Yixuan Liu, Yuhang Zhang, Ling Zheng, Yihan Wang, Qi Song

Deep learning has brought significant progress to medical image classification, yet most existing methods still rely on isolated visual evidence and cannot effectively leverage similar cases or external knowledge. In clinical practice, diagnosis is typically supported by historical similar cases and their associated symptoms. To simulate this diagnostic process, we propose a framework that performs case-aware reasoning using multimodal knowledge graphs for explainable medical image diagnosis. Given an input image, our method constructs a multimodal knowledge graph from adaptively retrieved similar cases, enabling more effective utilization of related samples. We further introduce a knowledge propagation and injection mechanism, where an image-centric Graph Attention Network propagates knowledge semantics to obtain case-based features, followed by a bidirectional cross-modal attention mechanism that injects these features into visual representations for cross-modal alignment. To mitigate noisy retrieval, we design a confidence-calibrated decision refinement scheme that estimates the reliability of each retrieved case by jointly considering prediction confidence and sample similarity, adaptively adjusting its contribution to the final prediction and providing interpretable case-level evidence. Extensive experiments on multiple medical imaging datasets show that our approach consistently outperforms strong baselines, and ablation studies validate the effectiveness of each component. The source code is publicly available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/MKG-CARE-8B7B.

##### **Dynamic Hypergraph Representation Learning for Multivariate Time Series without Prior Knowledge**
2605.22540v1 by Marco Gregnanin, Johannes De Smedt, Giorgio Gnecco, Maurizio Parton

Hypergraphs have the capacity to capture higher-dimensional relationships among entities across various domains, making them a subject of growing interest within the research community for understanding the structure and dynamics of complex systems. However, a key challenge is the derivation of hypergraph representations from time series data in situations where the structure of the hypergraph is limited or absent. In this study, we propose a model that constructs a dynamic hypergraph representation for multivariate time series without relying on prior knowledge of the data. This is achieved by applying community detection to the time series and transforming the resulting communities, obtained through an attention mechanism, into a hypergraph using a clique-based technique. Hypergraph representations are derived from different time series datasets, and the resulting hypergraphs are then used by a Dynamic Hypergraph Attention Convolution Network (DHACN) for multivariate time series predictions. This research advances the field of hypergraph representation by introducing a novel approach that is better suited to uncover high-order relationships without prior knowledge.

##### **LACO: Adaptive Latent Communication for Collaborative Driving**
2605.22504v1 by Tianhao Chen, Yuheng Wu, Dongman Lee

Collaborative driving aims to improve safety and efficiency by enabling connected vehicles to coordinate under partial observability. Recent approaches have evolved from sharing visual features for perception to exchanging language-based reasoning through foundation models for behavioral coordination. Though communicating in language provides intuitive information, it introduces two challenges: high latency caused by autoregressive decoding and information loss caused by compressing rich internal representations into discrete tokens. To address these challenges, we analyze latent communication in collaborative driving under inherent limitations of multi-agent settings. Our analysis reveals agent identity confusion, where direct fusion of latent states entangles decision representations across vehicles. Motivated by this, we propose LACO, a training-free \textbf{LA}tent \textbf{CO}mmunication paradigm that seamlessly adapts pretrained driving models to collaborative settings. LACO introduces Iterative Latent Deliberation (ILD) for latent reasoning, Cross-Horizon Saliency Attribution (CHSA) for communication-efficient information selection, and Structured Semantic Knowledge Distillation (SSKD) to stabilize ego-centric decision making. Closed-loop experiments in CARLA show that LACO notably reduces communication and inference latency while maintaining strong collaborative driving performance.

摘要：協作駕駛旨在透過使連接的車輛在部分可觀察性下協調來提高安全性和效率。最近的方法已經從共享視覺特徵以進行感知演變為通過基礎模型進行基於語言的推理交換，以實現行為協調。雖然用語言進行溝通提供了直觀的信息，但它引入了兩個挑戰：由自回歸解碼引起的高延遲和由於將豐富的內部表示壓縮為離散標記而導致的信息損失。為了解決這些挑戰，我們分析了在多代理設置的固有限制下協作駕駛中的潛在通信。我們的分析揭示了代理身份混淆，其中潛在狀態的直接融合使車輛之間的決策表示交纏在一起。受到此啟發，我們提出了LACO，一種無需訓練的\textbf{LA}tent \textbf{CO}mmunication範式，能夠無縫地將預訓練的駕駛模型適應於協作環境。LACO引入了迭代潛在深思（ILD）用於潛在推理，跨地平線顯著性歸因（CHSA）用於通信高效的信息選擇，以及結構化語義知識蒸餾（SSKD）以穩定自我中心的決策。CARLA中的閉環實驗顯示，LACO顯著減少了通信和推理延遲，同時保持強大的協作駕駛性能。

##### **Compiling Agentic Workflows into LLM Weights: Near-Frontier Quality at Two Orders of Magnitude Less Cost**
2605.22502v1 by Simon Dennis, Rivaan Patil, Kevin Shabahang, Hao Guo

Agent orchestration frameworks have proliferated, collectively exceeding 290,000 GitHub stars across LangGraph, CrewAI, Google ADK, OpenAI Agents SDK, Semantic Kernel, Strands, and LlamaIndex. All follow the same pattern: an external orchestrator above the LLM, injecting instructions and routing decisions every turn. Recent work has shown this architecture is dominated for procedural tasks by simply providing the procedure in a frontier model's system prompt [Dennis et al., 2026a], at the cost of consuming the context window, requiring a frontier model for every conversation, and exposing proprietary procedures to third-party providers. Compiling the procedure into the weights of a small fine-tuned model -- creating a subterranean agent -- should resolve all of these concerns, and prior work (SimpleTOD, FireAct, SynTOD, WorkflowLLM, Agent Lumos) has shown the technique works. Yet developer adoption has overwhelmingly favored orchestration. We identify three perceived barriers and address each empirically across travel booking (14 nodes), Zoom support (14 nodes, product-specific knowledge), and insurance claims (55 nodes, 6 decision hubs).

摘要：代理協調框架已經大量增長，LangGraph、CrewAI、Google ADK、OpenAI Agents SDK、Semantic Kernel、Strands 和 LlamaIndex 的 GitHub 星數總計超過 290,000。所有這些框架都遵循相同的模式：在 LLM 之上有一個外部協調器，每次轉換時注入指令和路由決策。最近的研究顯示，這種架構在程序性任務中占主導地位，只需在前沿模型的系統提示中提供程序 [Dennis et al., 2026a]，但這會消耗上下文窗口，要求每次對話都使用前沿模型，並將專有程序暴露給第三方供應商。將程序編譯進小型微調模型的權重中——創建一個地下代理——應該能解決所有這些問題，而先前的工作（SimpleTOD、FireAct、SynTOD、WorkflowLLM、Agent Lumos）已經顯示這種技術是有效的。然而，開發者的採用卻壓倒性地偏向於協調。我們識別了三個感知的障礙，並在旅行訂票（14 個節點）、Zoom 支援（14 個節點，產品特定知識）和保險索賠（55 個節點，6 個決策中心）中實證解決每一個問題。

##### **KAPPS: A knowledge-based CPPS Architecture for the Circular Factory**
2605.22457v1 by Etienne Hoffmann, Jan-Felix Klein, Sören Weindel, Max Goebels, Sebastian Behrendt, Daniel Hernández, Ratan Bahadur Thapa, Jürgen Fleischer, Kai Furmans, Steffen Staab

While linear manufacturing relies on homogeneous materials and predefined process sequences, circular manufacturing reintroduces used products with heterogeneous and uncertain conditions. This shift demands manufacturing systems capable of handling variable product states, dynamically reconfigurable processes, and the integration of human and machine knowledge. Conventional manufacturing IT architectures, designed for stable structures and deterministic execution, are unable to meet these requirements, as they cannot adequately represent and manage the uniqueness of individual components at runtime. KAPPS incorporates modules for constraint enforcement and event-driven planning, enabling incremental adaptation of execution plans under uncertainty and human-machine knowledge exchange.
