##### **GenAI-Driven Threat Detection with Microsoft Security Copilot**
2605.20896v1 by Scott Freitas, Amir Gharib

Defending against today's increasingly sophisticated cyberattacks requires security analysts to continuously translate evolving attacker tradecraft into detection logic. This places defenders in a reactive posture, requiring constantly updated expertise across an increasingly fragmented security landscape. We introduce the Dynamic Threat Detection Agent (DTDA), an always-on adaptive agent that continuously investigates security incidents across Microsoft Defender to uncover hidden threats and generate explainable detections when attack-story gaps are found. DTDA combines: (1) a unified activity timeline spanning alerts, events, user and entity behavior analytics, and threat intelligence; (2) versioned LLM prompt contracts with schema validation, grounding requirements, bounded retries, and fail-closed suppression; (3) a planner-executor investigation loop that generates attack-specific hypotheses and gathers supporting and refuting evidence; and (4) dynamic alert generation with a context-relevant title, severity, MITRE mappings, remediation guidance, implicated entities, and natural-language attack description. Integrated into Microsoft Security Copilot and deployed across tens of thousands of Defender customers, DTDA operates continuously at industry scale. In a 120-day online evaluation, DTDA achieves 80.1% precision from customer feedback while generating novel alerts for approximately 15% of investigated incidents. In offline evaluation, DTDA recovers hidden malicious activity with 0.78 F1 using GPT-5.4, improving over GPT-4.1 by 0.12 F1 and outperforming the baseline by 0.26 F1 points. Operationally, DTDA processes single-incident investigations end-to-end in a median of 28 minutes at a median token cost of USD 2.04, with a 0.38% job-level failure rate. These results demonstrate that autonomous agents can identify missed malicious activity at a production scale.

摘要：防禦當今日益複雜的網絡攻擊要求安全分析師不斷將不斷演變的攻擊者技術轉化為檢測邏輯。這使得防禦者處於反應狀態，要求在日益分散的安全環境中不斷更新專業知識。我們介紹了動態威脅檢測代理（DTDA），這是一個始終在線的自適應代理，持續調查 Microsoft Defender 中的安全事件，以發現隱藏的威脅並在發現攻擊故事漏洞時生成可解釋的檢測。DTDA 結合了：（1）涵蓋警報、事件、用戶和實體行為分析以及威脅情報的統一活動時間線；（2）具有模式驗證、基準要求、限制重試和失敗關閉抑制的版本化 LLM 提示合約；（3）生成特定攻擊假設並收集支持和反駁證據的規劃-執行調查循環；以及（4）具有上下文相關標題、嚴重性、MITRE 對應、修復指導、相關實體和自然語言攻擊描述的動態警報生成。DTDA 集成於 Microsoft Security Copilot 並部署於數萬個 Defender 客戶中，持續在行業規模上運作。在一項為期 120 天的在線評估中，DTDA 從客戶反饋中實現了 80.1% 的精確度，同時為約 15% 的調查事件生成了新警報。在離線評估中，DTDA 使用 GPT-5.4 恢復隱藏的惡意活動，F1 值為 0.78，較 GPT-4.1 提高了 0.12 F1，並超過基準 0.26 F1 點。在運營上，DTDA 以中位數 28 分鐘的時間處理單一事件調查，平均代幣成本為 2.04 美元，工作層級失敗率為 0.38%。這些結果表明，自主代理可以在生產規模上識別錯過的惡意活動。

##### **VBFDD-Agent for Electric Vehicle Battery Fault Detection and Diagnosis: Descriptive Text Modeling of Battery Digital Signals**
2605.20742v1 by Joey Chan, Zhen Chen, Ershun Pan

With the rapid proliferation of electric vehicles, the safety and reliability of lithium-ion batteries have become critical concerns. Effective anomaly detection is essential for ensuring safe battery operation. However, as battery systems and operating scenarios become increasingly complex, battery fault diagnosis and maintenance require stronger cross-domain adaptability and human-AI collaboration. Traditional fault detection and diagnosis methods are usually designed for specific scenarios and predefined workflows, making them less effective in complex real-world applications.
  To address the scarcity of open-source battery fault report corpora and the lack of unified maintenance knowledge representation, this study proposes a descriptive text modeling approach for battery signal reports. Monitoring signals, statistical features, anomaly records, and state assessment results are transformed into structured and readable natural language descriptions, forming a language corpus for battery health diagnosis and maintenance.
  Based on this corpus, we propose VBFDD-Agent, a vehicle battery fault detection and diagnosis agent for automotive-grade battery systems. VBFDD-Agent integrates descriptive battery-state texts, historical case retrieval, local maintenance manuals, and large language model reasoning to generate structured diagnostic results and maintenance recommendations. Experiments show that the proposed framework can accurately perform anomaly monitoring based on descriptive textual representations and provide flexible, efficient, and actionable maintenance suggestions. Expert evaluation further confirms the practical value of the generated recommendations. Overall, VBFDD-Agent extends traditional battery diagnosis from label prediction to interpretable and maintenance-oriented decision support.

摘要：隨著電動車的快速普及，鋰離子電池的安全性和可靠性已成為關鍵關注點。有效的異常檢測對於確保電池安全運行至關重要。然後，隨著電池系統和操作場景變得越來越複雜，電池故障診斷和維護需要更強的跨領域適應性和人機協作。傳統的故障檢測和診斷方法通常是針對特定場景和預定工作流程設計的，使其在複雜的現實應用中效果不佳。<lb/>為了解決開源電池故障報告語料庫的稀缺性和缺乏統一的維護知識表示，本研究提出了一種電池信號報告的描述性文本建模方法。監控信號、統計特徵、異常記錄和狀態評估結果被轉換為結構化且可讀的自然語言描述，形成一個用於電池健康診斷和維護的語言語料庫。<lb/>基於這個語料庫，我們提出了VBFDD-Agent，一種針對汽車級電池系統的車輛電池故障檢測和診斷代理。VBFDD-Agent整合了描述性電池狀態文本、歷史案例檢索、本地維護手冊和大型語言模型推理，以生成結構化的診斷結果和維護建議。實驗表明，所提出的框架可以基於描述性文本表示準確地執行異常監控，並提供靈活、高效且可行的維護建議。專家評估進一步確認了生成建議的實際價值。總體而言，VBFDD-Agent將傳統電池診斷從標籤預測擴展到可解釋和以維護為導向的決策支持。

##### **On the limits and opportunities of AI reviewers: Reviewing the reviews of Nature-family papers with 45 expert scientists**
2605.20668v1 by Seungone Kim, Dongkeun Yoon, Kiril Gashteovski, Juyoung Suk, Jinheon Baek, Pranjal Aggarwal, Ian Wu, Viktor Zaverkin, Spase Petkoski, Daniel R. Schrider, Ilija Dukovski, Francesco Santini, Biljana Mitreska, Yong Jeong, Kyeongha Kwon, Young Min Sim, Dragana Manasova, Arthur Porto, Biljana Mojsoska, Makoto Takamoto, Marko Shuntov, Ruoqi Liu, Hyunjoo Jenny Lee, Niyazi Ulas Dinç, Yehhyun Jo, Sunkyu Han, Chungwoo Lee, Huishan Li, Esther H. R. Tsai, Ergun Simsek, Khushboo Shafi, Yeonseung Chung, Jihye Park, Aleksandar Shulevski, Henrik Christiansen, Yoosang Son, Elly Knight, Amanda Montoya, Jeongyoun Ahn, Christian Langkammer, Heera Moon, Changwon Yoon, Nikola Stikov, Mooseok Jang, Edward Choi, Junhan Kim, Yeon Sik Jung, Woo Youn Kim, Jae Kyoung Kim, Ishraq Md Anjum, Hyun Uk Kim, Drew Bridges, Carolin Lawrence, Xiang Yue, Alice Oh, Akari Asai, Sean Welleck, Graham Neubig

With the advancement of AI capabilities, AI reviewers are beginning to be deployed in scientific peer review, yet their capability and credibility remain in question: many scientists simply view them as probabilistic systems without the expertise to evaluate research, while other researchers are more optimistic about their readiness without concrete evidence. Understanding what AI reviewers do well, where they fall short, and what challenges remain is essential. However, existing evaluations of AI reviewers have focused on whether their verdicts match human verdicts (e.g., score alignment, acceptance prediction), which is insufficient to characterize their capabilities and limits. In this paper, we close this gap through a large-scale expert annotation study, in which 45 domain scientists in Physical, Biological, and Health Sciences spent 469 hours rating 2,960 individual criticisms (each targeting one specific aspect of a paper) from human-written and AI-generated reviews of 82 Nature-family papers on correctness, significance, and sufficiency of evidence. On a composite of all three dimensions, a reviewing agent powered by GPT-5.2 scores above each paper's top-rated human reviewer (60.0% vs. 48.2%, p = 0.009), while all three AI reviewers (including Gemini 3.0 Pro and Claude Opus 4.5) exceed the lowest-rated human across every dimension. AI reviewers' accurate criticisms are also more often rated significant and well-evidenced, and surface a distinct 26% of issues no human raises. However, AI reviewers overlap far more than humans do (21% vs. 3% for cross-reviewer pairs), and exhibit 16 recurring weaknesses humans do not share, such as limited subfield knowledge, lack of long context management over multiple files, and overly critical stance on minor issues. Overall, our results position current AI reviewers as complements to, not substitutes for, human reviewers.

摘要：隨著人工智慧能力的進步，AI 評審者開始在科學同行評審中被部署，但它們的能力和可信度仍然受到質疑：許多科學家僅將其視為缺乏評估研究專業知識的概率系統，而其他研究人員則對其準備情況持較樂觀的態度，儘管缺乏具體證據。了解 AI 評審者擅長的地方、短板以及仍面臨的挑戰至關重要。然則，現有的 AI 評審者評估主要集中在其判決是否與人類判決相符（例如，分數一致性、接受預測），這不足以表徵其能力和限制。在本文中，我們通過一項大規模專家標註研究填補了這一空白，在該研究中，45 位物理、生物和健康科學領域的科學家花費 469 小時對 82 篇 Nature 系列論文中人類撰寫和 AI 生成的 2,960 條個別批評（每條針對論文的特定方面）進行評分，評估其正確性、重要性和證據的充分性。在所有三個維度的綜合評分中，由 GPT-5.2 驅動的評審代理的得分高於每篇論文的最高人類評審（60.0% 對 48.2%，p = 0.009），而所有三位 AI 評審者（包括 Gemini 3.0 Pro 和 Claude Opus 4.5）在每個維度上都超過了最低評分的人類。AI 評審者的準確批評也更常被評為重要且證據充分，並提出了 26% 的人類未提及的獨特問題。然而，AI 評審者的重疊程度遠超過人類（交叉評審者對的重疊率為 21% 對 3%），並表現出 16 種人類不具備的重複性弱點，例如有限的子領域知識、缺乏對多個文件的長期上下文管理，以及對小問題的過度批評。總體而言，我們的結果將當前的 AI 評審者定位為人類評審者的補充，而非替代品。

##### **Targeting Clause Type Distributions: a Picklock for Random Satisfiability Problems**
2605.20328v1 by J. Schwardt, J. C. Budich

Optimization problems such as the NP-complete 3-SAT provide an important benchmark for the difficult task of finding ground-states in strongly correlated many-body systems with rugged energy landscapes. The study of random 3-SAT problems as Ising spin Hamiltonians in statistical physics has yielded major insights including the existence of a satisfiability phase transition, and the prediction of a critical parameter line of particularly hard instances. Yet, progress on solving those instances has been scarce for several decades. Here, introducing the Target-SAT (TSAT) algorithm, we roughly triple the tractable problem sizes in the hardest regime, with an even greater improvement in a vast range of neighboring regions. By leveraging statistical information hidden in the combinatorial constraints of the problem, TSAT is actively guided in its stochastic local search toward a target within the relevant parameter space. Our analysis also explains why established local search algorithms are limited to relatively small system sizes due to a vast low-energy trap. Furthermore, we characterize the aforementioned critical line in terms of a dominant additional complexity barrier, whose exponential scaling is quickly overcome by TSAT only in the surrounding parameter space. With TSAT, the lead in solving the hardest known random satisfiability problems returns to the realm of stochastic local search algorithms.

摘要：優化問題如 NP 完全的 3-SAT 為在具有崎嶇能量景觀的強相關多體系統中尋找基態的困難任務提供了一個重要的基準。將隨機 3-SAT 問題作為統計物理中的伊辛自旋哈密頓量進行研究，產生了重大見解，包括可滿足性相變的存在，以及對特別困難實例的臨界參數線的預測。然而，解決這些實例的進展在幾十年來一直很少。在這裡，引入 Target-SAT (TSAT) 算法，我們將最困難範疇中的可處理問題大小大約增加了三倍，並在廣泛的鄰近區域中有更大的改進。通過利用隱藏在問題組合約束中的統計信息，TSAT 在其隨機局部搜索中積極引導朝向相關參數空間內的目標。我們的分析還解釋了為什麼現有的局部搜索算法受到限制，僅能處理相對較小的系統大小，這是因為存在一個龐大的低能量陷阱。此外，我們在一個主導的額外複雜性障礙的基礎上對上述臨界線進行了特徵化，其指數規模在周圍的參數空間中被 TSAT 快速克服。使用 TSAT，解決已知最困難的隨機可滿足性問題的領先地位回到了隨機局部搜索算法的領域。

##### **Rethinking Visual Attribution for Chest X-ray Reasoning in Large Vision Language Models**
2605.20158v1 by Guangzhi Xiong, Qiao Jin, Sanchit Sinha, Zhiyong Lu, Aidong Zhang

Large Vision Language Models (LVLMs) show promise in medical applications, but their inability to faithfully ground responses in visual evidence raises serious concerns about clinical trustworthiness. While visual attribution methods are widely used to explain LVLM predictions, whether these explanations actually reflect the visual evidence underlying the model's decision is largely unverified, since ground-truth annotations for internal model reasoning are typically unavailable. We address this question for chest X-ray (CXR) reasoning by developing a causal evaluation framework that retains only CXR-VQA samples for which the expert-annotated region is verified, via counterfactual editing, to be causally responsible for the model's prediction. Using this framework across 11 attribution methods, six open-source LVLMs, and two output modes (direct answer and step-by-step reasoning), we find that existing attribution methods often fail to identify the evidence used by LVLMs. To address this failure, we propose MedFocus, a concept-based attribution method that localizes clinically meaningful anatomical regions via unbalanced optimal transport and measures their causal effect on model outputs through targeted interventions. MedFocus produces spatial, concept-level, and token-level attributions and substantially outperforms prior methods, taking a step toward more trustworthy attribution for medical LVLMs. Our data and code are available at https://github.com/gzxiong/medfocus/.

摘要：大型視覺語言模型（LVLMs）在醫療應用中顯示出潛力，但它們無法忠實地將回應與視覺證據相結合，這引發了對臨床可信度的嚴重擔憂。雖然視覺歸因方法被廣泛用來解釋LVLM的預測，但這些解釋是否實際反映了模型決策背後的視覺證據在很大程度上尚未得到驗證，因為內部模型推理的真實標註通常無法獲得。我們通過開發一個因果評估框架來解決這一問題，該框架僅保留那些經過專家標註並通過反事實編輯驗證為對模型預測具有因果責任的CXR-VQA樣本。利用這一框架，我們對11種歸因方法、六個開源LVLM和兩種輸出模式（直接回答和逐步推理）進行了研究，發現現有的歸因方法往往無法識別LVLM所使用的證據。為了解決這一失敗，我們提出了MedFocus，一種基於概念的歸因方法，通過不平衡最優運輸定位臨床上有意義的解剖區域，並通過針對性干預測量它們對模型輸出的因果影響。MedFocus生成空間、概念級和標記級的歸因，並顯著超越先前的方法，朝著為醫療LVLM提供更可信的歸因邁出了一步。我們的數據和代碼可在 https://github.com/gzxiong/medfocus/ 獲得。

##### **Less Data, Faster Training: repeating smaller datasets speeds up learning via sampling biases**
2605.20314v1 by Jingwen Liu, Ezra Edelman, Surbhi Goel, Bingbin Liu

This work investigates the ``small-vs-large gap'', where repeating on fewer samples can lead to compute saving during training compared to using a larger dataset. This is observed across algorithmic tasks, architectures and optimizers and cannot be explained using prior theory. We argue that the speedup comes from appropriate layer-wise growth enabled by sampling biases, which is more pronounced when the dataset size is smaller. We provide both theoretical analysis and empirical evidence from various interventions. Our results suggest that using a smaller dataset with more repetitions is not just a fallback strategy under data scarcity, but can be proactively leveraged as a favorable inductive biases for optimization, particularly in reasoning tasks.

摘要：這項工作探討了「小樣本與大樣本之間的差距」，即在訓練過程中，重複較少樣本可以相較於使用較大數據集來節省計算資源。這一現象在各種算法任務、架構和優化器中均有觀察到，且無法用先前的理論來解釋。我們主張，這種加速來自於由取樣偏差所促成的適當層次增長，當數據集大小較小時，這一現象更加明顯。我們提供了理論分析和來自各種干預的實證證據。我們的結果表明，使用較小的數據集並進行更多重複不僅僅是在數據稀缺下的應急策略，而是可以主動利用作為優化的有利歸納偏見，特別是在推理任務中。

##### **CopT: Contrastive On-Policy Thinking with Continuous Spaces for General and Agentic Reasoning**
2605.20075v1 by Dachuan Shi, Hanlin Zhu, Xiangchi Yuan, Wanjia Zhao, Kejing Xia, Wen Xiao, Wenke Lee

Chain-of-thought (CoT) is a standard approach for eliciting reasoning capabilities from large language models (LLMs). However, the common CoT paradigm treats thinking as a prerequisite for answering, which can delay access to plausible answers and incur unnecessary token costs even when the model is able to identify an answer before extended thinking, a behavior known as performative reasoning. In this paper, we introduce CopT, a reformulated reasoning pipeline that reverses the usual order of thinking and answering. Instead of thinking before answering, CopT first elicits a draft answer and then invokes subsequent on-policy thinking conditioned on its own draft answer for reflection and correction. To assess whether the draft answer should be trusted, CopT recasts continuous embeddings as inference-time contrastive verifiers. Specifically, it contrasts the model's support for the same generated tokens under discrete-token inputs and continuous-embedding inputs, yielding a sequence-level reverse KL estimator for answer reliability. Our analysis shows that under certain assumptions, the expected estimate equals the mutual information between the unresolved latent state and the emitted answer token, explaining why it captures answer-relevant uncertainty rather than arbitrary uncertainty in the latent state. When the answer is deemed insufficiently reliable, CopT performs further on-policy thinking, where a second KL estimator dynamically controls draft-answer visibility, preserving useful partial information while reducing the risk of being misled by unreliable content. Across mathematics, coding, and agentic reasoning tasks, CopT improves peak accuracy by up to 23% and reduces token usage by up to 57% at comparable or higher accuracy, without any additional training. The code is available at https://github.com/sdc17/CopT.

摘要：Chain-of-thought (CoT) 是一種標準方法，用於從大型語言模型 (LLMs) 中引出推理能力。<lb/>然而，常見的 CoT 範式將思考視為回答的前提，這可能會延遲獲得合理答案的時間，並在模型能夠在擴展思考之前識別答案時，產生不必要的標記成本，這種行為被稱為表現性推理。<lb/>在本文中，我們介紹了 CopT，一種重新構建的推理管道，顛倒了思考和回答的通常順序。<lb/>CopT 不是在回答之前進行思考，而是首先引出一個草擬答案，然後根據其自己的草擬答案進行後續的政策內思考，以進行反思和修正。<lb/>為了評估草擬答案是否應該被信任，CopT 將連續嵌入重新表述為推理時的對比驗證器。<lb/>具體而言，它對比模型在離散標記輸入和連續嵌入輸入下對相同生成標記的支持，從而產生一個序列級的逆 KL 估計器，用於答案的可靠性。<lb/>我們的分析顯示，在某些假設下，期望估計等於未解決潛在狀態與發出答案標記之間的互信息，解釋了為什麼它捕捉到與答案相關的不確定性，而不是潛在狀態中的任意不確定性。<lb/>當答案被認為不夠可靠時，CopT 會進行進一步的政策內思考，其中第二個 KL 估計器動態控制草擬答案的可見性，保留有用的部分信息，同時減少被不可靠內容誤導的風險。<lb/>在數學、編碼和代理推理任務中，CopT 將峰值準確率提高了多達 23%，並在可比或更高的準確率下將標記使用量減少了多達 57%，而無需任何額外的訓練。<lb/>代碼可在 https://github.com/sdc17/CopT 獲得。

##### **Probing Embodied LLMs: When Higher Observation Fidelity Hurts Problem Solving**
2605.20072v1 by Oussama Zenkri, Oliver Brock

Large Language Models are increasingly proposed as cognitive components for robotic systems, yet their opaque decision processes make it difficult to explain success or failure in closed-loop embodied tasks. Following an empirical AI methodology, we study embodied LLM agents behaviorally by varying the information available to the agent and measuring the resulting changes in behavior. Using the Lockbox, a sequential mechanical puzzle with hidden interdependencies, we evaluate LLMs across RGB, RGB-D, and ground-truth symbolic observations in a physical robotic setup and use controlled simulation to probe the resulting behavior. Counterintuitively, agents perform best under raw RGB input and worst under perfect ground-truth observations. In simulation, we probe this effect by randomly flipping perceived action outcomes and find that moderate noise improves performance, peaking at a 40% flip probability with a 2.85-fold success rate increase over the noise-free baseline. Further analysis links this gain to a reduction in repetitive action loops. These findings suggest that success rates alone are insufficient for evaluating LLMs, as measured performance may reflect the interaction between perceptual errors and reasoning failures rather than robust problem solving.

摘要：大型語言模型越來越多地被提議作為機器人系統的認知組件，然而它們不透明的決策過程使得在封閉回路具身任務中解釋成功或失敗變得困難。根據實證人工智慧方法論，我們通過改變可用於代理的資訊並測量行為的變化來行為上研究具身的LLM代理。使用鎖箱，一種具有隱藏相互依賴性的序列機械謎題，我們在物理機器人設置中評估LLM在RGB、RGB-D和真實符號觀察中的表現，並使用受控模擬來探查結果行為。出乎意料的是，代理在原始RGB輸入下表現最佳，而在完美的真實觀察下表現最差。在模擬中，我們通過隨機翻轉感知的行動結果來探查這一效應，發現適度的噪音能改善性能，在40%的翻轉概率下，成功率較無噪音基線提高了2.85倍。進一步分析將這一增益與重複行動循環的減少聯繫起來。這些發現表明，僅僅依賴成功率來評估LLM是不夠的，因為測得的性能可能反映了感知錯誤與推理失敗之間的互動，而不是穩健的問題解決能力。

##### **A Framework for Evaluating Zero-Shot Image Generation in Concept-based Explainability**
2605.19855v1 by Giacomo Astolfi, Matteo Bianchi, Riccardo Campi, Antonio De Santis, Marco Brambilla

Concept-based Explainable Artificial Intelligence (XAI) interprets deep learning models using human-understandable visual features (e.g., textures or object parts) by linking internal representations to class predictions, thereby bridging the gap between low-level image data and high-level semantics. A major challenge, however, is the reliance on large sets of labeled images to represent each concept, which limits scalability. In this work, we investigate the use of zero-shot Text-to-Image (T2I) generative models as a source of synthetic concept datasets for concept-based XAI methods. Specifically, we generate concepts using predefined prompts and evaluate their faithfulness to real ones through four complementary analyses: (1) comparing synthetic vs. real concept images via concept representation similarity; (2) evaluating their intra-similarity by comparing pairs of subsets of the same concept with progressively increasing size; (3) evaluating their performance for downstream explanation tasks using relevant class images; (4) evaluating how removing a concept from tested class images affects explanations of generated concepts. While current T2I generative models promise a shortcut to concept-based XAI, our study highlights challenges and raises open questions about the use of synthetic data generated by zero-shot pipelines in model analyses. The resulting dataset is available at https://github.com/DataSciencePolimi/ZeroShot-T2I-Concepts.

摘要：概念基礎的可解釋人工智慧（XAI）透過將內部表示與類別預測聯繫起來，使用人類可理解的視覺特徵（例如，紋理或物體部分）來解釋深度學習模型，從而彌合低階影像數據與高階語義之間的差距。然而，一個主要挑戰是依賴大量標記圖像來代表每個概念，這限制了可擴展性。在本研究中，我們調查了使用零樣本文本到影像（T2I）生成模型作為概念基礎的 XAI 方法的合成概念數據集來源。具體而言，我們使用預定義的提示生成概念，並通過四種互補分析評估其對真實概念的忠實度：（1）通過概念表示相似性比較合成與真實概念圖像；（2）通過比較同一概念的子集對，評估其內部相似性，並逐步增加大小；（3）使用相關類別圖像評估其在下游解釋任務中的表現；（4）評估從測試類別圖像中移除概念如何影響生成概念的解釋。雖然當前的 T2I 生成模型為概念基礎的 XAI 提供了一條捷徑，但我們的研究突顯了挑戰並提出了關於在模型分析中使用零樣本管道生成的合成數據的未解決問題。所得到的數據集可在 https://github.com/DataSciencePolimi/ZeroShot-T2I-Concepts 獲得。

##### **Explainable Wastewater Digital Twins: Adaptive Context-Conditioned Structured Simulators with Self-Falsifying Decision Support**
2605.19826v1 by Gary Simethy, Daniel Ortiz Arroyo, Petar Durdevic

Operators of safety-critical industrial processes increasingly rely on digital twins to screen control interventions, but such simulators rarely carry certified safety guarantees. Wastewater treatment plants exemplify the gap: operators face a daily safety-efficiency trade-off where aerating too little risks effluent violations and nitrous-oxide (N2O) spikes, and aerating too much wastes energy. We develop an explainable digital twin for aeration and dosing setpoints. CCSS-IX, the simulator, is a bank of interpretable locally linear state-space "experts" adaptively mixed by a context-aware gating network, building on a continuous-time regime-switching scaffold. A runtime decision layer applies conformal risk control to abstain, reopen, or return a falsifying temporal witness for any operator-proposed action that cannot be statistically certified. The artificial-intelligence contribution is twofold: an identifiable, context-conditioned structured surrogate that retains operator-readable dynamics, and a self-falsifying decision rule with finite-sample coverage guarantees. The engineering contribution is a validated, end-to-end decision-support pipeline, tested on a 1000-step slice of the Avedøre full-scale plant (42.6% sensor missingness, 2-minute sampling), the Agtrup/BlueKolding full-scale plant in Denmark, and the Benchmark Simulation Model No. 2 (BSM2) international benchmark, under a matched ten-seed protocol. The static structured ensemble lies within 0.78% root-mean-square error of an unconstrained black-box reference, and the adaptive variant within 1.08%. The calibrated reopen rule cuts aggregate two-plant regret by 43.6% at an unsafe-action cost weight of 4 and eliminates unsafe chosen actions on the BSM2 main slice. Event-aligned temporal witnesses prevent 93 of 187 false-safe N2O approvals, about 4.65x the dyadic baseline (paired McNemar p < 1e-21).

摘要：操作安全關鍵工業過程的操作者越來越依賴數位雙胞胎來篩選控制干預，但這些模擬器很少具備經過認證的安全保證。廢水處理廠就是這一差距的典範：操作者面臨每日的安全與效率取捨，通氣不足會導致排放違規和一氧化二氮 (N2O) 峰值，而通氣過多則浪費能源。我們開發了一個可解釋的數位雙胞胎，用於通氣和投藥設置點。CCSS-IX，這個模擬器，是一組可解釋的局部線性狀態空間“專家”，由一個上下文感知的閘網絡自適應混合，建立在一個連續時間的狀態轉換框架上。運行時決策層應用符合風險控制，以對任何無法統計認證的操作者提議行動進行放棄、重新開放或返回一個虛假時間見證。人工智慧的貢獻是雙重的：一個可識別的、上下文條件的結構化替代品，保留了操作者可讀的動態，以及一個具有有限樣本覆蓋保證的自我虛假決策規則。工程貢獻是一個經過驗證的端到端決策支持管道，在 Avedøre 全規模工廠（42.6% 傳感器缺失，2 分鐘取樣）、丹麥的 Agtrup/BlueKolding 全規模工廠和基準模擬模型第 2 號 (BSM2) 國際基準下進行測試，遵循匹配的十種種子協議。靜態結構化集成在不受限的黑箱參考的根均方誤差內為 0.78%，而自適應變體則為 1.08%。經過校準的重新開放規則在不安全行動成本權重為 4 的情況下，將兩個工廠的總後悔減少了 43.6%，並消除了 BSM2 主要切片上的不安全選擇行動。事件對齊的時間見證防止了 187 次虛假安全 N2O 批準中的 93 次，約為二元基線的 4.65 倍（配對 McNemar p < 1e-21）。

##### **ST-TGExplainer: Disentangling Stability and Transition Patterns for Temporal GNN Interpretability**
2605.19822v1 by Hongjiang Chen, Xin Zheng, Pengfei Jiao, Huan Liu, Zhidong Zhao, Huaming Wu, Feng Xia, Shirui Pan

Temporal graph neural networks (TGNNs) have gained significant traction for solving real-world temporal graph tasks. However, their interpretability remains limited, as most TGNNs fail to identify which historical interactions most influence a given prediction. Despite promising progress on interpretable TGNNs, existing methods predominantly focus on previously seen historical interactions, which we term stability patterns, while overlooking newly emerging first-time interactions, which we term transition patterns. Both types of patterns are essential for faithful temporal explanations. To address this limitation, we propose ST-TGExplainer, a self-explainable TGNN that disentangles Stability and Transition patterns in temporal graphs for a more faithful Temporal GNN Explainer. Guided by a disentangled information bottleneck objective, ST-TGExplainer learns a compact explanatory subgraph that remains predictive of the event label while explicitly suppressing label-conditioned redundancy between stability and transition patterns. Extensive experiments demonstrate that ST-TGExplainer achieves strong predictive performance and yields more faithful explanations. Code is available at https://github.com/hjchen-hdu/ST-TGExplainer.

摘要：時間圖神經網絡（TGNNs）在解決現實世界的時間圖任務中獲得了顯著的關注。<lb/>然而，它們的可解釋性仍然有限，因為大多數TGNN無法識別哪些歷史互動對給定預測的影響最大。<lb/>儘管在可解釋的TGNN上取得了有希望的進展，但現有方法主要集中在先前見過的歷史互動上，我們稱之為穩定模式，同時忽略了新出現的首次互動，我們稱之為過渡模式。<lb/>這兩種類型的模式對於真實的時間解釋都是必不可少的。<lb/>為了解決這一限制，我們提出了ST-TGExplainer，一種自我解釋的TGNN，能夠在時間圖中解開穩定和過渡模式，以實現更真實的時間GNN解釋器。<lb/>在解開信息瓶頸目標的指導下，ST-TGExplainer學習了一個緊湊的解釋子圖，該子圖在保持對事件標籤的預測能力的同時，明確抑制了穩定和過渡模式之間的標籤條件冗餘。<lb/>大量實驗表明，ST-TGExplainer實現了強大的預測性能並提供了更真實的解釋。<lb/>代碼可在 https://github.com/hjchen-hdu/ST-TGExplainer 獲得。

##### **What Really Improves Mathematical Reasoning: Structured Reasoning Signals Beyond Pure Code**
2605.19762v1 by Yuze Zhao, Junpeng Fang, Lu Yu, Zhenya Huang, Kai Zhang, Qing Cui, Qi Liu, Jun Zhou, Enhong Chen

Code has become a standard component of modern foundation language model (LM) training, yet its role beyond programming remains unclear. We revisit the claim that code improves reasoning through controlled pretraining experiments on a 10T-token corpus with fine-grained domain separation. Our findings are threefold. First, when code is restricted to standalone executable programs and Code-NL data are controlled for, code substantially improves programming ability but does not act as a general reasoning enhancer; instead, it competes with knowledge-intensive tasks, especially complex mathematical reasoning. Second, the reasoning gains often attributed to code are better explained by cross-domain structured reasoning traces, such as code-text and math-text mixtures, rather than by executable code alone. Third, increasing the density of structured math-domain samples within a fixed math budget yields substantial gains on difficult mathematical reasoning while largely preserving programming performance, suggesting that cognitive scaffolds offer a targeted way to mitigate cross-domain trade-offs. Finally, routing analyses show that data-composition effects are reflected in expert-activation patterns, providing mechanism-level evidence for competitive and synergistic interactions across domains. Our results clarify which data characteristics transfer across capability dimensions and point to more precise data-centric optimization strategies.

摘要：代碼已成為現代基礎語言模型（LM）訓練的標準組成部分，但其在編程之外的角色仍不明確。<lb/>我們重新檢視了代碼通過控制預訓練實驗在10T-token語料庫上改善推理的說法，並進行了細緻的領域分離。<lb/>我們的發現有三個方面。<lb/>首先，當代碼僅限於獨立可執行程序且控制了Code-NL數據時，代碼顯著提高了編程能力，但並不作為一般推理的增強器；相反，它與知識密集型任務競爭，特別是複雜的數學推理。<lb/>其次，通常歸因於代碼的推理增益更好地解釋為跨領域結構化推理痕跡，例如代碼-文本和數學-文本混合，而非僅由可執行代碼解釋。<lb/>第三，在固定的數學預算內增加結構化數學領域樣本的密度，能在難度較大的數學推理上帶來顯著增益，同時大幅保留編程表現，這表明認知支架提供了一種針對性的方法來減輕跨領域的權衡。<lb/>最後，路由分析顯示數據組合效應反映在專家激活模式中，為跨領域的競爭和協同互動提供了機制層面的證據。<lb/>我們的結果澄清了哪些數據特徵在能力維度之間轉移，並指向更精確的以數據為中心的優化策略。

##### **Are Rationales Necessary and Sufficient? Tuning LLMs for Explainable Misinformation Detection**
2605.19285v1 by Bing Wang, Rui Miao, Ximing Li, Chen Shen, Shaotian Yan, Changchun Li, Kaiyuan Liu, Xiaosong Yuan, Jieping Ye

The rapid spread of misinformation on social media platforms has become a formidable challenge. To mitigate its proliferation, Misinformation Detection (MD) has emerged as a critical research topic. Traditional MD approaches based on small models typically perform binary classification through a black-box process. Recently, the rise of Large Language Models (LLMs) has enabled explainable MD, where models generate rationales that explain their decisions, thereby enhancing transparency. Existing explainable MD methods primarily focus on crafting sophisticated prompts to elicit rationales from off-the-shelf LLMs. In this work, we propose a pipeline to fine-tune a dedicated LLM specifically for explainable MD. Our pipeline begins by collecting large-scale fact-checked articles, and then uses multiple strong LLMs to produce veracity predictions and rationales. To ensure high-quality training data, we leverage a filtering strategy that selects only the correct instances for fine-tuning. While this pipeline is intuitive and prevalent, our experiments reveal that naive filtering based solely on label correctness is insufficient in practice and suffers from two critical limitations: (1) Coarse-grained labels cause insufficient rationales: Rationales filtered solely based on binary labels are insufficient to adequately support their decisions; (2) Over-verification behavior causes unnecessary rationales: Stronger LLMs tend to exhibit over-verification behavior, producing excessively verbose and unnecessary rationales. To address these issues, we introduce LONSREX, a novel data synthesis pipeline to Locate Necessary and Sufficient Rationales for Explainable MD. Specifically, we propose a metric that quantifies the contribution of each verification step to the final prediction, thereby evaluating its necessity and sufficiency. Experimental results demonstrate the effectiveness of LONSREX.

摘要：社交媒體平台上虛假信息的迅速傳播已成為一個艱鉅的挑戰。為了減輕其擴散，虛假信息檢測（MD）已成為一個關鍵的研究主題。基於小型模型的傳統MD方法通常通過黑箱過程執行二元分類。最近，大型語言模型（LLMs）的興起使得可解釋的MD成為可能，這些模型生成解釋其決策的理由，從而增強了透明度。現有的可解釋MD方法主要集中在設計複雜的提示，以從現成的LLMs中引出理由。在這項工作中，我們提出了一個管道，以專門針對可解釋MD微調一個專用的LLM。我們的管道首先收集大規模的事實檢查文章，然後使用多個強大的LLM來生成真實性預測和理由。為了確保高質量的訓練數據，我們利用一種過濾策略，只選擇正確的實例進行微調。雖然這個管道直觀且普遍，但我們的實驗顯示，僅基於標籤正確性的天真過濾在實踐中是不足的，並且存在兩個關鍵限制：（1）粗粒度標籤導致理由不足：僅基於二元標籤過濾的理由不足以充分支持其決策；（2）過度驗證行為導致不必要的理由：較強的LLM往往會表現出過度驗證行為，生成過於冗長且不必要的理由。為了解決這些問題，我們引入了LONSREX，一個新穎的數據合成管道，用於定位可解釋MD所需的必要和充分理由。具體而言，我們提出了一種量化每個驗證步驟對最終預測貢獻的指標，從而評估其必要性和充分性。實驗結果證明了LONSREX的有效性。

##### **ExECG: An Explainable AI Framework for ECG models**
2605.19258v1 by Jong-Hwan Jang, Yong-yeon Jo

Deep learning has enabled ECG diagnostic models with strong performance in tasks such as arrhythmia classification and abnormality detection. However, accuracy alone is insufficient for clinical deployment because it does not explain why a specific output was produced, limiting justification, error analysis, and trust. Although ECG XAI has been extensively investigated and steadily improved, practical pipelines and reporting conventions vary across studies, hindering reuse and reproducibility. To address these issues, we present Explainable AI framework for ECG models (ExECG), a Python framework that provides a three-stage pipeline: Wrapper standardizes access across heterogeneous ECG formats and intermediate representations, Explainer unifies diverse XAI methods under a shared execution protocol, and Visualizer supports consistent cross-method comparison within a unified interface. ##### **On-Device Continual Learning with Dual-Stage Buffer and Dynamic Loss for Point-of-Care Pneumonia Diagnosis**
2605.19201v1 by Danu Kim

Deep learning models detect pneumonia from chest X-rays with high accuracy, but the performance declines under domain shifts caused by differences in devices, patients, or institutions. We present PneumoNet, a domain-incremental learning method for point-of-care pneumonia diagnosis in resource-limited settings. PneumoNet combines a lightweight CNN for on-device prediction, a dual-stage balanced buffer for class-balanced replay, and a dynamic class-weighted loss to correct training-batch imbalances. Evaluated on a domain-shifted PneumoniaMNIST dataset simulating five realistic domain change scenarios, PneumoNet achieves 86.6% accuracy with 1.4% forgetting while being smaller and faster than existing baselines. ##### **What Does the AI Doctor Value? Auditing Pluralism in the Clinical Ethics of Language Models**
2605.18738v1 by Payal Chandak, Victoria Alkin, David Wu, Maya Dagan, Taposh Dutta Roy, Maria Clara Saad Menezes, Ayush Noori, Nirali Somia, John S. Brownstein, Ran Balicer, Rebecca W. Brendel, Noa Dagan, Isaac S. Kohane, Gabriel A. Brat

Medicine is inherently pluralistic. Principles such as autonomy, beneficence, nonmaleficence, and justice routinely conflict, and such ethical dilemmas often sharply divide reasonable physicians. Good clinical practice navigates these tensions in concert with each patient's values rather than imposing a single ethical stance. The ethical values that large language models bring to medical advice, however, have not been systematically examined. We present a framework for auditing value pluralism in medical AI, comprising a benchmark of clinician-verified dilemmas and an attribution method that recovers value priorities directly from decisions. The ecosystem of frontier models spans physician-level value heterogeneity, and models discuss competing values in their reasoning (Overton pluralism) before committing to a decision. However, individual model decisions are near-deterministic across repeated sampling and semantic variations, failing to reproduce the distributional pluralism of the physician panel. Across benchmark cases, these consistent decisions reflect committed, systematic value preferences. While most model priorities fall within the natural range of inter-physician variation, some significantly underweight patient autonomy. A single LLM deployed without regard for its value priorities could amplify those priorities at scale to every patient it serves. Without explicit efforts to balance ethical perspectives with one or multiple models, these tools risk replacing clinical pluralism with a deployment monoculture.

摘要：醫學本質上是多元的。自主、行善、不傷害和正義等原則經常發生衝突，這些倫理困境常常使合理的醫生產生尖銳的分歧。良好的臨床實踐在與每位患者的價值觀協調的過程中，導航這些緊張局勢，而不是強加單一的倫理立場。然而，大型語言模型在醫療建議中所帶來的倫理價值尚未得到系統性的檢視。我們提出了一個審計醫療人工智慧中價值多元主義的框架，這包括一個臨床醫生驗證的困境基準和一種從決策中直接恢復價值優先順序的歸因方法。前沿模型的生態系統涵蓋了醫生層級的價值異質性，模型在其推理中討論競爭的價值（Overton 多元主義），然後才做出決策。然而，個別模型的決策在重複抽樣和語義變化中近乎確定性，未能再現醫生小組的分佈多元主義。在基準案例中，這些一致的決策反映了堅定的系統性價值偏好。雖然大多數模型的優先順序落在醫生之間變異的自然範圍內，但有些模型顯著低估了患者的自主權。未考慮其價值優先順序而單一部署的 LLM 可能會將這些優先順序以規模擴大到每位患者身上。如果不明確努力將倫理觀點與一個或多個模型平衡，這些工具可能會將臨床多元主義取代為部署的單一文化。

##### **Evaluating the Utility of Personal Health Records in Personalized Health AI**
2605.18937v1 by Rory Sayres, Kejia Chen, Ayush Jain, Matthew Thompson, Jonathan Richina, Xiang Yin, Jimmy Hu, Fan Zhang, Bob Lou, Mike Sanchez, Ines Mezerreg, Meredith Schreier, Hamsa Subramaniam, I-Ching Lee, Yugang Jia, Daniel Mcduff, Yossi Matias, Avinatan Hassidim, Dale Webster, Yun Liu, Jackie Barr, Quang Duong

Patient-managed Personal Health Records (PHRs) promises to empower patients to better understand their health; but information in the record is complex, potentially hindering insights. In this study, we assess the potential of large language models (LLMs, Gemini 3.0 Flash) to provide helpful answers to user health queries, when provided clinical data from PHRs as context. A total of 2,257 user queries were drawn from 3 different distributions to represent patient questions: shorter web search queries, longer questions derived from templates of chatbot conversations, and questions patients asked to their healthcare team (patient calls). Queries were matched with de-identified PHRs (from a pool of 1,945). Gemini responses were generated (1) without PHR context; (2) with a basic summary of demographics, conditions, and medications; (3) with full, extensive clinical notes. For evaluation, we leveraged an existing rating framework (SHARP), and developed a new framework for specific error modes when interpreting PHRs. Evaluation was performed using autoraters for the full set, and with clinician ratings for a subset (n=95), with both sets of raters knowing the full PHR context. We see significant improvements in the helpfulness of answers to all question types with PHR data (p < 0.001, paired t-test). We also observe potential gains in safety, accuracy, relevance and personalization of answers. Our PHR evaluation framework further identifies gaps in LLM understanding of particular aspects of complex PHRs, such as temporal disorientation, and rare but meaningful confabulations. These results suggest potential for PHR data to help people with a wide range of user needs; and provide a framework for monitoring for gaps in LLM answers based on PHR context. This study motivates further work to assess and realize potential benefits to users from understanding their health records.

摘要：病人管理的個人健康記錄（PHRs）有望使患者更好地理解他們的健康；但記錄中的信息是複雜的，可能會妨礙洞察力。在這項研究中，我們評估大型語言模型（LLMs，Gemini 3.0 Flash）在提供有用的健康查詢答案方面的潛力，當提供來自PHRs的臨床數據作為上下文時。總共從3種不同的分佈中提取了2,257個用戶查詢，以代表患者問題：較短的網絡搜索查詢、從聊天機器人對話模板衍生的較長問題，以及患者向其醫療團隊提出的問題（患者來電）。查詢與去識別的PHRs（來自1,945個樣本）相匹配。Gemini的回應生成方式為（1）無PHR上下文；（2）提供基本的人口統計、病情和藥物的摘要；（3）提供完整的、詳細的臨床筆記。為了評估，我們利用了一個現有的評分框架（SHARP），並針對解釋PHRs時的特定錯誤模式開發了一個新的框架。評估是使用自動評分工具對完整數據集進行的，並對一個子集（n=95）進行臨床醫生評分，兩組評分者均了解完整的PHR上下文。我們看到使用PHR數據後，對所有問題類型的答案的有用性有顯著改善（p < 0.001，配對t檢驗）。我們還觀察到在安全性、準確性、相關性和個性化方面的潛在增益。我們的PHR評估框架進一步識別了LLM在理解複雜PHRs的特定方面的差距，例如時間錯位和稀有但有意義的虛構。這些結果表明PHR數據有潛力幫助滿足各種用戶需求的人；並提供了一個基於PHR上下文監控LLM答案差距的框架。這項研究激勵進一步工作，以評估和實現用戶從理解其健康記錄中獲得潛在好處的可能性。

##### **Predictable Confabulations: Factual Recall by LLMs Scales with Model Size and Topic Frequency**
2605.18732v1 by Matthew L. Smith, Jonathan P. Shock, Samuel T. Segun, Iyiola E. Olatunji, Tegawendé F. Bissyandé

While scaling laws govern aggregate large language model performance, no scaling law has linked factual recall to both model size and training-data composition. We evaluated 38 models on over 8,900 scholarly references evaluated by an automated reference verification system. Recall quality follows a sigmoid in the log-linear combination of model parameter count and topic representation in training data. These two variables alone explain 60% of the variance across 16 dense models from four families, rising to 74-94% within individual families. The form matches a superposition-inspired account in which recall is gated by a signal-to-noise ratio: signal strength scales with concept frequency and the noise floor with model capacity.

摘要：雖然縮放法則支配著大型語言模型的整體性能，但尚未有縮放法則將事實回憶與模型大小和訓練數據組成聯繫起來。<lb/>我們評估了38個模型，基於超過8,900個學術參考文獻，這些文獻由自動參考驗證系統進行評估。<lb/>回憶質量在模型參數數量和訓練數據中的主題表示的對數-線性組合中遵循S型曲線。<lb/>這兩個變量單獨解釋了來自四個家族的16個密集模型中60%的變異性，在個別家族中上升至74-94%。<lb/>這種形式與一種受疊加啟發的解釋相符，其中回憶受到信噪比的限制：信號強度隨著概念頻率的增加而增強，而噪聲底線則隨著模型容量的增加而變化。

##### **Learning Quantifiable Visual Explanations Without Ground-Truth**
2605.18681v1 by Amritpal Singh, Andrey Barsky, Mohamed Ali Souibgui, Ernest Valveny, Dimosthenis Karatzas

Explainable AI (XAI) techniques are increasingly important for the validation and responsible use of modern deep learning models, but are difficult to evaluate due to the lack of good ground-truth to compare against. We propose a framework that serves as a quantifiable metric for the quality of XAI methods, based on continuous input perturbation. Our metric formally considers the sufficiency and necessity of the attributed information to the model's decision-making, and we illustrate a range of cases where it aligns better with human intuitions of explanation quality than do existing metrics.
  To exploit the properties of this metric, we also propose a novel XAI method, considering the case where we fine-tune a model using a differentiable approximation of the metric as a supervision signal. The result is an adapter module that can be trained on top of any black-box model to output causal explanations of the model's decision process, without degrading model performance. We show that the explanations generated by this method outperform those of competing XAI techniques according to a number of quantifiable metrics.
